### [1] [Not All Prefills Are Equal: PPD Disaggregation for Multi-turn LLM Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13358)
*Zongze Li,Jingyu Liu,Zach Xu,Yineng Zhang,Tahseen Rabbani,Ce Zhang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对多轮对话场景下的PD分离架构，提出了PPD动态路由系统。该系统识别出追加预填充对解码性能干扰较小，通过动态决策是否在解码节点本地处理第2轮及以后的请求，减少了68%的TTFT，有效缓解了KV传输拥塞问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代LLM推理引擎采用的Prefill-Decode(PD)分离架构在多轮对话场景中存在两个基本低效问题：(1)每轮对话都需要重新预填充新提示和上一轮的响应；(2)预填充和解码节点之间重复的KV传输会饱和带宽，导致高延迟甚至服务降级。作者发现并非所有预填充操作都具有同等的破坏性，追加预填充（仅处理新输入tokens并复用缓存的KV状态）比完整预填充对解码造成的减速要小得多。

Method: 提出了Prefill-Prefill-capable Decode(PPD)分离架构，这是一个动态路由系统。该系统基于追加预填充对解码性能干扰较小的洞察，动态决策是否利用缓存的KV状态在解码节点本地处理第2轮及以后的请求。PPD通过可配置的权重适应不同的服务等级目标(SLO)，并能与传统的PD部署无缝集成。分析表明，没有单一固定的路由策略能同时满足所有SLO要求，因此需要动态路由。

Result: 通过广泛的评估，PPD将第2轮及以后请求的首令牌时间(TTFT)减少了68%，同时保持了具有竞争力的每输出令牌时间(TPOT)，有效缓解了高负载下的KV传输拥塞问题。

Conclusion: PPD代表了一种灵活高效的多轮LLM服务范式，通过动态路由策略在解码节点本地处理追加预填充操作，显著降低了延迟并改善了系统吞吐量，为多轮交互场景下的LLM服务提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Prefill-Decode (PD) disaggregation has become the standard architecture for modern LLM inference engines, which alleviates the interference of two distinctive workloads. With the growing demand for multi-turn interactions in chatbots and agentic systems, we re-examined PD in this case and found two fundamental inefficiencies: (1) every turn requires prefilling the new prompt and response from the last turn, and (2) repeated KV transfers between prefill and decode nodes saturate the bandwidth, leading to high latency and even service degradation. Our key insight is that not all prefill operations are equally disruptive: append-prefill -- processing only the new input tokens while reusing cached KV states -- incurs substantially less decoding slowdown than full prefill. This motivates routing append-prefill to decode nodes locally. However, through comprehensive analysis, we show that no single fixed routing strategy satisfies all Service Level Objectives (SLOs) simultaneously. Based on this insight, we propose Prefill Prefill-capable Decode (PPD) disaggregation, a dynamic routing system that decides when to process Turn 2+ requests locally on decode nodes using cached KV states. PPD adapts to varying SLOs via configurable weights and seamlessly integrates with traditional PD deployments. With extensive evaluations, we show that PPD reduces Turn 2+ time-to-first-token (TTFT) by 68% while maintaining competitive time-per-output-token (TPOT), effectively alleviating KV transfer congestion under high load. We believe PPD represents a flexible and efficient paradigm for multi-turn LLM serving.

</details>


### [2] [AI-Enabled Bit-Mapping Medium Access Control Protocol for Intelligent and Energy-Efficient IoT Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13577)
*Jesmine Damilola Omonori,Iyanu Tomiwa Durotola,Godspower Paul Osilama*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了EEI-BMA协议，一种基于AI辅助和事件概率感知的MAC协议，通过轻量级神经网络预测动态调整传输调度，在混合流量模式下相比传统TDMA、能量感知TDMA和传统BMA分别实现了35-45%、22-30%和18-28%的节能效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统TDMA和BMA类MAC协议无法自适应传感器活动的时空变化，导致不必要的无线唤醒和能耗增加，特别是在事件驱动与连续监测混合流量场景下。

Method: 提出EEI-BMA协议，集成轻量级神经网络事件预测、单节点概率估计、自适应时隙激活和选择性信道访问机制，动态调整传输调度以减少收发器活动。

Result: MATLAB仿真表明，EEI-BMA（最佳预测）在不同节点密度、包大小、事件生成概率和连续监测负载下，能耗比传统TDMA降低35-45%，比能量感知TDMA降低22-30%，比传统BMA降低18-28%；即使预测不完美，仍保持稳健的优越性能。

Conclusion: 预测引导的MAC调度是下一代低功耗WSN和IoT系统的高效策略，EEI-BMA在混合流量环境下展现出显著的节能效果和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Energy-efficient medium access control (MAC) protocols remain critical in resource-constrained Wireless Sensor Networks (WSNs) and IoT deployments, especially under mixed traffic patterns that combine event-driven and continuous monitoring operations. Traditional Time Division Multiple Access (TDMA)- and Bit Map Assisted (BMA)-based MAC protocols fail to adapt their duty cycles to spatiotemporal variations in sensor activity, resulting in unnecessary radio wake-ups and increased energy expenditure. To address this limitation, this paper proposes EEI-BMA, an AI-assisted, event-probability-aware MAC protocol that dynamically adjusts transmission scheduling using lightweight neural-network-based event prediction. The proposed framework incorporates per-node probability estimation, adaptive slot activation, and selective channel access to reduce transceiver activity while preserving sensing reliability. Simulation results obtained in the MATLAB environment show that EEI-BMA (Best Prediction) achieves 35--45% lower energy consumption than Traditional-TDMA, 22--30% savings compared with Energy-Aware TDMA, and 18--28% improvement over Traditional-BMA across varying node densities, packet sizes, event-generation probabilities, and continuous monitoring loads. Even with imperfect prediction, EEI-BMA consistently outperforms all baseline protocols, demonstrating strong robustness. The results confirm that prediction-guided MAC scheduling is a highly effective strategy for next-generation low-power WSNs and IoT systems.

</details>


### [3] [SAIL: Unsupervised Spatial-Angular Interpretable Feature Learning for RF Map Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13630)
*Sopan Sarkar,Marwan Krunz*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出了SAIL框架，一种基于GAN的无监督学习方法，可从无标签RF地图中学习可解释的潜在变量，实现快速、可控的RF地图合成，平均SSIM达0.8576，PSNR达23.33 dB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RF地图获取方法（现场勘测、射线追踪仿真）在高频和密集网络部署场景下劳动密集或计算成本高昂。监督式生成AI方法因缺乏可靠的标注数据而不可行，而纯无监督方法缺乏对合成过程的显式控制。

Method: 提出SAIL框架，基于InfoGAN原理构建 Wasserstein GAN模型，引入梯度惩罚提升训练稳定性和合成质量。框架从无标签RF地图中学习结构化表示：(i)分类潜在变量捕获与发射机位置相关的离散楼层平面区域；(ii)连续潜在变量捕获与发射机波束视轴角对应的角向变化，无需位置或方向监督。

Result: 在射线追踪RF地图上的实验表明，SAIL成功学习了具有物理意义的空间-角向因子，实现了快速可控的RF地图合成。与射线追踪仿真相比，平均SSIM达到0.8576，平均PSNR达到23.33 dB。

Conclusion: SAIL框架成功解决了RF地图合成中的数据标注和控制难题，通过无监督学习获得物理可解释的潜在变量，为无线网络容量规划、覆盖估计和定位等任务提供了高效的RF地图生成方案。

Abstract: In wireless networks, radio-frequency (RF) maps are critical for tasks such as capacity planning, coverage estimation, and localization. Traditional approaches for obtaining RF maps, including site surveys and ray-tracing simulations, are labor-intensive or computationally expensive, especially at high frequencies and dense network deployments. Generative AI offers a promising alternative for RF map synthesis. However, supervised methods are often infeasible due to the lack of reliable labeled training data, while purely unsupervised methods typically lack explicit control over the synthesis process. To address these challenges, we propose SAIL (Spatial-Angular Interpretable Feature Learning), a generative adversarial network (GAN)-based framework that learns interpretable and controllable latent variables directly from unlabeled RF maps and enables targeted RF map synthesis at inference time through latent-variable manipulation. SAIL builds on the information-maximizing GAN (InfoGAN) principle to learn a structured representation comprising: (i) a categorical latent variable that captures discrete floor-plan regions associated with Tx location and (ii) a continuous latent variable that captures angular variations corresponding to the Tx boresight angle, without requiring any location or orientation supervision during training. We further adopt a Wasserstein GAN objective with a gradient penalty to improve training stability and synthesis quality. Our results using ray-tracing-based RF maps indicate that SAIL learns physically meaningful spatial-angular factors and enables fast controlled RF map synthesis, achieving an average SSIM of 0.8576 and an average PSNR of 23.33 dB relative to ray-tracing simulations.

</details>


### [4] [Linnaeus: A Hierarchical, Multi-Label Framework for Autonomous System Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13649)
*Marcos Piotto,Ignacio Schuemer,Santiago T. Torres,Mariano G. Beiró,Esteban Carisimo,Fabián E. Bustamante*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出Linnaeus，一个结合网络特征与非网络特征的分层AS分类框架，利用领域适配的大语言模型和传统机器学习技术，实现了18个一级和38个二级类别的多标签AS分类，整体准确率达到0.83，召回率为0.76。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于网络级特征的AS分类方法无法捕捉自治系统在语义和运营上的异质性，例如社区骨干网、超大规模内容提供商和海底电缆运营商等多样化的角色无法被有效区分。

Method: 提出了一个分层AS分类框架Linnaeus，该方法结合了网络中心数据（如拓扑结构、BGP公告）与丰富的非网络特征，并利用领域适配的大语言模型和传统机器学习技术进行分类。框架支持多标签分配以反映混合角色，提供从数据摄取到标签推理的端到端流程。

Result: 在近2000个手动标注的AS数据集上，Linnaeus实现了0.83的整体精确率和0.76的召回率，并通过案例研究展示了其在揭示互联网基础设施结构和语义维度方面的实际价值。

Conclusion: Linnaeus框架能够有效捕捉自治系统的语义和运营异质性，提供了一个两级分类体系（18个一级类和38个二级类），为理解互联网基础设施的结构和语义维度提供了新的视角和实用工具。

Abstract: Autonomous systems (ASes) play diverse roles in today's Internet, from community and research backbones to hyperscale content providers and submarine-cable operators. However, existing taxonomies based solely on network-level features fail to capture their semantic and operational heterogeneity.
  In this paper, we present Linnaeus, a hierarchical AS-classification framework that combines network-centric data (e.g., topology, BGP announcements) with rich non-network features and leverages domain-adapted large language models alongside traditional machine-learning techniques. Linnaeus provides a two-level taxonomy with 18 top-level and 38 second-level classes, supports multi-label assignments to reflect hybrid roles (e.g., research backbone and transit provider), and provides an end-to-end pipeline from data ingestion to label inference. On a manually annotated dataset of nearly 2,000 ASes, Linnaeus achieves an overall precision and recall of 0.83 and 0.76, respectively. We further demonstrate its practical value through case studies, highlighting Linnaeus's potential to reveal both structural and semantic dimensions of Internet infrastructure.

</details>


### [5] [LLM-Based Net Analyzer rApp for Explainable and Safe Automation in O-RAN Non-RT RIC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13775)
*Tuan V. Ngo,Mao V. Ngo,Binbin Chen,Tony Q. S. Quek,Tejaswita Kumari,Maziar Nekovee*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的Net Analyzer rApp，部署于O-RAN非实时RIC中，通过事件驱动、批量触发、人在回路的推理框架，将RAN遥测数据转化为可解释的分析结果和受控的配置修改建议，实现了安全、可审计的RAN运维自动化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代5G/6G O-RAN网络虽然可编程性增强，但 disaggregation、开放接口和细粒度控制参数带来了运营复杂性。现有KPI监控和移动性事件报告等RAN侧分析机制存在局限，运营商难以关联异构事件并安全地将观测转化为可执行的配置变更。

Method: 提出基于LLM的Net Analyzer rApp，采用事件通知、批量触发的推理框架：(1)解读移动性事件；(2)通过针对性日志检查确认异常；(3)通过工具门控访问检查配置；(4)仅在操作员明确批准后提出最小化配置变更。架构严格分离推理与执行，确保可审计性和操作安全。

Result: 在真实O-RAN测试平台上实现并演示了该系统，采用可复现的乒乓切换场景进行验证。展示了LLM如何作为推理副驾驶，将原始RAN遥测数据转化为结构化解释和受控的修复工作流程，补充了Non-RT RIC中现有的纯分析方法。

Conclusion: LLM可以作为有效的推理辅助工具，在人在回路的前提下实现RAN运维的可解释、安全自动化，将原始遥测转化为结构化输出和受控行动，是对现有分析方法的补充而非替代。推理与执行的严格分离是实现操作安全的关键。

Abstract: Modern 5G/6G radio access networks are increasingly programmable through O-RAN, yet their operational complexity has grown with disaggregation, open interfaces, and fine-grained control parameters. While RAN-side analytics and telemetry mechanisms, such as KPI-based monitoring and mobility event reporting, provide visibility into network behavior, operators still face challenges in correlating heterogeneous events and safely translating observations into actionable configuration changes. This paper presents an LLM-based Net Analyzer rApp for the O-RAN Non-RT RIC that enables explainable and safe, human-in-the-loop automation for RAN operations. The proposed rApp adopts an event-informed, batch-triggered reasoning framework in which mobility events are first interpreted, anomalies are confirmed through targeted log inspection, configurations are inspected via tool-gated access, and minimal configuration changes are proposed only after explicit operator approval. The architecture enforces a strict separation between reasoning and actuation, ensuring auditability and operational safety. The system is implemented and demonstrated on a real O-RAN testbed using a reproducible ping-pong handover scenario, illustrating how large language models can function as reasoning co-pilots that transform raw RAN telemetry into structured explanations and controlled remediation workflows, complementing existing analytics-only approaches in the NonRT RIC.

</details>


### [6] [A Case for CATS: A Conductor-driven Asymmetric Transport Scheme for Semantic Prioritization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13945)
*Syed Muhammad Aqdas Rizvi*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出CATS框架，通过在TCP中引入传输原生的"Conductor"调度器，赋予协议语义感知能力以优先传输关键内容，在极端场景下将首次内容渲染(FCP)时间降低超过78%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统TCP协议采用盲目FIFO的数据传输模型，无法区分数据优先级，对于延迟敏感和交互式应用性能欠佳。现有的历史优化方案存在诸多局限：HTTP/1.1并行连接开销高、HTTP/2存在传输层队首阻塞、HTTP/3 over QUIC的优先级实现存在异构性问题。

Method: 提出CATS（Conductor驱动的非对称传输方案）框架，在TCP协议中引入集中式调度智能组件"Conductor"，赋予传输层语义感知能力。该架构基于TCP BBR实现，能够识别并优先调度关键内容，而非盲目按FIFO顺序传输所有数据。作者在ns-3仿真环境中完成了系统实现。

Result: 在故意设计的极端网页下载场景中，CATS将首次内容渲染(First Contentful Paint)时间降低超过78%，同时总页面加载时间相比基线无性能损失。

Conclusion: 通过将调度智能集中化并赋予传输层语义感知能力，CATS框架证明可以有效改善用户感知性能，为解决传输层优先级调度问题提供了新思路，且不会牺牲整体传输效率。

Abstract: Standard transport protocols like TCP operate as a blind, FIFO conveyor belt for data, a model that is increasingly suboptimal for latency-sensitive and interactive applications. This paper challenges this model by introducing CATS (Conductor-driven Asymmetric Transport Scheme), a framework that provides TCP with the semantic awareness necessary to prioritize critical content. By centralizing scheduling intelligence in a transport-native "Conductor", CATS significantly improves user-perceived performance by delivering essential data first. This architecture directly confronts a cascade of historical performance workarounds and their limitations, including the high overhead of parallel connections in HTTP/1.1, the transport-layer Head-of-Line blocking in HTTP/2, and the observed implementation heterogeneity of prioritization in HTTP/3 over QUIC. Built upon TCP BBR, our ns-3 implementation demonstrates this principle by reducing the First Contentful Paint by over 78% in a representative webpage download configured as a deliberate worst-case scenario, with no penalty to total page load time compared to the baseline.

</details>


### [7] [Measuring Weather Effects and Link Quality Dynamics in LEO Satellite Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14008)
*Clemens Lottermoser,Simon Damm,Stefan Schmid*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本研究通过对Starlink进行56天的实证分析，发现大气液态水（LWP）是影响LEO卫星通信链路质量的关键天气因素，会导致下载速率降低最高60 MBit/s，而云层本身影响不大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着低地球轨道（LEO）卫星通信（如Starlink）的快速发展，理解动态因素对链路质量的影响至关重要，但现有研究缺乏对气象因素的系统性实证分析。

Method: 在56天内收集112组高质量气象测量数据（主要为1分钟间隔）和网络性能数据，使用云高仪、微波辐射计等专业设备及视觉-语言模型分析天空图像来估算云特征，结合网络性能数据进行相关性分析。

Result: 云层的存在本身对吞吐量或延迟没有显著影响；大气液态水含量（LWP）是关键因素，与下载吞吐量的显著降低（高达60 MBit/s）相关，尤其在降雨期间；上传性能和延迟基本不受影响；新型卫星硬件和基础设施升级也对性能提升有贡献。

Conclusion: 大气液态水是影响LEO卫星通信链路质量的主要天气相关因素，网络基础设施的演进同样重要，这些发现对优化卫星通信系统设计和运维具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: This paper presents an empirical study of dynamic factors affecting link quality in Low Earth Orbit (LEO) satellite communications, using Starlink as a case study. Over 56 days, 112 high-quality meteorological measurements in mostly 1-min intervals, co-located with a user terminal, were collected, alongside frequent network performance data. Cloud characteristics were estimated using professional weather instruments such as a ceilometer, microwave radiometer, and vision-language model on sky images. Our results show that general cloud presence does not significantly impact throughput or latency. The impact of cloud coverage rather depends on the presence of liquid water in the atmosphere, quantified by liquid water path (LWP), which correlates with notable download throughput reductions (up to 60 MBit/s), especially during rain. Upload and latency were largely unaffected. Analysis of the evolving satellite network revealed that newer satellite hardware and infrastructural upgrades also contributed to performance increases during the experiment period. These findings highlight atmospheric liquid water as the key weather-related factor affecting link quality and underscore the influence of network changes over time.

</details>


### [8] [An Analytic Hierarchy Process (AHP) Based QoS-aware Mode Selection Algorithm for D2D Enabled Heterogeneous Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14551)
*Souvik Deb,Shankar K. Ghosh,Avirup Das,Sridevi S,Jacob Augustine,Rajib Mall*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于双层AHP的D2D使能NSA网络模式选择算法，通过结合服务需求和RSRP变化来优化模式选择并减少切换开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在D2D使能的非独立组网5G网络中，用户设备可以通过四种模式获得服务（仅LTE、仅NR、通过D2D的LTE、通过D2D的NR）。现有模式选择方法主要忽略了用户设备的服务需求（如高数据速率、低延迟、超高可靠性等）以及切换带来的开销问题。

Method: 提出了一种基于双层层次分析法（AHP）的模式选择算法：第一层考虑用户设备的服务需求，第二层考虑四种模式选择选项；然后将双层AHP计算的静态排名与不同模式下的参考信号接收功率（RSRP）变化相结合，从而捕捉用户移动性的影响并减少不必要的切换。

Result: 仿真结果表明，所提出的算法在三个网络切片（eMBB、uRLLc和mMTc）的所有主要关键性能指标（KPI）上均优于现有最佳相关研究方案。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了将服务需求与移动性影响相结合的模式选择方法能够有效提升D2D使能NSA网络的性能，为未来网络切片场景下的资源管理提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Device-to-device (D2D) communication was proposed to enhance the coverage of cellular base stations. In a D2D enabled non-standalone fifth generation cellular network (NSA), service demand of a user equipment (UE) may be served in four \emph{modes}: through LTE only, through NR only, through LTE via D2D and through NR via D2D. Such mode selection should consider the service requirements of the UEs (e.g., high data rate, low latency, ultra-reliability, etc.) and the overhead incurred by handovers. In existing mode selection approaches for D2D enabled NSA, the service requirements of the UEs have been largely ignored. To address this, in this paper, we propose a mode selection algorithm for D2D enabled NSA based on a two-level Analytic Hierarchy Process (AHP). The proposed AHP-based mechanism considers the service requirements of the UEs in level 1; and mode selection options (i.e., LTE only, NR only, LTE via D2D and NR via D2D) in level 2. Thereafter, a novel mode selection algorithm is proposed by combining the static ranking computed by the proposed two-level AHP and the variation of Reference Signal Received Power (RSRP) in different modes, thus capturing the impact of UE mobility and reducing unnecessary handovers. Simulation results show that our proposed algorithm outperforms the best performing related work in terms of the major Key performance indicators (KPIs) for all three slices, i.e., enhanced mobile broadband (eMBB), ultra reliable low latency (uRLLc) and massive machine type communications (mMTc).

</details>


### [9] [AtlasRAN: Modeling and Performance Evaluation of Open 5G Platforms for Ubiquitous Wireless Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14661)
*Ryan Barker,Tolunay Seyfi,Alireza Ebrahimi Dorcheh,Julia Boone,Fatemeh Afghah,Joseph Boccuzzi*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出AtlasRAN框架，用于5G O-RAN平台的建模与性能评估。研究发现现有研究中常将时序、I/O和控制循环行为在不同仿真环境中视为等效，但实际上并不如此，导致性能瓶颈被误判。通过CU-DU上行负载实验验证，发现聚合吞吐量随用户数增加而下降的主要原因并非解码器饱和，而是仿真环境的时序扩展和I/O饥饿，强调了时序、内存和传输语义应作为首要实验变量报告。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有5G系统研究中，来自仿真器、操作系统模拟器、数字孪生和硬件在环测试平台的实验结果常被直接比较，但它们在时序、输入/输出和控制循环行为方面并不等效。这导致吞吐量、延迟、可扩展性或实时行为等方面的表观限制可能反映的是执行环境而非无线设计本身的问题，亟需一个能够区分功能兼容性与时序保真度的评估框架。

Method: 提出AtlasRAN，一个面向能力的框架，用于建模和评估5G开放无线接入网（O-RAN）平台。该框架引入了两种参考架构、将功能兼容性与时序保真度分离的术语体系，以及一个能力矩阵，用于将研究问题映射到能够可信支持它们的评估环境。框架以O-RAN作为实验坐标系，涵盖集中单元/分布式单元划分、前传传输、控制暴露和核心网锚定。在一套一致的CPU-GPU边缘平台上通过CU-DU上行负载研究进行验证。

Result: 在CPU-only基线和GPU加速的低密度奇偶校验解码变体中，聚合有效吞吐量随用户数从1增加到12而急剧下降，而公平性保持接近理想状态，计算利用率反而下降而非上升。这一模式表明，主要的扩展限制来自仿真环境的时序扩展和在线I/O饥饿，而非解码器饱和。

Conclusion: 在评估无处不在的5G基础设施时，时序、内存和传输语义必须作为首要实验变量进行报告，而不是假设不同仿真环境在这些方面等效。这对于准确识别性能瓶颈的真正来源至关重要。

Abstract: Fifth-generation (5G) systems are increasingly studied as shared communication and computing infrastructure for connected vehicles, roadside edge platforms, and future unmanned-system applications. Yet results from simulators, host-OS emulators, digital twins, and hardware-in-the-loop testbeds are often compared as if timing, input/output (I/O), and control-loop behavior were equivalent across them. They are not. Consequently, apparent limits in throughput, latency, scalability, or real-time behavior may reflect the execution harness rather than the wireless design itself.
  This paper presents \textit{AtlasRAN}, a capability-oriented framework for modeling and performance evaluation of 5G Open Radio Access Network (O-RAN) platforms. It introduces two reference architectures, terminology that separates functional compatibility from timing fidelity, and a capability matrix that maps research questions to evaluation environments that can support them credibly. O-RAN is used here as an experimental coordinate system spanning Centralized Unit (CU)/Distributed Unit (DU) partitioning, fronthaul transport, control exposure, and core-network anchoring.
  We validate \textit{AtlasRAN} through a CU-DU uplink load study on a coherent CPU-GPU edge platform. For both a CPU-only baseline and a GPU-accelerated low-density parity-check decoding variant, aggregate goodput drops sharply as user count rises from 1 to 12, while fairness remains near ideal and compute utilization decreases rather than increases. This pattern indicates time-scale dilation and online I/O starvation in the emulation harness, not decoder saturation, as the dominant scaling limit. The key lesson is that timing, memory, and transport semantics must be reported as first-class experimental variables when evaluating ubiquitous 5G infrastructure.

</details>


### [10] [SliceMapper: Intelligent Mapping of O-CU and O-DU onto O-Cloud Sites in 6G O-RAN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15242)
*Mohammad Asif Habibi,Xavier Costa-Pérez,Hans D. Schotten*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了SliceMapper，一个用于优化6G O-RAN切片子网映射到O-Cloud站点的rApp，通过对比四种强化学习方法，发现函数近似方法稳定性更好，而表格表示方法平均奖励更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在第六代（6G）开放无线接入网（O-RAN）中，开放集中单元（O-CU）和开放分布单元（O-DU）的切片子网到底层开放云（O-Cloud）站点的映射过程需要优化，以提高网络效率和资源利用率。

Method: 首先设计SliceMapper的系统模型并引入其数学框架；然后将映射过程建模为序贯决策优化问题；接着实现了Q-learning算法的策略上和策略外两种变体，每种变体分别采用表格表示和函数近似两种方法，共四种实现方案进行对比。

Result: 仿真实验表明，策略上的函数近似方法在所有随机种子下表现更稳定且标准差更低；而策略上和策略外的表格表示方法分别获得了5.42和5.12的更高平均奖励。

Conclusion: 本文成功提出了SliceMapper并验证了不同强化学习方法的有效性，不同方法在稳定性和平均奖励方面各有优势，最后提出了未来研究的若干方向。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose an rApp, named SliceMapper, to optimize the mapping process of the open centralized unit (O-CU) and open distributed unit (O-DU) of an open radio access network (O-RAN) slice subnet onto the underlying open cloud (O-Cloud) sites in sixth-generation (6G) O-RAN. To accomplish this, we first design a system model for SliceMapper and introduce its mathematical framework. Next, we formulate the mapping process addressed by SliceMapper as a sequential decision-making optimization problem. To solve this problem, we implement both on-policy and off-policy variants of the Q-learning algorithm, employing tabular representation as well as function approximation methods for each variant. To evaluate the effectiveness of these approaches, we conduct a series of simulations under various scenarios. We proceed further by performing a comparative analysis of all four variants. The results demonstrate that the on-policy function approximation method outperforms the alternative approaches in terms of stability and lower standard deviation across all random seeds. However, the on-policy and off-policy tabular representation methods achieve higher average rewards, with values of 5.42 and 5.12, respectively. Finally, we conclude the paper and introduce several directions for future research.

</details>


### [11] [ln(3): A Universal Percolation Constant for Collective Dynamics on One-Dimensional Proximity Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15521)
*Jian Ji*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文发现并证明了通用常数ln(3)≈1.099，它决定了一维泊松邻近网络中双向集体行为的涌现阈值。当拓扑密度(λL)≥ln(3)时，系统才能产生宏观协调性。该理论通过成都V2X数据集（1970万条记录）和德国高速公路数据集（163,896观测）验证，结果高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维空间中智能体之间产生双向集体行为的临界条件。作者旨在寻找一个普适的、与模型无关的拓扑阈值，以揭示空间对称性对协作信息交换的根本约束。

Method: 基于无记忆性对称公理推导泊松分布，证明ln(3)是方程2/(exp(x)-1)=1的唯一正解，即为合作渗透常数。通过数学分析证明当且仅当拓扑密度λL≥ln(3)时，邻近图的期望包含双向生成簇。使用两个独立大规模数据集验证：成都V2X车载单元数据集和德国highD高速公路轨迹数据集。

Result: 理论预测的ln(3)阈值在两个数据集中得到验证：成都数据集显示在阈值边界处速度方差降低1.60倍；德国数据集拟合LWR指数θ=1.033±0.088，理论值位于0.75σ置信区间内(R²=0.8631)。跨地理和物理尺度（从高速公路交通到一维生物信号传输）均观察到该阈值的一致性。

Conclusion: ln(3)是一个源于空间对称性的基本拓扑常数，代表协作信息交换必须支付的基本"租金"。该阈值是参数无关且模型无关的普适规律，揭示了双向集体行为涌现的根本拓扑约束，对理解交通流、生物信号传输等一维协作系统具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: We report the identification and proof of a universal constant, ln(3) = 1.09861, which governs the onset of bidirectional collective behavior in one-dimensional Poisson proximity networks. The constant - named the cooperative percolation constant and denoted by Lambda_c - is the unique positive solution to 2/(exp(x)-1) = 1 and equals the Shannon entropy of three equiprobable states. For agents distributed at intensity lambda and interacting within range L, bidirectional collective behavior is possible if and only if the topological density (lambda * L) >= ln(3). Below this threshold, no cooperative control policy can produce macroscopic coherence, as the proximity graph does not contain a bidirectional spanning cluster in expectation. The result is parameter-free and model-independent: the Poisson distribution is derived from memorylessness symmetry axioms, making ln(3) a fundamental consequence of spatial symmetry.
  The threshold is validated by two independent large-scale empirical datasets. Analysis of the Chengdu V2X OBU dataset (N = 19.7 million records) reveals a 1.60x reduction in speed variance at the predicted boundary. Furthermore, the highD German motorway dataset (N = 163,896 observations) yields a best-fit LWR exponent theta = 1.033 +/- 0.088, placing the theoretical value ln(3) within 0.75 sigma of naturalistic trajectory data (R^2 = 0.8631). The remarkable consistency across geographical and physical scales - from motorway traffic to documented thresholds in 1D biological signal transmission - suggests that ln(3) represents a fundamental topological rent for cooperative information exchange.

</details>

### [12] [Auditing Cascading Risks in Multi-Agent Systems via Semantic-Geometric Co-evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13325)
*Zixun Luo,Yuhang Fan,Hengyu Lin,Yufei Li,Youzhi Zhang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于语义-几何协同演化的级联风险检测框架，利用Ollivier-Ricci曲率分析多智能体系统的交互图结构，能够在语义违规发生前数轮交互中提前预警风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于大语言模型的多智能体系统存在级联风险，早期交互在语义上流畅且符合策略，但底层交互动态已经开始扭曲，潜伏不稳定性或不对齐问题。传统的基于单消息语义内容的审计方法本质上是反应性的，存在滞后性，无法捕捉这些早期结构前兆。

Method: 将多智能体系统交互建模为动态图，引入离散几何度量Ollivier-Ricci曲率（ORC）来刻画通信拓扑中的信息冗余和瓶颈形成。通过将语义流信号与图几何相结合，框架学习可信协作的正常协同演化动态，将偏离耦合流形的现象视为早期预警信号。

Result: 在一系列与风险类别对齐的级联风险场景实验中，曲率异常系统地早于显式语义违规数轮交互出现，使得主动干预成为可能。Ricci曲率的局部特性为根因归因提供了可解释性，能够识别导致可信协作崩溃的特定智能体或链接。

Conclusion: 该框架实现了对多智能体系统级联风险的前瞻性检测，克服了传统语义审计方法的滞后性缺陷，为系统安全性提供了早期预警和可解释的根因定位能力。

Abstract: Large Language model (LLM)-based Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) are prone to cascading risks, where early-stage interactions remain semantically fluent and policy-compliant, yet the underlying interaction dynamics begin to distort in ways that amplify latent instability or misalignment. Traditional auditing methods that focus on per-message semantic content are inherently reactive and lagging, failing to capture these early structural precursors. In this paper, we propose a principled framework for cascading-risk detection grounded in semantic--geometric co-evolution. We model MAS interactions as dynamic graphs and introduce Ollivier--Ricci Curvature (ORC) -- a discrete geometric measure -- to characterize information redundancy and bottleneck formation in communication topologies. By coupling semantic flow signals with graph geometry, the framework learns the normal co-evolutionary dynamics of trusted collaboration and treats deviations from this coupled manifold as early-warning signals. Experiments on a suite of cascading-risk scenarios aligned with the risk category demonstrate that curvature anomalies systematically precede explicit semantic violations by several interaction turns, enabling proactive intervention. Furthermore, the local nature of Ricci curvature provides principled interpretability for root-cause attribution, identifying specific agents or links that precipitate the collapse of trustworthy collaboration.

</details>

Result: 该框架成功实现了气候指标、社会变量和环境结果之间关系的自适应和可解释探索。通过多智能体AI系统与定量分析的结合，ClimateAgents展示了如何增强分析推理能力，促进对复杂社会-环境系统的跨学科、数据驱动调查。系统能够有效整合多源数据并支持研究人员探索社会-环境动态。

Abstract: The complex interaction between social behaviors and climate change requires more than traditional data-driven prediction; it demands interpretable and adaptive analytical frameworks capable of integrating heterogeneous sources of knowledge. This study introduces ClimateAgents, a multi-agent research assistant designed to support social-climate analysis through coordinated AI agents. Rather than focusing solely on predictive modeling, the framework assists researchers in exploring socio-environmental dynamics by integrating multimodal data retrieval, statistical modeling, textual analysis, and automated reasoning. Traditional approaches to climate analysis often address narrowly defined indicators and lack the flexibility to incorporate cross-domain socio-economic knowledge or adapt to evolving research questions. To address these limitations, ClimateAgents employs a set of collaborative, domain-specialized agents that collectively perform key stages of the research workflow, including hypothesis generation, data analysis, evidence retrieval, and structured reporting. The framework supports exploratory analysis and scenario investigation using datasets from sources such as the United Nations and the World Bank. By combining agent-based reasoning with quantitative analysis of socio-economic behavioral dynamics, ClimateAgents enables adaptive and interpretable exploration of relationships between climate indicators, social variables, and environmental outcomes. The results illustrate how multi-agent AI systems can augment analytical reasoning and facilitate interdisciplinary, data-driven investigation of complex socio-environmental systems.

### [15] [Beyond Self-Interest: Modeling Social-Oriented Motivation for Human-like Multi-Agent Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13890)
*Jingzhe Lin,Ceyao Zhang,Yaodong Yang,Yizhou Wang,Song-Chun Zhu,Fangwei Zhong*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了ASVO（自主社会价值导向智能体）框架，将基于LLM的智能体与欲望驱动机制和社会价值取向（SVO）理论相结合，实现了更具人类特征的多智能体社交交互。实验表明该方法在行为自然性和拟人化方面显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型方法在生成复杂行为方面具有潜力，但缺乏在多智能体交互中对人类社会动机的建模机制，无法真实模拟人类社交行为。

Method: 提出ASVO框架：1）智能体通过感知环境变化和他人行动更新信念；2）基于反思推理更新多维欲望值并推断他人动机状态；3）通过对比自身满足感与他人满足感动态计算SVO（从利他到竞争的谱系）；4）SVO指导活动选择，平衡欲望满足与社会一致性。

Result: 在School、Workplace和Family三种场景下的实验表明，ASVO在行为自然性和拟人化方面相比基线方法有显著提升。

Conclusion: 结构化的欲望系统和自适应的SVO漂移机制能够实现真实的多智能体社会模拟，验证了将社会心理学理论融入LLM智能体设计的有效性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate significant potential for generating complex behaviors, yet most approaches lack mechanisms for modeling social motivation in human-like multi-agent interaction. We introduce Autonomous Social Value-Oriented agents (ASVO), where LLM-based agents integrate desire-driven autonomy with Social Value Orientation (SVO) theory. At each step, agents first update their beliefs by perceiving environmental changes and others' actions. These observations inform the value update process, where each agent updates multi-dimensional desire values through reflective reasoning and infers others' motivational states. By contrasting self-satisfaction derived from fulfilled desires against estimated others' satisfaction, agents dynamically compute their SVO along a spectrum from altruistic to competitive, which in turn guides activity selection to balance desire fulfillment with social alignment. Experiments across School, Workplace, and Family contexts demonstrate substantial improvements over baselines in behavioral naturalness and human-likeness. These findings show that structured desire systems and adaptive SVO drift enable realistic multi-agent social simulations.

</details>


### [16] [A Benchmark for Multi-Party Negotiation Games from Real Negotiation Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14066)
*Leo Benac,Jonas Raedler,Zilin Ma,Finale Doshi-Velez*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文研究多方谈判中的序列承诺决策问题，提出可配置博弈生成器和三种价值函数近似方法，发现不同博弈结构需要不同的估值策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的多方谈判通常以一系列具有约束力的行动级承诺序列展开，而非一次性达成最终结果。然而，这一重要谈判机制在现有研究中尚未得到充分探索，缺乏相应的评估基准和分析框架。

Method: 研究者开发了可配置的博弈生成器，能够调节激励对齐、目标复杂性和收益分配等关键结构属性。同时设计了三种价值函数近似方法用于决策评估：近视奖励、乐观上界和悲观下界，这些方法作为交易评估的偏置视角。通过在小规模博弈上的精确评估和基于哈佛谈判挑战的大规模文档实例上的比较评估来验证方法。

Result: 研究发现不同的博弈结构要求不同的估值策略。研究团队成功绘制了每种近似方法成功或失败的战略机制图谱，揭示了博弈结构与最优估值策略之间的关联关系。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，需要开发能够学习鲁棒状态价值并在长期视野、绑定承诺和仅终端奖励条件下进行有效规划的新型智能体，以应对不同博弈结构的挑战。

Abstract: Many real-world multi-party negotiations unfold as sequences of binding, action-level commitments rather than a single final outcome. We introduce a benchmark for this under-studied regime featuring a configurable game generator that sweeps key structural properties such as incentive alignment, goal complexity, and payoff distribution. To evaluate decision-making, we test three value-function approximations - myopic reward, an optimistic upper bound, and a pessimistic lower bound - that act as biased lenses on deal evaluation. Through exact evaluation on small games and comparative evaluation on large, document-grounded instances derived from the Harvard Negotiation Challenge, we map the strategic regimes where each approximation succeeds or fails. We observe that different game structures demand different valuation strategies, motivating agents that learn robust state values and plan effectively over long horizons under binding commitments and terminal only rewards.

</details>


### [17] [Understanding Strategic Platform Entry and Seller Exploration: A Stackelberg Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14206)
*Garrett Seo,Xintong Wang,David C. Parkes*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文研究在线平台（如Amazon、Apple）进入自身市场并与第三方卖家竞争的现象。通过Stackelberg博弈模型和深度强化学习方法，分析了平台的进入策略与卖家的探索-开发策略，揭示了平台进入对卖家创新的激励影响，为监管政策提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建Stackelberg博弈模型，平台作为领导者承诺进入策略。针对单一卖家场景，采用Gittins指数策略刻画卖家的最优探索-开发决策，并设计算法计算平台的最优进入策略。针对多卖家场景（考虑竞争和信息溢出），Gittins指数方法失效，采用深度强化学习方法研究卖家均衡行为。

Result: 在单一卖家场景下，成功刻画了卖家的最优策略并给出了平台最优进入策略的计算方法。在多卖家场景下，通过深度强化学习揭示了卖家均衡行为特征。研究发现揭示了驱动平台进入和卖家创新的激励机制，与Amazon和Google Play等市场的实证证据相一致。

Conclusion: 平台的进入策略会对卖家的创新激励产生显著影响。研究为监管机构制定保护创新和市场多样性的政策提供了理论支撑和实证依据，对理解平台经济中的竞争动态具有重要意义。

Abstract: Online market platforms play an increasingly powerful role in the economy. An empirical phenomenon is that platforms, such as Amazon, Apple, and DoorDash, also enter their own marketplaces, imitating successful products developed by third-party sellers. We formulate a Stackelberg model, where the platform acts as the leader by committing to an entry policy: when will it enter and compete on a product? We study this model through a theoretical and computational framework. We begin with a single seller, and consider different kinds of policies for entry. We characterize the seller's optimal explore-exploit strategy via a Gittins-index policy, and give an algorithm to compute the platform's optimal entry policy. We then consider multiple sellers, to account for competition and information spillover. Here, the Gittins-index characterization fails, and we employ deep reinforcement learning to examine seller equilibrium behavior. Our findings highlight the incentives that drive platform entry and seller innovation, consistent with empirical evidence from markets such as Amazon and Google Play, with implications for regulatory efforts to preserve innovation and market diversity.

### [18] [EcoFair-CH-MARL: Scalable Constrained Hierarchical Multi-Agent RL with Real-Time Emission Budgets and Fairness Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14625)
*Saad Alqithami*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了EcoFair-CH-MARL框架，一种受约束的分层多智能体强化学习方法，通过预算层约束排放、公平感知奖励机制和双层策略架构，在海事物流场景中实现了排放降低、吞吐量提升和成本公平性的显著改善。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全球脱碳目标和市场压力要求海事物流解决方案同时具备高效、可持续和公平性，但在随机天气和需求下实现排放约束、异构船队公平协调和大规模智能体可扩展性仍是重大挑战。

Method: 提出EcoFair-CH-MARL框架，包含三个创新：(i)原始-对偶预算层，在随机天气和需求下可证明地约束累积排放；(ii)公平感知奖励转换器，通过动态惩罚调度实现异构船队的最大-最小成本公平；(iii)双层策略架构，解耦战略路由与实时船舶控制，实现智能体数量的线性扩展。理论证明约束违反和公平性损失均为O(√T)遗憾界。

Result: 在16港口、50船舶的高保真海事数字孪生及能源电网案例上的实验表明：相比最先进的分层和约束MARL基线，排放降低达15%，吞吐量提升12%，公平成本改善45%；相比公平性专用MARL基线（SOTO、FEN）具有更强的公平性（更低基尼系数和更高最小-最大福利）；模块化设计兼容策略基和价值基学习器。

Conclusion: EcoFair-CH-MARL推进了安全关键领域大规模、符合法规和社会责任的多智能体协调的可行性，为海事物流等领域的可持续公平决策提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Global decarbonisation targets and tightening market pressures demand maritime logistics solutions that are simultaneously efficient, sustainable, and equitable. We introduce EcoFair-CH-MARL, a constrained hierarchical multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that unifies three innovations: (i) a primal-dual budget layer that provably bounds cumulative emissions under stochastic weather and demand; (ii) a fairness-aware reward transformer with dynamically scheduled penalties that enforces max-min cost equity across heterogeneous fleets; and (iii) a two-tier policy architecture that decouples strategic routing from real-time vessel control, enabling linear scaling in agent count. New theoretical results establish O(\sqrt{T}) regret for both constraint violations and fairness loss. Experiments on a high-fidelity maritime digital twin (16 ports, 50 vessels) driven by automatic identification system traces, plus an energy-grid case study, show up to 15% lower emissions, 12% higher through-put, and a 45% fair-cost improvement over state-of-the-art hierarchical and constrained MARL baselines. In addition, EcoFair-CH-MARL achieves stronger equity (lower Gini and higher min-max welfare) than fairness-specific MARL baselines (e.g., SOTO, FEN), and its modular design is compatible with both policy- and value-based learners. EcoFair-CH-MARL therefore advances the feasibility of large-scale, regulation-compliant, and socially responsible multi-agent coordination in safety-critical domains.

### [19] [Forecast-Aware Cooperative Planning on Temporal Graphs under Stochastic Adversarial Risk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14697)
*Manshi Limbu,Xuan Wang,Gregory J. Stein,Daigo Shishika,Xuesu Xiao*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种预测感知的协同规划框架，通过集成随机风险预测和前瞻性支持分配来解决动态风险环境下的多机器人协同任务问题，显著降低了团队预期成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于支持协调的框架假设风险环境是静态的，无法应对由敌方巡逻或动态变化风险源引起的可预测风险时序变化，限制了协同任务的有效性。

Method: 将敌方动态建模为图边上的一阶马尔可夫停留-移动过程，通过时间传播生成时间索引的边缘风险预测；基于这些预测在时间图上进行前瞻性支持位置分配，并指导联合路径规划。

Result: 实验结果表明，与非预测性基线方法相比，该方法能够持续降低团队总预期成本，其性能接近于具有完全信息的oracle规划器。

Conclusion: 通过整合随机风险预测与前瞻性支持分配，该方法能够有效应对动态变化的风险环境，显著提升多机器人协同任务的效率和安全性。

Abstract: Cooperative multi-robot missions often require teams of robots to traverse environments where traversal risk evolves due to adversary patrols or shifting hazards with stochastic dynamics. While support coordination - where robots assist teammates in traversing risky regions - can significantly reduce mission costs, its effectiveness depends on the team's ability to anticipate future risk. Existing support-based frameworks assume static risk landscapes and therefore fail to account for predictable temporal trends in risk evolution. We propose a forecast-aware cooperative planning framework that integrates stochastic risk forecasting with anticipatory support allocation on temporal graphs. By modeling adversary dynamics as a first-order Markov stay-move process over graph edges, we propagate the resulting edge-occupancy probabilities forward in time to generate time-indexed edge-risk forecasts. These forecasts guide the proactive allocation of support positions to forecasted risky edges for effective support coordination, while also informing joint robot path planning. Experimental results demonstrate that our approach consistently reduces total expected team cost compared to non-anticipatory baselines, approaching the performance of an oracle planner.

### [20] [Translational Gaps in Graph Transformers for Longitudinal EHR Prediction: A Critical Appraisal of GT-BEHRT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13231)
*Krish Tadigotla*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对GT-BEHRT图Transformer架构进行了批判性综述，评估其在MIMIC-IV和All of Us数据集上的表现，发现该模型虽在心力衰竭预测任务上取得了优异的判别性能（AUROC 94.37），但在校准分析、公平性评估、队列选择敏感性及部署可行性等方面存在显著不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的EHR模型通常将每次临床就诊视为无序的代码集合，限制了对就诊内部有意义关系的捕捉能力。GT-BEHRT通过图Transformer方法建模就诊级别结构，声称解决了这一局限，本文旨在批判性审查其性能增益是否真实反映架构优势，以及评估方法是否支持其稳健性和临床相关性声明。

Method: 从七个维度对GT-BEHRT进行全面分析：表示设计、预训练策略、队列构建透明度、超越判别的评估、公平性评估、可复现性及部署可行性。审查其在MIMIC-IV重症监护结局和All of Us研究计划心力衰竭预测任务上的评估方法论。

Result: GT-BEHRT在365天内心力衰竭预测任务上报告了强劲的判别性能：AUROC 94.37±0.20，AUPRC 73.96±0.83，F1 64.70±0.85。然而，研究识别出多项重要缺陷：缺乏校准分析、公平性评估不完整、对队列选择敏感、跨表型和预测时间范围分析有限、以及对实际部署考虑的讨论不足。

Conclusion: GT-BEHRT代表了EHR表示学习领域的有意义架构进步，但需要更严格的评估，特别是在校准、公平性和部署方面，才能可靠地支持临床决策。模型在应用于临床实践前仍需填补这些关键缺口。

Abstract: Transformer-based models have improved predictive modeling on longitudinal electronic health records through large-scale self-supervised pretraining. However, most EHR transformer architectures treat each clinical encounter as an unordered collection of codes, which limits their ability to capture meaningful relationships within a visit. Graph-transformer approaches aim to address this limitation by modeling visit-level structure while retaining the ability to learn long-term temporal patterns. This paper provides a critical review of GT-BEHRT, a graph-transformer architecture evaluated on MIMIC-IV intensive care outcomes and heart failure prediction in the All of Us Research Program. We examine whether the reported performance gains reflect genuine architectural benefits and whether the evaluation methodology supports claims of robustness and clinical relevance. We analyze GT-BEHRT across seven dimensions relevant to modern machine learning systems, including representation design, pretraining strategy, cohort construction transparency, evaluation beyond discrimination, fairness assessment, reproducibility, and deployment feasibility. GT-BEHRT reports strong discrimination for heart failure prediction within 365 days, with AUROC 94.37 +/- 0.20, AUPRC 73.96 +/- 0.83, and F1 64.70 +/- 0.85. Despite these results, we identify several important gaps, including the lack of calibration analysis, incomplete fairness evaluation, sensitivity to cohort selection, limited analysis across phenotypes and prediction horizons, and limited discussion of practical deployment considerations. Overall, GT-BEHRT represents a meaningful architectural advance in EHR representation learning, but more rigorous evaluation focused on calibration, fairness, and deployment is needed before such models can reliably support clinical decision-making.

### [21] [RFX-Fuse: Breiman and Cutler's Unified ML Engine + Native Explainable Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13234)
*Chris Kuchar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RFX-Fuse 实现了 Breiman 和 Cutler 最初的随机森林完整愿景，提供一个统一的机器学习引擎，替代现代需要5+工具的复杂流水线，并引入了邻近度重要性和无监督填补验证两项创新。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代机器学习流水线需要组合多个独立工具（如XGBoost、FAISS、SHAP、Isolation Forest等）来完成不同任务，这增加了系统复杂性和维护成本。而 Breiman 和 Cutler 最初设计的随机森林本应是一个统一的机器学习引擎，具备分类、回归、无监督学习、相似性、异常检测、缺失值填补和可视化等完整能力，但现代库（如scikit-learn）从未完整实现这些功能。

Method: 开发了 RFX-Fuse（Random Forests X -- Forest Unified Learning and Similarity Engine），原生支持 GPU/CPU，通过一次性训练单一树集来实现所有功能，替代多个独立工具的组合使用。提出了两项创新：（1）Proximity Importance——原生可解释相似性，不仅测量样本相似度，还能解释相似的原因；（2）针对通用表格数据的数据集特定填补验证——通过评估填补数据的真实性来排序填补方法，无需真实标签。

Result: RFX-Fuse 成功实现了 Breiman 和 Cutler 的完整随机森林愿景，提供了包含分类、回归、无监督学习、邻近度相似性、异常检测、缺失值填补和可视化等功能的统一模型对象。通过单一树集替代了传统需要5个以上工具的机器学习流水线，同时引入了新的可解释性方法和填补验证技术。

Conclusion: RFX-Fuse 证明了一个统一、可解释的随机森林引擎在现代机器学习场景中的可行性和优势，能够显著简化机器学习流水线，减少对多个独立工具的依赖，同时提供了更原生的可解释性和更高效的数据处理能力。

Abstract: Breiman and Cutler's original Random Forest was designed as a unified ML engine -- not merely an ensemble predictor. Their implementation included classification, regression, unsupervised learning, proximity-based similarity, outlier
  detection, missing value imputation, and visualization -- capabilities that modern libraries like scikit-learn never implemented. RFX-Fuse (Random Forests X [X=compression] -- Forest Unified Learning and Similarity Engine) delivers
  Breiman and Cutler's complete vision with native GPU/CPU support. Modern ML pipelines require 5+ separate tools -- XGBoost for prediction, FAISS for similarity, SHAP for explanations, Isolation Forest for outliers, custom code for
  importance. RFX-Fuse provides a 1 to 2 model object alternative -- a single set of trees grown once. Novel Contributions: (1) Proximity Importance -- native explainable similarity: proximity measures that samples are similar;
  proximity importance explains why. (2) Dataset-specific imputation validation for general tabular data -- ranking imputation methods by how real the imputed data looks, without ground truth labels.

</details>


### [22] [Continual Fine-Tuning with Provably Accurate and Parameter-Free Task Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13235)
*Hang Thi-Thuy Le,Long Minh Bui,Minh Hoang,Trong Nghia Hoang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的参数自适应持续微调方法，结合了输入自适应和参数自适应的优势，通过无参数检索实现测试时的自适应表示使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的持续微调方法存在局限性：输入自适应方法需要在测试时检索相关提示，但检索函数容易遗忘；参数自适应方法避免了遗忘但牺牲了表示适应性。作者希望结合两者的优势。

Method: 提出两个关键组件：（1）自适应模块组合策略，学习有信息的任务特定更新以保持和补充先验知识；（2）基于聚类的检索机制，捕获每个任务的独特表示签名，实现测试时的自适应表示使用。同时推导了基于聚类的无参数范式的任务检索误差界，提供了理论保证。

Result: 理论分析表明，组织良好的聚类结构能够实现可靠的检索。实验表明，这两个组件协同工作，在任务语义发生大幅变化时能够提高检索和预测性能。

Conclusion: 该方法成功结合了输入自适应和参数自适应方法的优势，通过无参数检索实现了测试时的自适应表示使用，在保持性能的同时避免了遗忘问题。

Abstract: Continual fine-tuning aims to adapt a pre-trained backbone to new tasks sequentially while preserving performance on earlier tasks whose data are no longer available. Existing approaches fall into two categories which include input- and parameter-adaptation. Input-adaptation methods rely on retrieving the most relevant prompts at test time, but require continuously learning a retrieval function that is prone to forgetting. Parameter-adaptation methods instead use a fixed input embedding function to enable retrieval-free prediction and avoid forgetting, but sacrifice representation adaptability. To combine their best strengths, we propose a new parameter-adaptation method that enables adaptive use of input embeddings during test time with parameter-free retrieval. We derive task-retrieval error bounds for a clustering-based, parameter-free paradigm, providing theoretical guarantees that link low retrieval error to structural properties of task-specific representation clusters, revealing a fresh insight into how well-organized clustering structure will enable reliable retrieval. Motivated by this insight, our method is designed with two key components: (i) an adaptive module composition strategy that learns informative task-specific updates to preserve and complement prior knowledge, and (ii) a clustering-based retrieval mechanism that captures distinct representation signatures for each task, enabling adaptive representation use at test time. Extensive experiments show that these components work synergistically to improve retrieval and predictive performance under large shifts in task semantics.

</details>


### [23] [Introducing Feature-Based Trajectory Clustering, a clustering algorithm for longitudinal data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13254)
*Marie-Pierre Sylvestre,Laurence Boulanger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的纵向数据聚类算法，通过两步法将具有相似时间演化特征的个体进行聚类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纵向数据中，个体的时间演化模式既存在差异性也存在共性特征。现有方法难以有效识别共享特定时间演化特征的个体群体，因此需要开发一种能够捕捉这些共性特征并进行聚类的新方法。

Method: 采用两步法：第一步将每个个体映射到欧几里得空间中的点，其坐标由特定数学公式确定，用以捕捉多种时间演化的特征；第二步对得到的点云应用谱聚类算法进行聚类。

Result: 该方法能够有效地将具有相似潜在时间演化特征的个体识别并聚集到同一簇中，实现了纵向数据的聚类。

Conclusion: 所提出的算法为纵向数据分析提供了一种有效的聚类工具，能够发现个体间共享的时间演化模式。

Abstract: We present a new algorithm for clustering longitudinal data. Data of this type can be conceptualized as consisting of individuals and, for each such individual, observations of a time-dependent variable made at various times. Generically, the specific way in which this variable evolves with time is different from one individual to the next. However, there may also be commonalities; specific characteristic features of the time evolution shared by many individuals. The purpose of the method we put forward is to find clusters of individual whose underlying time-dependent variables share such characteristic features. This is done in two steps. The first step identifies each individual to a point in Euclidean space whose coordinates are determined by specific mathematical formulae meant to capture a variety of characteristic features. The second step finds the clusters by applying the Spectral Clustering algorithm to the resulting point cloud.

</details>


### [24] [Your Code Agent Can Grow Alongside You with Structured Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13258)
*Yi-Xuan Deng,Xiaoqin Liu,Yi Zhang,Guo-Wei Yang,Shuojin Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出MemCoder框架，通过挖掘项目历史提交中的意图-代码映射、实时验证反馈和经验内化机制，使代码智能体能持续与人类协同进化，在SWE-bench Verified上实现SOTA性能，较DeepSeek-V3.2提升9.4%解决率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码智能体仅依赖静态代码快照，无法捕捉项目时间演化过程中隐含的推理轨迹和成功实践经验，导致行为逻辑僵化、缺乏自适应能力，难以应对复杂的仓库级问题。

Method: 提出MemCoder框架：1）从历史提交中结构化人类经验，提炼潜在意图到代码的映射；2）引入基于验证反馈的自精炼机制实时修正智能体行为；3）设计经验自我内化机制，将人类验证的解决方案固化为长期知识，支持持续演化。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified基准上达到SOTA性能，相比通用基础模型DeepSeek-V3.2，解决率提升9.4%。实验证明通过项目历史和实时反馈实现人机协同进化的有效性。

Conclusion: 赋予智能体通过项目历史和实时反馈与人类协同进化的能力，能有效释放通用大模型在复杂软件工程任务中的潜力，为意图导向编程范式下的智能体发展提供了可行路径。

Abstract: While "Intent-oriented programming" (or "Vibe Coding") redefines software engineering, existing code agents remain tethered to static code snapshots. Consequently, they struggle to model the critical information embedded in the temporal evolution of projects, failing to leverage the "reasoning trajectories" implicit in past successful practices. This limitation results in rigid behavioral logic and a lack of autonomous adaptability, ultimately hindering their ability to tackle complex, repository-level problems. To bridge this static-dynamic mismatch, we propose MemCoder, a framework designed to enable continual human-AI co-evolution. MemCoder first structures historical human experience to distill latent intent-to-code mappings from past commits. It then employs a self-refinement mechanism driven by verification feedback to correct agent behavior in real-time. Crucially, an experience self-internalization mechanism is introduced to crystallize human-validated solutions into long-term knowledge, thereby supporting sustained evolution. Experimental results on SWE-bench Verified demonstrate that MemCoder not only achieves State-of-the-Art (SOTA) performance but also delivers a 9.4% improvement in resolved rate over the general foundation model DeepSeek-V3.2. These findings indicate that equipping agents with the capability to co-evolve with humans via project history and real-time feedback effectively unlocks the potential of general models in complex software engineering tasks.

</details>


### [25] [Beyond Attention: True Adaptive World Models via Spherical Kernel Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13263)
*Vladimer Khasia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出球面核算子（SKO）替代标准注意力机制，通过将数据流形投影到超球面并利用Gegenbauer多项式进行积分重建，突破了传统方法中正算子的饱和现象，使近似误差仅依赖于流形内在维度而非环境维度，从而为世界模型构建提供了数学上更严谨的范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的世界模型范式存在数学缺陷：将高维观测投影到参数化潜在空间后学习转移动态，只是将流形学习问题转移到了潜在空间。当数据分布变化时，潜在流形随之变化，迫使预测算子隐式重新学习新的拓扑结构。此外，经典近似理论表明，点积注意力等正算子不可避免地遭受饱和现象，永久性地限制了预测能力并使其易受维度灾难影响。

Method: 受Ryan O'Dowd基础工作的启发，引入球面核算子（SKO）框架替代标准注意力。核心方法包括：（1）将未知数据流形投影到统一的环绕超球面；（2）利用局部化的超球面（Gegenbauer）多项式序列，对目标函数进行直接积分重建；（3）将非归一化输出形式化为真实的测度支持估计器，从数学上将真实环境转移动力学与智能体的有偏观测频率解耦。

Result: 理论结果表明，由于局部化球面多项式核不是严格正定的，SKO成功绕过了饱和现象，获得了仅依赖于内在流形维度q而非环境维度的近似误差界。实证评估证实，SKO显著加速了收敛速度，在自回归语言建模任务中优于标准注意力基线。

Conclusion: SKO框架为世界模型构建提供了数学上严谨的范式，成功解决了传统方法中潜在空间流形学习和正算子饱和现象的根本缺陷，在理论和实证层面均展现出优越性，为基于世界模型的人工智能研究开辟了新方向。

Abstract: The pursuit of world model based artificial intelligence has predominantly relied on projecting high-dimensional observations into parameterized latent spaces, wherein transition dynamics are subsequently learned. However, this conventional paradigm is mathematically flawed: it merely displaces the manifold learning problem into the latent space. When the underlying data distribution shifts, the latent manifold shifts accordingly, forcing the predictive operator to implicitly relearn the new topological structure. Furthermore, by classical approximation theory, positive operators like dot product attention inevitably suffer from the saturation phenomenon, permanently bottlenecking their predictive capacity and leaving them vulnerable to the curse of dimensionality. In this paper, we formulate a mathematically rigorous paradigm for world model construction by redefining the core predictive mechanism. Inspired by Ryan O'Dowd's foundational work we introduce Spherical Kernel Operator (SKO), a framework that replaces standard attention. By projecting the unknown data manifold onto a unified ambient hypersphere and utilizing a localized sequence of ultraspherical (Gegenbauer) polynomials, SKO performs direct integral reconstruction of the target function. Because this localized spherical polynomial kernel is not strictly positive, it bypasses the saturation phenomenon, yielding approximation error bounds that depend strictly on the intrinsic manifold dimension q, rather than the ambient dimension. Furthermore, by formalizing its unnormalized output as an authentic measure support estimator, SKO mathematically decouples the true environmental transition dynamics from the biased observation frequency of the agent. Empirical evaluations confirm that SKO significantly accelerates convergence and outperforms standard attention baselines in autoregressive language modeling.

Our results further show that real user data is critical for effective personalization, as synthetic data degrades performance by up to 46%. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基础模型在语言和视觉领域通过在模态原生结构上学习取得成功，但无线数据包追踪通常被处理为扁平字符串。然而，无线数据包的有意义信息实际上来自分层头部、类型化字段、时间间隙和跨包状态机，因此需要一种能够理解和学习这种原生结构的方法。

Method: 提出Plume模型，使用协议感知的分词器：沿解析器字段树分割、发出时间间隙标记、标准化标识符，产生比BPE短6.2倍的序列且具有更高的每标记信息密度。模型在精心策划的语料库上训练，从结构化PDML解析中学习。

Abstract: Foundation models succeed when they learn in the native structure of a modality, whether morphology-respecting tokens in language or pixels in vision. Wireless packet traces deserve the same treatment: meaning emerges from layered headers, typed fields, timing gaps, and cross-packet state machines, not flat strings. We present Plume (Protocol Language Understanding Model for Exchanges), a compact 140M-parameter foundation model for 802.11 traces that learns from structured PDML dissections. A protocol-aware tokenizer splits along the dissector field tree, emits gap tokens for timing, and normalizes identifiers, yielding 6.2x shorter sequences than BPE with higher per token information density. Trained on a curated corpus, Plume achieves 74-97% next-packet token accuracy across five real-world failure categories and AUROC >= 0.99 for zero-shot anomaly detection. On the same prediction task, frontier LLMs (Claude Opus 4.6, GPT-5.4) score comparably despite receiving identical protocol context, yet Plume does so with > 600x fewer parameters, fitting on a single GPU at effectively zero marginal cost vs. cloud API pricing, enabling on-prem, privacy-preserving root cause analysis.

### [28] [Knowledge, Rules and Their Embeddings: Two Paths towards Neuro-Symbolic JEPA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13265)
*Yongchao Huang,Hassan Raza*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代自监督预测架构擅长从高维数据中捕获复杂统计相关性，但缺乏内化可验证人类逻辑的机制，容易受到虚假相关性和捷径学习的影响；传统基于规则的推理系统提供严谨、可解释的逻辑，但受限于离散边界和NP难组合爆炸问题。两者之间存在明显鸿沟，需要一种融合框架来协同两者优势。

Method: 提出以规则信息联合嵌入预测架构（RiJEPA）为核心的双向神经符号框架：
1. 前向方向：通过基于能量的约束（EBC）和多模态双编码器架构将结构化归纳偏置注入JEPA训练，用几何合理的逻辑能量盆地替代任意统计相关性，重塑表示流形；
2. 反向方向：将刚性离散符号规则松弛为连续可微逻辑，在规则能量景观中利用梯度引导的朗之万扩散，实现连续规则发现的新范式，支持无条件联合生成、条件前向推理、溯因推理和边际预测转换。

Result: 在合成拓扑仿真和高风险临床应用案例上的实验评估证实了该方法的有效性。框架成功实现了鲁棒、生成式且可解释的神经符号表示学习，证明了双向融合方法在解决虚假相关性、提升推理能力方面的优势。

Conclusion: 该框架为鲁棒、生成式和可解释的神经符号表示学习建立了强大的基础，成功弥合了统计驱动的深度学习与逻辑驱动的符号推理之间的鸿沟，为未来神经符号AI发展提供了新的研究方向。

Abstract: Modern self-supervised predictive architectures excel at capturing complex statistical correlations from high-dimensional data but lack mechanisms to internalize verifiable human logic, leaving them susceptible to spurious correlations and shortcut learning. Conversely, traditional rule-based inference systems offer rigorous, interpretable logic but suffer from discrete boundaries and NP-hard combinatorial explosion. To bridge this divide, we propose a bidirectional neuro-symbolic framework centered around Rule-informed Joint-Embedding Predictive Architectures (RiJEPA). In the first direction, we inject structured inductive biases into JEPA training via Energy-Based Constraints (EBC) and a multi-modal dual-encoder architecture. This fundamentally reshapes the representation manifold, replacing arbitrary statistical correlations with geometrically sound logical basins. In the second direction, we demonstrate that by relaxing rigid, discrete symbolic rules into a continuous, differentiable logic, we can bypass traditional combinatorial search for new rule generation. By leveraging gradient-guided Langevin diffusion within the rule energy landscape, we introduce novel paradigms for continuous rule discovery, which enable unconditional joint generation, conditional forward and abductive inference, and marginal predictive translation. Empirical evaluations on both synthetic topological simulations and a high-stakes clinical use case confirm the efficacy of our approach. Ultimately, this framework establishes a powerful foundation for robust, generative, and interpretable neuro-symbolic representation learning.

### [29] [Joint Routing and Model Pruning for Decentralized Federated Learning in Bandwidth-Constrained Multi-Hop Wireless Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15188)
*Xiaoyu He,Weicai Li,Tiejun Lv,Xi Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个联合路由与剪枝框架，通过优化路由路径和剪枝率来解决去中心化联邦学习中的通信瓶颈问题。仿真结果显示，该框架将平均传输延迟降低了27.8%，测试精度提高了约12%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化联邦学习（D-FL）在没有中央服务器的情况下实现了隐私保护的训练，但其多跳模型交换和聚合过程常常受到通信资源约束的瓶颈限制。现有方法在通信效率和模型性能之间存在权衡问题，亟需一种能够在保持通信延迟在规定限制内的同时最大化模型性能的解决方案。

Method: 提出了一个联合路由与剪枝框架，通过优化路由路径和剪枝率来维持通信延迟在规定限制内。首先分析了所有客户端的模型偏差总和如何影响D-FL的收敛界，然后构建了一个优化问题，在通信约束下最大化模型保留率以最小化这些偏差。进一步分析发现每个客户端的模型保留率是路径相关的，从而将原问题简化为路由优化问题。基于此洞察，开发了一种路由算法，选择延迟高效的传输路径，允许在时间预算内传输更多参数。

Result: 仿真实验表明，与未剪枝系统相比，所提出的框架将平均传输延迟降低了27.8%，测试精度提高了约12%。此外，与标准基准路由算法相比，所提出的路由方法将精度提高了约8%。

Conclusion: 该研究成功证明了通过联合优化路由和剪枝策略可以有效缓解去中心化联邦学习中的通信瓶颈问题。所提出的框架不仅在降低通信延迟方面表现优异，还显著提升了模型性能，为D-FL系统的实际部署提供了有效的解决方案。研究揭示了模型保留率的路径依赖特性，为未来D-FL系统的通信优化研究提供了新的理论基础和实践指导。

Abstract: Decentralized federated learning (D-FL) enables privacy-preserving training without a central server, but multi-hop model exchanges and aggregation are often bottlenecked by communication resource constraints. To address this issue, we propose a joint routing-and-pruning framework that optimizes routing paths and pruning rates to maintain communication latency within prescribed limits. We analyze how the sum of model biases across all clients affects the convergence bound of D-FL and formulate an optimization problem that maximizes the model retention rate to minimize these biases under communication constraints. Further analysis reveals that each client's model retention rate is path-dependent, which reduces the original problem to a routing optimization. Leveraging this insight, we develop a routing algorithm that selects latency-efficient transmission paths, allowing more parameters to be delivered within the time budget and thereby improving D-FL convergence. Simulations demonstrate that, compared with unpruned systems, the proposed framework reduces average transmission latency by 27.8% and improves testing accuracy by approximately 12%. Furthermore, relative to standard benchmark routing algorithms, the proposed routing method improves accuracy by roughly 8%.

### [30] [CAMEL-CLIP: Channel-aware Multimodal Electroencephalography-text Alignment for Generalizable Brain Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13272)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的脑电图(EEG)基础模型在学习可泛化表示方面展现出潜力，但它们对通道异构性(如通道组成或顺序的变化)仍然非常敏感，这限制了模型在不同下游任务中的广泛应用。

Method: 提出了CAMEL-CLIP对比式EEG-文本多模态基础模型，包含三个核心组件：(1)基于通道属性的位置编码，通过语义信息识别通道；(2)动态通道投影，独立投影每个通道生成可变长度嵌入，避免特征压缩；(3)双层级对比学习，联合执行通道级和样本级对比学习，捕获通道特异性和全局信号特征。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) foundation models have shown promise for learning generalizable representations, yet they remain sensitive to channel heterogeneity, such as changes in channel composition or ordering. CAMEL-CLIP introduces three key components: (1) channel attribute-based positional encoding, which identifies channels through semantic information; (2) dynamic channel projection, which generates variable-length embeddings by independently projecting each channel without feature compression; and (3) dual-level contrastive learning, which jointly performs channel-level and sample-level contrastive learning to capture both channel-specific and global signal characteristics. Experimental results demonstrate that CAMEL-CLIP achieves state-of-the-art performance under linear-probing and outperforms existing foundation models that rely on full-finetuning.

### [31] [EARCP: Self-Regulating Coherence-Aware Ensemble Architecture for Sequential Decision Making -- Ensemble Auto-Regule par Coherence et Performance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14651)
*Mike Amega*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了EARCP，一种新颖的集成学习架构，通过在线学习机制动态权衡异构专家模型，同时考虑个体性能与模型间的一致性，并在理论和实验上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的集成学习方法通常依赖静态或离线学习的组合策略，难以适应非平稳环境中时间依赖性强的任务。作者旨在设计一种能够在线动态调整模型权重、兼顾高性能与共识信号的通用框架。

Method: EARCP框架结合了乘法权重更新算法的理论基础与基于一致性的正则化项，设计了一种在线学习机制。该机制在利用高性能模型（开发）与由共识信号引导的探索之间实现平衡，并为异构专家模型动态分配权重。

Result: 作者在标准假设下证明了该框架具有O(sqrt(T log M))的次线性遗憾界，提供了理论保证。在时间序列预测、活动识别和金融预测等序列预测任务上的实证评估证明了其有效性。

Conclusion: EARCP作为一个通用框架，适用于任何具有时间依赖性的集成学习场景，同时提供了开源实现，具有良好的理论与实践价值。

Abstract: We present EARCP (Ensemble Auto-Régulé par Cohérence et Performance), a novel ensemble architecture that dynamically weights heterogeneous expert models based on both their individual performance and inter-model coherence. Unlike traditional ensemble methods that rely on static or offline-learned combinations, EARCP continuously adapts model weights through a principled online learning mechanism that balances exploitation of high-performing models with exploration guided by consensus signals. The architecture combines theoretical foundations from multiplicative weight update algorithms with a novel coherence-based regularization term, providing both theoretical guarantees through regret bounds and practical robustness in non-stationary environments. We formalize the EARCP framework, prove sublinear regret bounds of O(sqrt(T log M)) under standard assumptions, and demonstrate its effectiveness through empirical evaluation on sequential prediction tasks including time series forecasting, activity recognition, and financial prediction. The architecture is designed as a general-purpose framework applicable to any domain requiring ensemble learning with temporal dependencies. An open-source implementation is available at https://github.com/Volgat/earcp and via PyPI (pip install earcp).

</details>


### [32] [Spatially Aware Deep Learning for Microclimate Prediction from High-Resolution Geospatial Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13273)
*Idan Sulami,Alon Itzkovitch,Michael R. Kearney,Moni Shahar,Ofir Levy*

Method: 基于卷积神经网络原理设计任务特定的深度神经网络，训练一系列模型并系统改变输入数据的空间范围。利用无人机获取的空间图层和气象数据预测目标位置的地面温度，直接评估预测精度随空间背景扩大的变化。

Abstract: Microclimate models are essential for linking climate to ecological processes, yet most physically based frameworks estimate temperature independently for each spatial unit and rely on simplified representations of lateral heat exchange. As a result, the spatial scales over which surrounding environmental conditions influence local microclimates remain poorly quantified. Here, we show how remote sensing can help quantify the contribution of spatial context to microclimate temperature predictions. Building on convolutional neural network principles, we designed a task-specific deep neural network and trained a series of models in which the spatial extent of input data was systematically varied. Drone-derived spatial layers and meteorological data were used to predict ground temperature at a focal location, allowing direct assessment of how prediction accuracy changes with increasing spatial context. Our results show that incorporating spatially adjacent information substantially improves prediction accuracy, with diminishing returns beyond spatial extents of approximately 5-7 m. This characteristic scale indicates that ground temperatures are influenced not only by local surface properties, but also by horizontal heat transfer and radiative interactions operating across neighboring microhabitats. The magnitude of spatial effects varied systematically with time of day, microhabitat type, and local environmental characteristics, highlighting context-dependent spatial coupling in microclimate formation. By treating deep learning as a diagnostic tool rather than solely a predictive one, our approach provides a general and transferable method for quantifying spatial dependencies in microclimate models and informing the development of hybrid mechanistic-data-driven approaches that explicitly account for spatial interactions while retaining physical interpretability.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于局部特征的深度学习模型在密集欧几里得图中表现良好，但在稀疏网络中泛化能力较差，因为拓扑不规则性需要更广泛的结构感知能力。

Method: 提出级联混合专家模型(Ca-MoE)，采用双层模块化架构：底层专家依赖局部特征，上层专家依赖全局特征。实现自适应推理机制，仅在底层专家决策质量不足时触发上层专家。引入在线元学习策略，支持独立专家微调并采用稳定性更新机制防止灾难性遗忘。

Result: 在稀疏网络中，Ca-MoE路由相比单专家基线准确率提升高达29.1%；在不同图密度下，性能保持在理論上界的1%-6%范围内。

Conclusion: Ca-MoE通过分层专家架构和自适应推理机制，成功解决了稀疏网络中的路由泛化问题，在保持计算效率的同时实现了接近理论最优的性能表现。

Abstract: While deep learning models that leverage local features have demonstrated significant potential for near-optimal routing in dense Euclidean graphs, they struggle to generalize well in sparse networks where topological irregularities require broader structural awareness. To address this limitation, we train a Cascaded Mixture of Experts (Ca-MoE) to solve the all-pairs near-shortest path (APNSP) routing problem. Our Ca-MoE is a modular two-tier architecture that supports the decision-making for forwarder selection with lower-tier experts relying on local features and upper-tier experts relying on global features. It performs adaptive inference wherein the upper-tier experts are triggered only when the lower-tier ones do not suffice to achieve adequate decision quality. Computational efficiency is thus achieved by escalating model capacity only when necessitated by topological complexity, and parameter redundancy is avoided. Furthermore, we incorporate an online meta-learning strategy that facilitates independent expert fine-tuning and utilizes a stability-focused update mechanism to prevent catastrophic forgetting as new graph environments are encountered. Experimental evaluations demonstrate that Ca-MoE routing improves accuracy by up to 29.1% in sparse networks compared to single-expert baselines and maintains performance within 1%-6% of the theoretical upper bound across diverse graph densities.

### [34] [Sample-Efficient Hypergradient Estimation for Decentralized Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14867)
*Mikoto Kudo,Takumi Tanabe,Akifumi Wachi,Youhei Akimoto*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Boltzmann协方差技巧的双层强化学习超梯度优化方法，首次实现了在分散式设置下对双人马尔可夫博弈的超梯度优化，能够在领导者无法干预跟随者优化过程的情况下，仅从交互样本中高效估计超梯度，适用于高维决策空间。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 推导了领导者目标的超梯度（考虑跟随者最优策略变化的策略梯度）；提出基于Boltzmann协方差技巧的替代超梯度公式；该方法避免了现有方法需要大量重复状态访问数据或在高维领导者决策空间下复杂度急剧增加的问题，仅从交互样本即可高效估计超梯度。

Result: 成功实现了分散式设置下双人马尔可夫博弈的超梯度优化（据作者所知为首次）；实验证明了超梯度更新的影响；方法在离散和连续状态任务中均表现出有效性；能够处理高维领导者决策空间。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法有效解决了分散式双层强化学习中超梯度估计的挑战，为领导者无法干预跟随者优化过程的场景提供了实用的优化方案，扩展了超梯度方法在双人马尔可夫博弈中的应用范围。

Abstract: Many strategic decision-making problems, such as environment design for warehouse robots, can be naturally formulated as bi-level reinforcement learning (RL), where a leader agent optimizes its objective while a follower solves a Markov decision process (MDP) conditioned on the leader's decisions. In many situations, a fundamental challenge arises when the leader cannot intervene in the follower's optimization process; it can only observe the optimization outcome. We address this decentralized setting by deriving the hypergradient of the leader's objective, i.e., the gradient of the leader's strategy that accounts for changes in the follower's optimal policy. Unlike prior hypergradient-based methods that require extensive data for repeated state visits or rely on gradient estimators whose complexity can increase substantially with the high-dimensional leader's decision space, we leverage the Boltzmann covariance trick to derive an alternative hypergradient formulation. This enables efficient hypergradient estimation solely from interaction samples, even when the leader's decision space is high-dimensional. Additionally, to our knowledge, this is the first method that enables hypergradient-based optimization for 2-player Markov games in decentralized settings. Experiments highlight the impact of hypergradient updates and demonstrate our method's effectiveness in both discrete and continuous state tasks.

*Gianluigi Silvestri,Edoardo Cetin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向推理的语言模型在推理时生成长思维链可获得强大性能，但带来巨大且通常过度的计算成本，表现为冗余或低效的推理过程。

Method: 提出截断推理自蒸馏(TRSD)：冻结的教师模型生成完整推理轨迹并构建答案分布作为合成训练目标；学生模型在仅看到截断的推理前缀条件下，被训练匹配教师的答案分布。

Result: 在多个推理基准和token预算下，TRSD显著提升了对截断推理的鲁棒性，大幅降低准确率损失；且未显式正则化短生成，训练后的模型天然输出更短的推理轨迹，显著降低推理成本。

Abstract: Reasoning-oriented language models achieve strong performance by generating long chain-of-thought traces at inference time. However, this capability comes with substantial and often excessive computational cost, which can materialize in redundant or inefficient reasoning. We study this setting and introduce Truncated-Reasoning Self-Distillation (TRSD), a lightweight post-training procedure that encourages models to produce correct predictions from partial reasoning traces. In TRSD, a frozen teacher model first generates a full reasoning trace and evaluates the corresponding answer distribution conditioned on the prompt and the complete reasoning to construct a synthetic training target. A student model with the same architecture is then trained to match the teacher's answer distribution while being conditioned only on a truncated prefix of its reasoning trace. Across multiple reasoning benchmarks and token budgets, we demonstrate that TRSD improves robustness to truncated inference, with far reduced accuracy tradeoffs when applied to a diverse set of reasoning models. Moreover, although never explicitly regularized for shorter generation during training, we also find that TRSD-trained models inherently output shorter reasoning traces without truncation, significantly reducing inference-time costs even without artificial interventions.

In contrast, zero-shot LLM inference offers a promising training-free alternative but it lacks grounding in institution-specific clinical context (e.g., local demographics and case-mix distributions), making its predictions clinically misaligned and prone to instability. To address these limitations, we present PREBA, a retrieval-augmented framework that integrates PCA-weighted retrieval and Bayesian averaging aggregation to ground LLM predictions in institution-specific clinical evidence and statistical priors. The core of PREBA is to construct an evidence-based prompt for the LLM, comprising (1) the most clinically similar historical surgical cases and (2) clinical statistical priors. To achieve this, PREBA first encodes heterogeneous clinical features into a unified representation space enabling systematic retrieval. It then performs PCA-weighted retrieval to identify clinically relevant historical cases, which form the evidence context supplied to the LLM. Finally, PREBA applies Bayesian averaging to fuse multi-round LLM predictions with population-level statistical priors, yielding calibrated and clinically plausible duration estimates. We evaluate PREBA on two real-world clinical datasets using three state-of-the-art LLMs, including Qwen3, DeepSeek-R1, and HuatuoGPT-o1. ### [39] [RESQ: A Unified Framework for REliability- and Security Enhancement of Quantized Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15413)
*Ali Soltan Mohammadi,Samira Nazari,Ali Azarpeyvand,Mahdi Taheri,Milos Krstic,Michael Huebner,Christian Herglotz,Tara Ghasempouri*

Method: 提出三阶段统一框架：（1）通过微调使特征表示对小输入扰动不敏感，提升对抗攻击鲁棒性；（2）在模拟位翻转故障下进行故障感知微调，增强故障鲁棒性；（3）轻量级训练后调整引入量化以提升效率并进一步缓解故障敏感性，同时不损害对抗鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该框架成功实现了量化DNN中故障鲁棒性与对抗攻击鲁棒性的平衡优化，揭示了两者间的不对称相互作用关系，为设计更鲁棒的量化神经网络提供了新的见解和方法。

Abstract: This work proposes a unified three-stage framework that produces a quantized DNN with balanced fault and attack robustness. The first stage improves attack resilience via fine-tuning that desensitizes feature representations to small input perturbations. The second stage reinforces fault resilience through fault-aware fine-tuning under simulated bit-flip faults. Finally, a lightweight post-training adjustment integrates quantization to enhance efficiency and further mitigate fault sensitivity without degrading attack resilience. Experiments on ResNet18, VGG16, EfficientNet, and Swin-Tiny in CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and GTSRB show consistent gains of up to 10.35% in attack resilience and 12.47% in fault resilience, while maintaining competitive accuracy in quantized networks. The results also highlight an asymmetric interaction in which improvements in fault resilience generally increase resilience to adversarial attacks, whereas enhanced adversarial resilience does not necessarily lead to higher fault resilience.

### [40] [FedPBS: Proximal-Balanced Scaling Federated Learning Model for Robust Personalized Training for Non-IID Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13909)
*Eman M. AbouNassara,Amr Elshalla,Sameh Abdulah*

TL;DR: 本文提出了FedPBS算法，通过结合FedBS和FedProx的优势，采用动态批次大小适配和选择性近端校正策略，有效解决了联邦学习中的统计异质性和客户端参与不均问题，在高度非独立同分布环境下显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习在医疗、金融、移动出行和智慧城市等隐私敏感领域应用前景广阔，但面临统计异质性和客户端参与不均两大关键挑战，这些问题会导致模型收敛性能下降和质量劣化，亟需有效的解决方案。

Method: 提出FedPBS算法，融合FedBS和FedProx的互补思想：(1)根据客户端资源动态调整批次大小，支持均衡且可扩展的参与；(2)对小批次客户端选择性应用近端校正项，稳定本地更新并减少与全局模型的偏差。

Result: 在CIFAR-10和UCI-HAR等基准数据集的高度非独立同分布(Non-IID)设置下，FedPBS持续优于FedBS、FedGA、MOON和FedProx等最先进方法。实验显示在极端数据异质性下具有鲁棒的性能提升，损失曲线平滑且收敛稳定。

Conclusion: FedPBS有效应对联邦学习中的统计异质性和客户端参与不均挑战，在保持稳定可靠收敛的同时，在高度非独立同分布环境下实现了优于现有最先进方法的性能，为实际联邦学习应用提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) enables a set of distributed clients to jointly train machine learning models while preserving their local data privacy, making it attractive for applications in healthcare, finance, mobility, and smart-city systems. However, FL faces several challenges, including statistical heterogeneity and uneven client participation, which can degrade convergence and model quality. In this work, we propose FedPBS, an FL algorithm that couples complementary ideas from FedBS and FedProx to address these challenges. FedPBS dynamically adapts batch sizes to client resources to support balanced and scalable participation, and selectively applies a proximal correction to small-batch clients to stabilize local updates and reduce divergence from the global model. Experiments on benchmarking datasets such as CIFAR-10 and UCI-HAR under highly non-IID settings demonstrate that FedPBS consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, including FedBS, FedGA, MOON, and FedProx. The results demonstrate robust performance gains under extreme data heterogeneity, with smooth loss curves indicating stable convergence across diverse federated environments. FedPBS consistently outperforms state-of-the-art federated learning baselines on UCI-HAR and CIFAR-10 under severe non-IID conditions while maintaining stable and reliable convergence.

SPLARE-7B, a multilingual retrieval model capable of producing generalizable sparse latent embeddings for a wide range of languages and domains, achieves top results on MMTEB's multilingual and English retrieval tasks. Our findings demonstrate the relevance of our approach for different types of inputs, even when the horizon of the problem is uncertain.
