<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 校准性是一个依赖于预测器所保留信息的条件性质，现有研究尚未显式量化这种依赖关系，因此需要建立分解框架来明确信息层级与校准性能之间的联系。

Method: 针对任意正常损失函数，推导分解恒等式：在任意信息层级A上，将A可测预测器的期望损失分解为正常遗憾（可靠性）项和条件熵（残余不确定性）项；对嵌套信息层级建立链式分解量化信息增益；应用于特征X和分数S的分类任务，得到包含失校准、分组项（信息损失）和不可约不确定性三项的恒等式。

Result: 推导出了适用于任意正常损失的分解恒等式，在分类任务中具体化为三项恒等式：失校准项、衡量从X到S信息损失的分组项、以及特征层级的不可约不确定性；给出了Brier损失和log损失的显式形式。

Conclusion: 该分解框架为事后重校准、校准模型聚合、以及分阶段/boosting构造提供了理论分析工具，能够显式量化信息流动对校准性能的影响，为理解校准性的本质提供了新视角。

Abstract: Calibration is a conditional property that depends on the information retained by a predictor. We develop decomposition identities for arbitrary proper losses that make this dependence explicit. At any information level $\mathcal A$, the expected loss of an $\mathcal A$-measurable predictor splits into a proper-regret (reliability) term and a conditional entropy (residual uncertainty) term. For nested levels $\mathcal A\subseteq\mathcal B$, a chain decomposition quantifies the information gain from $\mathcal A$ to $\mathcal B$. Applied to classification with features $\boldsymbol{X}$ and score $S=s(\boldsymbol{X})$, this yields a three-term identity: miscalibration, a {\em grouping} term measuring information loss from $\boldsymbol{X}$ to $S$, and irreducible uncertainty at the feature level. We leverage the framework to analyze post-hoc recalibration, aggregation of calibrated models, and stagewise/boosting constructions, with explicit forms for Brier and log-loss.

*Alma Lago*

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability has transformed the analysis of transformer circuits by decomposing model behavior into competing algorithms, identifying phase transitions during training, and deriving closed-form predictions for when and why strategies shift. However, this program has remained largely confined to sequence-prediction architectures, leaving embodied control systems without comparable mechanistic accounts. Here we extend this framework to sensorimotor-cognitive development, using infant motor learning as a model system. We show that foundational inductive biases give rise to causal control circuits, with learned gating mechanisms converging toward theoretically motivated uncertainty thresholds. The resulting dynamics reveal a clean phase transition in the arbitration gate whose commitment behavior is well described by a closed-form exponential moving-average surrogate. We identify context window k as the critical parameter governing circuit formation: below a minimum threshold (k$\leq$4) the arbitration mechanism cannot form; above it (k$\geq$8), gate confidence scales asymptotically as log k. A two-dimensional phase diagram further reveals task-demand-dependent route arbitration consistent with the prediction that prospective execution becomes advantageous only when prediction error remains within the task tolerance window. Together, these results provide a mechanistic account of how reactive and prospective control strategies emerge and compete during learning. More broadly, this work sharpens mechanistic accounts of cognitive development and provides principled guidance for the design of interpretable embodied agents.

### [249] [FuXiWeather2: Learning accurate atmospheric state estimation for operational global weather forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15358)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统数值天气预报在数据同化和数值建模方面长期受限于计算瓶颈。现有的机器学习模型主要充当“再分析产品的模拟器”，因此继承了其系统性偏差，且未能解决训练与部署阶段背景场输入分布偏移的问题，导致业务延迟依然存在。

Method: 1. 提出FuXiWeather2统一端到端神经框架，将训练目标直接与真实观测及再分析数据的组合对齐，以纠正再分析产品的固有误差。\n2. 引入递归展开训练方法，解决训练时NWP背景输入与部署时自生成背景之间的分布偏移，提升分析场生成的精度与稳定性。\n3. 使用原始观测与模拟观测的混合数据集进行训练，缓解观测分布不一致的影响。

Result: 1. FuXiWeather2能在数分钟内生成0.25°高分辨率全球分析场和10天预报。\n2. 分析场在大部分变量上优于NCEP-GFS，在对流层低层和地面变量上精度优于ERA5和ECMWF-HRES系统。\n3. 高质量分析场驱动的确定性预报在91%的评估指标上超越了HRES系统的预报技巧。\n4. 在台风路径预测方面表现卓越，证明了其对极端天气事件快速响应的实用价值。

Conclusion: FuXiWeather2成功构建了一个融合数据同化与预报的统一端到端框架，有效克服了传统数值模式与现有ML模型的局限性。其在预报精度、计算效率及极端天气事件应对方面的显著优势，展示了其作为新一代气象业务系统的巨大潜力与实用价值。

Abstract: Numerical weather prediction has long been constrained by the computational bottlenecks inherent in data assimilation and numerical modeling. While machine learning has accelerated forecasting, existing models largely serve as "emulators of reanalysis products," thereby retaining their systematic biases and operational latencies. Here, we present FuXiWeather2, a unified end-to-end neural framework for assimilation and forecasting. We align training objectives directly with a combination of real-world observations and reanalysis data, enabling the framework to effectively rectify inherent errors within reanalysis products. To address the distribution shift between NWP-derived background inputs during training and self-generated backgrounds during deployment, we introduce a recursive unrolling training method to enhance the precision and stability of analysis generation. Furthermore, our model is trained on a hybrid dataset of raw and simulated observations to mitigate the impact of observational distribution inconsistency. FuXiWeather2 generates high-resolution ($0.25^{\circ}$) global analysis fields and 10-day forecasts within minutes. The analysis fields surpass the NCEP-GFS across most variables and demonstrate superior accuracy over both ERA5 and the ECMWF-HRES system in lower-tropospheric and surface variables. These high-quality analysis fields drive deterministic forecasts that exceed the skill of the HRES system in 91\% of evaluated metrics. Additionally, its outstanding performance in typhoon track prediction underscores its practical value for rapid response to extreme weather events. The FuXiWeather2 analysis dataset is available at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.18872728.

### [251] [More Test-Time Compute Can Hurt: Overestimation Bias in LLM Beam Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15377)
*Gal Dalal,Assaf Hallak,Gal Chechik,Yftach Ziser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究发现扩大束搜索宽度并不总是有益的：基于极值理论分析，提出存在一个临界宽度阈值$\hat{k}$，超过该值后搜索性能会下降。该阈值由评分器的信噪比决定，呈指数关系。实验验证了在PRM引导下最优宽度≥4，而困惑度引导下最优宽度仅为1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有束搜索宽度选择研究主要关注推理效率，未分析扩大搜索宽度是否会损害输出质量。研究者希望解决“何时应该停止扩大束搜索宽度”这一关键问题。

Method: 基于极值理论(EVT)建立理论分析框架，推导出最大有效束宽度$\hat{k}$的计算公式：$\hat{k}$与评分器信噪比$(Δ/σ)^2$呈指数增长关系，其中$Δ$为正确路径相对错误路径的质量优势，$σ$为评分器噪声。通过在三个7B参数模型和MR-BEN数据集的10个领域上比较困惑度引导和PRM引导的束搜索进行实验验证。

Result: 理论预测得到实验验证：(1)困惑度评分具有高噪声，导致$\hat{k}=1$，任何宽度下的搜索均无益处；(2)PRM评分噪声较低，$\hat{k}≥4$，性能提升最高达8.9个百分点；(3)相同模型和算法配合不同评分器，最优宽度位于束宽度范围的两端。

Conclusion: 评分器的信噪比是决定束搜索宽度的关键因素，信噪比越高则可使用的有效束宽度越大。研究提出了在实践中选择束宽度的诊断指标，为LLM推理中的搜索策略优化提供了理论依据和实践指导。

Abstract: Wider beam search should improve LLM reasoning, but when should you stop widening? Prior work on beam width selection has focused on inference efficiency \citep{qin2025dsbd, freitag2017beam}, without analyzing whether wider search can \emph{hurt} output quality. We present an analysis, grounded in Extreme Value Theory, that answers this question. Beam selection over noisy scorer outputs introduces a systematic overestimation bias that grows with the candidate pool size, and we derive a maximum useful beam width $\hat{k}$ beyond which search degrades performance. This critical width depends on the signal-to-noise ratio of the scorer: $\hat{k}$ grows exponentially with $(Δ/σ)^2$, where $Δ> 0$ is the quality advantage of correct paths over incorrect ones and $σ$ is the scorer noise. We validate this theory by comparing perplexity-guided and PRM-guided beam search across three 7B-parameter models and ten domains on MR-BEN (5,975 questions). Perplexity scoring, with its high noise, yields $\hat{k} = 1$: search provides no benefit at any width tested. PRM scoring, with lower noise, yields $\hat{k} \geq 4$, with gains of up to 8.9 percentage points. The same model, the same algorithm, but different scorers place $\hat{k}$ at opposite ends of the beam width range. Our analysis identifies the scorer's signal-to-noise ratio as the key quantity governing beam width selection, and we propose diagnostic indicators for choosing the beam width in practice.

</details>

A recent approach uses minibatch optimal transport (OT) to reassign noise-data pairs in each training step to streamline sampling trajectories and thus accelerate inference. To address this shortcoming, we introduce LOOM-CFM (Looking Out Of Minibatch-CFM), a novel method to extend the scope of minibatch OT by preserving and optimizing these assignments across minibatches over training time. Method: 从博弈论视角重新审视协同设计问题，将形态与控制之间的内在耦合建模为Stackelberg博弈的新变体。提出Stackelberg Proximal Policy Optimization（Stackelberg PPO）算法，在形态优化过程中显式纳入控制的自适应动态，使形态更新与控制自适应相协调。

Abstract: Morphology-control co-design concerns the coupled optimization of an agent's body structure and control policy. This problem exhibits a bi-level structure, where the control dynamically adapts to the morphology to maximize performance. Existing methods typically neglect the control's adaptation dynamics by adopting a single-level formulation that treats the control policy as fixed when optimizing morphology. This can lead to inefficient optimization, as morphology updates may be misaligned with control adaptation. In this paper, we revisit the co-design problem from a game-theoretic perspective, modeling the intrinsic coupling between morphology and control as a novel variant of a Stackelberg game. We propose Stackelberg Proximal Policy Optimization (Stackelberg PPO), which explicitly incorporates the control's adaptation dynamics into morphology optimization. By modeling this intrinsic coupling, our method aligns morphology updates with control adaptation, thereby stabilizing training and improving learning efficiency. Experiments across diverse co-design tasks demonstrate that Stackelberg PPO outperforms standard PPO in both stability and final performance, opening the way for dramatically more efficient robotics designs.

*Panos Stinis*

Method: 将待分类数据视为向量，首先将其提升到更高维空间，然后作为初始条件让混沌动力系统在规定时间区间内演化。演化后的状态被输入到一个可训练的softmax分类器中，输出各类别的概率。

Result: 在随机扰动的正交向量样本（维度为2到20）上进行的概念验证实验表明，与传统softmax分类器以及仅提升维度但不进行演化的分类器相比，该方法能够显著加速训练过程并提高分类准确率。同时，论文还对混沌增强分类器的性能提升给出了理论解释。

Abstract: We propose a novel approach which exploits chaos to enhance classification accuracy. Specifically, the available data that need to be classified are treated as vectors that are first lifted into a higher-dimensional space and then used as initial conditions for the evolution of a chaotic dynamical system for a prescribed temporal interval. The evolved state of the dynamical system is then fed to a trainable softmax classifier which outputs the probabilities of the various classes. As proof-of-concept, we use samples of randomly perturbed orthogonal vectors of moderate dimension (2 to 20), with a corresponding number of classes equal to the vector dimension, and show how our approach can both significantly accelerate the training process and improve the classification accuracy compared to a standard softmax classifier which operates on the original vectors, as well as a softmax classifier which only lifts the vectors to a higher-dimensional space without evolving them. We also provide an explanation for the improved performance of the chaos-enhanced classifier.

### [256] [Amplification Effects in Test-Time Reinforcement Learning: Safety and Reasoning Vulnerabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15417)
*Vanshaj Khattar,Md Rafi ur Rashid,Moumita Choudhury,Jing Liu,Toshiaki Koike-Akino,Ming Jin,Ye Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了测试时训练（TTT）方法存在安全漏洞，发现有害提示注入会导致模型行为放大（安全性或有害性放大）并伴随推理能力下降（推理税），且可被对抗性利用以增强有害性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时训练（TTT）通过直接从测试数据学习来提升大语言模型的推理能力，但这种对测试数据的依赖使其容易受到有害提示注入的攻击。目前缺乏对TTT方法安全性的系统研究，需要深入了解其潜在的安全漏洞。

Method: 以代表性的测试时强化学习（TTRL）方法为研究对象，该方法是 一种基于自一致性的测试时学习方法，通过将多数投票作为奖励信号来提升LLM推理能力。研究者通过注入有害提示来测试TTRL的安全性，并设计了"HarmInject"提示进行对抗性攻击实验。

Result: 实验发现TTRL中的有害提示注入会放大模型的现有行为：当基础模型相对安全时会出现安全性放大，当模型易受注入数据影响时会出现有害性放大。在两种情况下都会导致推理能力下降（称为"推理税"）。使用"HarmInject"提示可以强制模型同时回答越狱和推理查询，导致更强的有害性放大。

Conclusion: 通过促进自一致性来增强LLM推理的TTT方法会导致行为放大和推理退化，凸显了开发更安全的TTT方法的必要性。研究结果强调了在设计TTT方法时必须考虑安全性问题，以防止潜在的对抗性利用。

Abstract: Test-time training (TTT) has recently emerged as a promising method to improve the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), in which the model directly learns from test data without access to labels. However, this reliance on test data also makes TTT methods vulnerable to harmful prompt injections. In this paper, we investigate safety vulnerabilities of TTT methods, where we study a representative self-consistency-based test-time learning method: test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL), a recent TTT method that improves LLM reasoning by rewarding self-consistency using majority vote as a reward signal. We show that harmful prompt injection during TTRL amplifies the model's existing behaviors, i.e., safety amplification when the base model is relatively safe, and harmfulness amplification when it is vulnerable to the injected data. In both cases, there is a decline in reasoning ability, which we refer to as the reasoning tax. We also show that TTT methods such as TTRL can be exploited adversarially using specially designed "HarmInject" prompts to force the model to answer jailbreak and reasoning queries together, resulting in stronger harmfulness amplification. Overall, our results highlight that TTT methods that enhance LLM reasoning by promoting self-consistency can lead to amplification behaviors and reasoning degradation, highlighting the need for safer TTT methods.

Motivation: 尽管R中存在多种特征重要性方法，但在条件重要性方法和相关统计推断程序方面仍存在显著空白。现有的工具缺乏对条件重要性的全面支持，特别是在处理连续和混合数据时的条件采样架构和统计推断能力不足。

Method: 开发了一个名为xplainfi的R包，实现了置换特征重要性、条件特征重要性、相对特征重要性、留一协变量法及其推广形式，以及边际和条件Shapley加性全局重要性方法。采用模块化条件采样架构，支持基于高斯分布、对抗随机森林、条件推断树和knockoff采样器。统计推断通过多种方法实现，包括方差校正置信区间和条件预测影响框架。

Result: 实验证明xplainfi在多种仿真设置和学习器类型下产生的重要性得分与现有实现一致，同时具有竞争力的运行时性能。该包已在CRAN上发布，为研究人员和从业者提供了全面的特征重要性分析和模型解释工具。

Conclusion: xplainfi成功填补了R语言在条件特征重要性方法和统计推断程序方面的空白，为机器学习模型的特征重要性分析提供了全面、模块化且高效的解决方案，具有重要的实践应用价值。

Abstract: We introduce xplainfi, an R package built on top of the mlr3 ecosystem for global, loss-based feature importance methods for machine learning models. Various feature importance methods exist in R, but significant gaps remain, particularly regarding conditional importance methods and associated statistical inference procedures. The package implements permutation feature importance, conditional feature importance, relative feature importance, leave-one-covariate-out, and generalizations thereof, and both marginal and conditional Shapley additive global importance methods. It provides a modular conditional sampling architecture based on Gaussian distributions, adversarial random forests, conditional inference trees, and knockoff-based samplers, which enable conditional importance analysis for continuous and mixed data. Statistical inference is available through multiple approaches, including variance-corrected confidence intervals and the conditional predictive impact framework. We demonstrate that xplainfi produces importance scores consistent with existing implementations across multiple simulation settings and learner types, while offering competitive runtime performance. The package is available on CRAN and provides researchers and practitioners with a comprehensive toolkit for feature importance analysis and model interpretation in R.

Abstract: Foundation models for partial differential equations (PDEs) have emerged as powerful surrogates pre-trained on diverse physical systems, but adapting them to new downstream tasks remains challenging due to limited task-specific data and distribution shifts. In this work, we introduce a physics-informed fine-tuning framework that adapts pre-trained PDE foundation models by incorporating physical constraints (PDE residuals and boundary conditions) directly into the fine-tuning objective. This enables effective adaptation in data-scarce regimes while promoting physical consistency. We evaluate our method on a downstream task composed of an unseen PDE class and compare it with data-driven finetuning counterparts. Our results demonstrate that physics-informed fine-tuning achieves competitive accuracy without requiring PDE solutions for training. Furthermore, a hybrid fine-tuning strategy yields superior generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios when only minimal training data is available. These findings establish physics-informed fine-tuning as a scalable and data-efficient paradigm, providing a physically interpretable pathway for adapting foundation models in scientific machine learning.

  <summary>Details</summary>

In particular, multilayer perceptrons are widely employed due to their ability to recognize nonlinear relationships. This is the first step toward employing surrogate models to speed up reactive transport simulations and optimize the safety assessment of deep geological waste repositories.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Rashomon集（性能接近参考模型的模型集合）的高效构建方法仅适用于少数模型类，而实际机器学习通常会搜索多个模型类且最佳模型类未知。研究旨在解决CASH设置下Rashomon集（即CASHomon集）的构建问题，使用户能够选择符合领域知识、隐藏约束或用户偏好的模型。

Method: 提出CASHomon集概念，将其定义在CASH设置下的Rashomon集；开发TruVaRImp算法——一种基于模型的主动学习方法，用于具有隐式阈值的水平集估计，并提供收敛性保证。该算法能够高效识别CASHomon集成员。

Result: 在合成数据集和真实数据集上，TruVaRImp可靠地识别CASHomon集成员，性能匹配或优于朴素采样、贝叶斯优化、经典和隐式水平集估计方法及其他基线方法。跨模型类的预测多重性和特征重要性变异性分析表明，通过单一模型类解释数据的常见做法存在问题。

Conclusion: CASHomon集为在多模型类场景下选择符合用户需求的模型提供了新途径；TruVaRImp算法能够高效构建此类模型集；跨模型类的分析揭示了单一模型类解释数据的局限性，强调了考虑模型类多样性的重要性。

Abstract: Rashomon sets are model sets within one model class that perform nearly as well as a reference model from the same model class. They reveal the existence of alternative well-performing models, which may support different interpretations. This enables selecting models that match domain knowledge, hidden constraints, or user preferences. However, efficient construction methods currently exist for only a few model classes. Applied machine learning usually searches many model classes, and the best class is unknown beforehand. We therefore study Rashomon sets in the combined algorithm selection and hyperparameter optimization (CASH) setting and call them CASHomon sets. We propose TruVaRImp, a model-based active learning algorithm for level set estimation with an implicit threshold, and provide convergence guarantees. On synthetic and real-world datasets, TruVaRImp reliably identifies CASHomon sets members and matches or outperforms naive sampling, Bayesian optimization, classical and implicit level set estimation methods, and other baselines. Our analyses of predictive multiplicity and feature-importance variability across model classes question the common practice of interpreting data through a single model class.

### [262] [Grokking as a Variance-Limited Phase Transition: Spectral Gating and the Epsilon-Stability Threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15492)
*Pratyush Acharya,Habish Dhakal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了AdamW优化器通过“谱门控”机制调控从记忆到泛化的转变。泛化解位于尖锐盆地，需要累积梯度方差来突破稳定性限制，从而解释了grokking的延迟现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准优化理论难以解释grokking现象（训练收敛后很长时间才出现泛化）。现有几何研究将其归因于缓慢漂移，但往往忽视了优化器噪声结构与景观曲率之间的相互作用。

Method: 分析AdamW在模算术任务上的动力学行为，提出“谱门控”机制。将AdamW建模为方差门控的随机系统，研究稳定性条件、梯度方差累积与进入尖锐流形的关系。通过消融实验识别三种复杂度机制，并测试各向同性噪声注入与自适应优化器的各向异性校正效果。

Result: 发现泛化解位于尖锐盆地（由最大Hessian特征值λ_max^H刻画），在低方差状态下不可达。延迟阶段代表梯度方差累积以提升有效稳定性上限。识别出三种机制：(1)容量崩溃（P<23）：秩亏阻止结构学习；(2)方差受限机制（P≈41）：等待谱门开启；(3)稳定性覆盖（P>67）：记忆在维度上不稳定。各向同性噪声注入无法诱导grokking，泛化需要自适应优化器独特的各向异性校正。

Conclusion: grokking延迟是方差受限的系统特征。AdamW的各向异性噪声校正引导噪声进入解流形的切空间，这是实现泛化的关键。挑战了算法任务中的“平坦极小值”假说，揭示了自适应优化器噪声结构的重要性。

Abstract: Standard optimization theories struggle to explain grokking, where generalization occurs long after training convergence. While geometric studies attribute this to slow drift, they often overlook the interaction between the optimizer's noise structure and landscape curvature. This work analyzes AdamW dynamics on modular arithmetic tasks, revealing a ``Spectral Gating'' mechanism that regulates the transition from memorization to generalization.
  We find that AdamW operates as a variance-gated stochastic system. Grokking is constrained by a stability condition: the generalizing solution resides in a sharp basin ($λ_{max}^H$) initially inaccessible under low-variance regimes. The ``delayed'' phase represents the accumulation of gradient variance required to lift the effective stability ceiling, permitting entry into this sharp manifold.
  Our ablation studies identify three complexity regimes: (1) \textbf{Capacity Collapse} ($P < 23$), where rank-deficiency prevents structural learning; (2) \textbf{The Variance-Limited Regime} ($P \approx 41$), where generalization waits for the spectral gate to open; and (3) \textbf{Stability Override} ($P > 67$), where memorization becomes dimensionally unstable. Furthermore, we challenge the "Flat Minima" hypothesis for algorithmic tasks, showing that isotropic noise injection fails to induce grokking. Generalization requires the \textit{anisotropic rectification} unique to adaptive optimizers, which directs noise into the tangent space of the solution manifold.

### [264] [Seeking SOTA: Time-Series Forecasting Must Adopt Taxonomy-Specific Evaluation to Dispel Illusory Gains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15506)
*Raeid Saqur,Christoph Bergmeir,Blanka Horvath,Daniel Schmidt,Frank Rudzicz,Terry Lyons*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文批判了当前时序预测基准测试过度依赖强周期性数据的现象，揭示了复杂深度学习模型在此类数据上相比经典方法并无显著优势，呼吁社区改革评估标准并强制纳入经典方法作为基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前时序预测评估实践存在严重缺陷：主流基准数据集普遍具有强持续周期性和季节性特征，这种选择偏差掩盖了真实进展，使人们难以判断深度学习模型相对于经典方法是否具有真正的性能优势。

Method: （1）分析标准基准数据集的自相关模式和季节周期特征，揭示其主导性规律；（2）对比简单线性/统计模型与复杂深度学习架构在这些特定数据特征上的性能表现；（3）评估边际性能提升是否足以证明计算开销和模型复杂度增加的合理性。

Result: 实验证明：（1）标准数据集存在主导性自相关模式和季节周期；（2）简单线性或统计模型即可有效捕获这些模式；（3）复杂深度学习架构在特定数据特征上并不比经典方法更优，边际改进往往无法证明其高昂的计算成本和复杂度的合理性。

Conclusion: 呼吁社区采取两项行动：（I）淘汰或大幅改进现有基准，纳入更多非平稳性数据（如结构性断点、时变波动性、概念漂移）及来自多样真实领域的不易预测动态；（II）要求所有深度学习论文必须包含针对下游任务时序特征适当选择的经典和简单基线，确保报告的提升反映真正的科学进步而非基准选择的人为优势。

Abstract: We argue that the current practice of evaluating AI/ML time-series forecasting models, predominantly on benchmarks characterized by strong, persistent periodicities and seasonalities, obscures real progress by overlooking the performance of efficient classical methods. We demonstrate that these "standard" datasets often exhibit dominant autocorrelation patterns and seasonal cycles that can be effectively captured by simpler linear or statistical models, rendering complex deep learning architectures frequently no more performant than their classical counterparts for these specific data characteristics, and raising questions as to whether any marginal improvements justify the significant increase in computational overhead and model complexity. We call on the community to (I) retire or substantially augment current benchmarks with datasets exhibiting a wider spectrum of non-stationarities, such as structural breaks, time-varying volatility, and concept drift, and less predictable dynamics drawn from diverse real-world domains, and (II) require every deep learning submission to include robust classical and simple baselines, appropriately chosen for the specific characteristics of the downstream tasks' time series. By doing so, we will help ensure that reported gains reflect genuine scientific methodological advances rather than artifacts of benchmark selection favoring models adept at learning repetitive patterns.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PINN作为求解偏微分方程的灵活深度学习方法，存在一个关键局限：缺乏对预测值与真实解偏差的洞察，阻碍了对其预测质量的信任评估。现有方法无法提供关于预测错误位置及程度的可解释性信息。

Method: 针对线性偏微分方程，发现PINN近似与真实解之间的误差满足与原问题相同的微分算子，但以PINN的PDE残差作为源项驱动。基于此理论发现，采用有限差分方法数值求解该误差方程，整个过程无需真实解的先验知识，仅利用PINN的残差信息。

Result: 在多个基准偏微分方程问题上的实验表明，该方法能够以较低的计算成本生成准确的误差分布图，有效识别预测错误的精确位置和程度。

Conclusion: 该方法成功填补了PINN可解释性验证的空白，实现了对PINN预测的目标化和可解释性验证，为建立对PINN预测质量的信任提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) constitute a flexible deep learning approach for solving partial differential equations (PDEs), which model phenomena ranging from heat conduction to quantum mechanical systems. Despite their flexibility, PINNs offer limited insight into how their predictions deviate from the true solution, hindering trust in their prediction quality. We propose a lightweight post-hoc method that addresses this gap by producing pointwise error estimates for PINN predictions, which offer a natural form of explanation for such models, identifying not just whether a prediction is wrong, but where and by how much. For linear partial differential equations, the error between a PINN approximation and the true solution satisfies the same differential operator as the original problem, but driven by the PINN's PDE residual as its source term. We solve this error equation numerically using finite difference methods requiring no knowledge of the true solution. Evaluated on several benchmark PDEs, our method yields accurate error maps at low computational cost, enabling targeted and interpretable validation of PINNs.

</details>

Conclusion: PokeAgent Challenge成功提供了一个大规模、多维度的决策基准，填补了现有评估体系的空白。该基准已转型为持续运行的活基准，提供战斗赛道的在线排行榜和速通赛道的自包含评估系统，将长期服务于RL和LLM研究社区。

Abstract: We present the PokeAgent Challenge, a large-scale benchmark for decision-making research built on Pokemon's multi-agent battle system and expansive role-playing game (RPG) environment. Partial observability, game-theoretic reasoning, and long-horizon planning remain open problems for frontier AI, yet few benchmarks stress all three simultaneously under realistic conditions. PokeAgent targets these limitations at scale through two complementary tracks: our Battling Track, which calls for strategic reasoning and generalization under partial observability in competitive Pokemon battles, and our Speedrunning Track, which requires long-horizon planning and sequential decision-making in the Pokemon RPG. Our Battling Track supplies a dataset of 20M+ battle trajectories alongside a suite of heuristic, RL, and LLM-based baselines capable of high-level competitive play. Our Speedrunning Track provides the first standardized evaluation framework for RPG speedrunning, including an open-source multi-agent orchestration system for modular, reproducible comparisons of harness-based LLM approaches. Our NeurIPS 2025 competition validates both the quality of our resources and the research community's interest in Pokemon, with over 100 teams competing across both tracks and winning solutions detailed in our paper. Participant submissions and our baselines reveal considerable gaps between generalist (LLM), specialist (RL), and elite human performance. Analysis against the BenchPress evaluation matrix shows that Pokemon battling is nearly orthogonal to standard LLM benchmarks, measuring capabilities not captured by existing suites and positioning Pokemon as an unsolved benchmark that can drive RL and LLM research forward. We transition to a living benchmark with a live leaderboard for Battling and self-contained evaluation for Speedrunning at https://pokeagentchallenge.com.

### [267] [Deep learning and the rate of approximation by flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15363)
*Jingpu Cheng,Qianxiao Li,Ting Lin,Zuowei Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在连续动力系统框架下研究深度残差网络的逼近能力对其深度的依赖关系，证明逼近微分同胚所需的最小时间可识别为子Finsler流形上的测地距离，揭示了深度学习的逼近机制与线性逼近理论存在根本差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度残差网络通过残差块堆叠实现函数逼近，其逼近能力与网络深度的关系缺乏理论解释。作者希望在连续动力系统框架下量化逼近特定函数所需的最小“时间范围”（对应网络深度），以理解网络架构选择与目标函数之间的兼容性如何影响学习效率。

Method: 将深度残差网络解释为连续动力系统的离散化，把逼近问题转化为“用给定向量场族$\mathcal{F}$驱动的流在最小时间内逼近微分同胚”的问题。利用子Finsler几何理论，证明该最小时间可识别为微分同胚空间上的测地距离，其中局部几何由涉及$\mathcal{F}$的变分原理刻画。

Result: 证明了逼近微分同胚所需的最小时间等于子Finsler流形上的测地距离；该距离度量了目标函数与架构选择的“兼容性”。学习效率由目标关系与学习架构之间的兼容性决定。揭示了深度学习的逼近机制——通过组合或动力学逼近函数——与线性逼近理论存在本质差异：线性空间与范数估计被流形与测地距离取代。

Conclusion: 深度残差网络的逼近能力可由微分同胚流形上的几何结构刻画，逼近复杂度由测地距离决定而非传统线性逼近中的维数或范数。这为理解网络深度需求提供了几何视角，并表明深度学习的逼近理论需要超越线性框架的新理论工具。

Abstract: We investigate the dependence of the approximation capacity of deep residual networks on its depth in a continuous dynamical systems setting. This can be formulated as the general problem of quantifying the minimal time-horizon required to approximate a diffeomorphism by flows driven by a given family $\mathcal F$ of vector fields. We show that this minimal time can be identified as a geodesic distance on a sub-Finsler manifold of diffeomorphisms, where the local geometry is characterised by a variational principle involving $\mathcal F$. This connects the learning efficiency of target relationships to their compatibility with the learning architectural choice. Further, the results suggest that the key approximation mechanism in deep learning, namely the approximation of functions by composition or dynamics, differs in a fundamental way from linear approximation theory, where linear spaces and norm-based rate estimates are replaced by manifolds and geodesic distances.

</details>

Abstract: Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) and neural operators (NOs) for solving the problem of diffraction of Extreme Ultraviolet (EUV) electromagnetic waves from contemporary lithography masks are presented. The emphasis is placed on investigation of solution accuracy by considered artificial neural systems for 13.5 nm and 11.2 nm wavelengths. Numerical experiments on realistic 2D and 3D masks demonstrate that PINNs and neural operators achieve competitive accuracy and significantly reduced prediction times, with the proposed WGNO architecture reaching state-of-the-art performance. The presented neural operator has pronounced generalizing properties, meaning that for unseen problem parameters it delivers a solution accuracy close to that for parameters seen in the training dataset. These results provide a highly efficient solution for accelerating the design and optimization workflows of next-generation lithography masks.

### [269] [Local Urysohn Width: A Topological Complexity Measure for Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15412)
*Xin Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出局部Urysohn宽度这一新指标，用于度量分类问题本身的拓扑几何复杂度，而非假设类的丰富度。证明了严格的层级定理、拓扑-几何标度律、与VC维的双向分离关系，以及独立于VC维的样本复杂度下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的复杂度度量（如VC维、fat-shattering维、Rademacher复杂度）刻画的是假设类的丰富度，而非分类问题本身的内在复杂度。本文旨在填补这一空白，引入一种新的复杂度度量来刻画分类问题本身的拓扑几何性质。

Method: 引入局部Urysohn宽度概念，定义为正确分类边界安全区域内所有点所需的最少连通、直径有界的局部专家数量。通过构造具有特定拓扑结构（圆束，Betti数为β₁=w）的度量空间，建立层级定理；分析宽度与拓扑（独立环数）、几何（环周长与局部尺度之比）的关系；构造反例展示与VC维的双向分离；推导样本复杂度下界。

Result: （1）严格层级定理：对任意w≥1，存在连通紧度量空间上的分类问题，其Urysohn宽度恰为w；（2）拓扑-几何标度律：宽度以Ω(w·L/D₀)的速率增长；（3）与VC维的双向分离：存在宽度无限增长而VC维有界的问题族，也存在VC维无限增长而宽度为1的问题族；（4）样本复杂度下界：任何学习器需要Ω(w log w)样本，独立于VC维。

Conclusion: 局部Urysohn宽度成功刻画了分类问题的内在拓扑几何复杂度，揭示了输入空间的拓扑复杂性如何迫使分类器复杂度增加。该度量与VC维互补，能够解释传统复杂度度量无法刻画的现象，为理解学习问题的本质难度提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce \emph{local Urysohn width}, a complexity measure for classification problems on metric spaces. Unlike VC dimension, fat-shattering dimension, and Rademacher complexity, which characterize the richness of hypothesis \emph{classes}, Urysohn width characterizes the topological-geometric complexity of the classification \emph{problem itself}: the minimum number of connected, diameter-bounded local experts needed to correctly classify all points within a margin-safe region. We prove four main results. First, a \textbf{strict hierarchy theorem}: for every integer $w \geq 1$, there exists a classification problem on a \emph{connected} compact metric space (a bouquet of circles with first Betti number $β_1 = w$) whose Urysohn width is exactly~$w$, establishing that topological complexity of the input space forces classifier complexity. Second, a \textbf{topology $\times$ geometry scaling law}: width scales as $Ω(w \cdot L/D_0)$, where $w$ counts independent loops and $L/D_0$ is the ratio of loop circumference to locality scale. Third, a \textbf{two-way separation from VC dimension}: there exist problem families where width grows unboundedly while VC dimension is bounded by a constant, and conversely, families where VC dimension grows unboundedly while width remains~1. Fourth, a \textbf{sample complexity lower bound}: any learner that must correctly classify all points in the safe region of a width-$w$ problem needs $Ω(w \log w)$ samples, independent of VC dimension.

</details>


### [270] [Federated Learning of Binary Neural Networks: Enabling Low-Cost Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15507)
*Nitin Priyadarshini Shankar,Soham Lahiri,Sheetal Kalyani,Saurav Prakash*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了FedBNN，一种面向边缘设备的联邦学习二值神经网络框架，通过在本地训练中直接学习二值表示，在保持与实值模型相当性能的同时，显著降低了模型大小、计算量和内存需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习在边缘设备上部署深度神经网络面临两大挑战：边缘设备计算能力有限，而传统DNN计算开销大、内存占用高；传统训练后二值化方法虽能减小模型尺寸，但会导致严重的精度损失。需要在保护隐私的前提下，设计适合资源受限边缘设备的高效模型。

Method: 提出FedBNN框架，一种旋转感知的二值神经网络，在联邦学习的本地训练阶段直接学习二值表示。通过将权重从32位浮点数编码为单个比特{-1, +1}，大幅压缩模型规模并减少推理时的计算量和内存需求。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的实验表明，FedBNN在资源消耗方面显著降低（模型大小约减少32倍，计算量大幅降低），同时性能与使用实值模型的联邦学习方法相当。

Conclusion: FedBNN成功解决了边缘设备上联邦学习的资源限制问题，通过直接学习二值表示避免了传统后训练二值化的精度损失，为资源受限环境下的隐私保护学习提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) preserves privacy by distributing training across devices. However, using DNNs is computationally intensive at the low-powered edge during inference. Edge deployment demands models that simultaneously optimize memory footprint and computational efficiency, a dilemma where conventional DNNs fail by exceeding resource limits. Traditional post-training binarization reduces model size but suffers from severe accuracy loss due to quantization errors. To address these challenges, we propose FedBNN, a rotation-aware binary neural network framework that learns binary representations directly during local training. By encoding each weight as a single bit $\{+1, -1\}$ instead of a $32$-bit float, FedBNN shrinks the model footprint, significantly reducing runtime (during inference) FLOPs and memory requirements in comparison to federated methods using real models. Evaluations across multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate that FedBNN significantly reduces resource consumption while performing similarly to existing federated methods using real-valued models.

### [271] [Not All Invariants Are Equal: Curating Training Data to Accelerate Program Verification with SLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15510)
*Ido Pinto,Yizhak Yisrael Elboher,Haoze Wu,Nina Narodytska,Guy Katz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高质量数据筛选管道Wonda，通过对验证器生成的原始不变式进行AST归一化和语义重写，生成高质量训练数据。基于此数据微调的40亿参数小语言模型达到GPT-OSS-120B性能并接近GPT-5.2，在困难实例上不变式正确率翻倍，验证任务虚拟最优性能提升达14.2%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出名为Wonda的严格数据筛选管道：首先形式化高质量训练不变式所需的属性；然后通过基于AST的归一化精炼噪声数据，接着进行LLM驱动的语义重写和增强，并提供可证明的质量保证；最后使用筛选后的数据集微调小语言模型（SLMs）。

Result: 微调后的40亿参数模型达到GPT-OSS-120B基线的性能并接近最先进的GPT-5.2，且无推理时开销。在InvBench评估套件的挑战性实例上，不变式正确率和加速率翻倍；验证任务的虚拟最优性能（VBP）率提升高达14.2%。

Conclusion: 高质量数据筛选管道能够从小语言模型中释放强大性能，使其匹配或接近大得多的模型，为缓解程序验证中不变式综合瓶颈提供了有效且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: The synthesis of inductive loop invariants is a critical bottleneck in automated program verification. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise in mitigating this issue, they often fail on hard instances, generating invariants that are invalid or computationally ineffective. While fine-tuning is a natural route to mitigate this limitation, obtaining high-quality training data for invariant generation remains an open challenge. We present a rigorous data curation pipeline designed to extract high-quality training signals from raw verifier-generated invariants. First, we formalize the properties required for a high-quality training invariant. Second, we propose Wonda, a pipeline that refines noisy data via AST-based normalization, followed by LLM-driven semantic rewriting and augmentation with provable quality guarantees. We demonstrate that fine-tuning Small Language Models (SLMs) on this curated dataset result in consistent and significant performance gain. In particular, a fine-tuned 4B parameter model matches the utility of a GPT-OSS-120B baseline and approaches the state-of-the-art GPT-5.2, without incurring reasoning-time overhead. On challenging instances from the recent InvBench evaluation suite, our approach doubles the invariant correctness and speedup rates of base models; and improves their Virtual Best Performance (VBP) rates on the verification task by up to 14.2%.

### [272] [Vib2ECG: A Paired Chest-Lead SCG-ECG Dataset and Benchmark for ECG Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15539)
*Guorui Lu,Xiaohui Cai,Todor Stefanov,Qinyu Chen*

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过低成本IMU传感器获取振动信号进行移动设备友好的ECG监测的可行性，拓展了心振动信号的应用范围，为理解心脏电-机械活动在不同空间位置的相互关系提供了新见解，为未来无创心脏监测技术发展奠定基础。

Abstract: Twelve-lead electrocardiography (ECG) is essential for cardiovascular diagnosis, but its long-term acquisition in daily life is constrained by complex and costly hardware. Recent efforts have explored reconstructing ECG from low-cost cardiac vibrational signals such as seismocardiography (SCG), however, due to the lack of a dataset, current methods are limited to limb leads, while clinical diagnosis requires multi-lead ECG, including chest leads. In this work, we propose Vib2ECG, the first paired, multi-channel electro-mechanical cardiac signal dataset, which includes complete twelve-lead ECGs and vibrational signals acquired by inertial measurement units (IMUs) at six chest-lead positions from 17 subjects. Based on this dataset, we also provide a benchmark. Experimental results demonstrate the feasibility of reconstructing electrical cardiac signals at variable locations from vibrational signals using a lightweight 364 K-parameter U-Net. Furthermore, we observe a hallucination phenomenon in the model, where ECG waveforms are generated in regions where no corresponding electrical activity is present. We analyze the causes of this phenomenon and propose potential directions for mitigation. This study demonstrates the feasibility of mobile-device-friendly ECG monitoring through chest-lead ECG prediction from low-cost vibrational signals acquired using IMU sensors. It expands the application of cardiac vibrational signals and provides new insights into the spatial relationship between cardiac electrical and mechanical activities with spatial location variation.

</details>


### [273] [Predictive Uncertainty in Short-Term PV Forecasting under Missing Data: A Multiple Imputation Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15564)
*Parastoo Pashmchi,Jérôme Benoit,Motonobu Kanagawa*

Result: 实验结果表明，忽略缺失数据不确定性会导致预测区间过窄；考虑该不确定性可在保持点预测精度相当的情况下改善区间校准性能。

Abstract: Missing values are common in photovoltaic (PV) power data, yet the uncertainty they induce is not propagated into predictive distributions. We develop a framework that incorporates missing-data uncertainty into short-term PV forecasting by combining stochastic multiple imputation with Rubin's rule. The approach is model-agnostic and can be integrated with standard machine-learning predictors. Empirical results show that ignoring missing-data uncertainty leads to overly narrow prediction intervals. Accounting for this uncertainty improves interval calibration while maintaining comparable point prediction accuracy. These results demonstrate the importance of propagating imputation uncertainty in data-driven PV forecasting.

### [274] [Mamba-3: Improved Sequence Modeling using State Space Principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15569)
*Aakash Lahoti,Kevin Y. Li,Berlin Chen,Caitlin Wang,Aviv Bick,J. Zico Kolter,Tri Dao,Albert Gu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Mamba-3模型，通过引入SSM启发的表达性递归、复数值状态更新规则和MIMO架构三项改进，在保持推理效率的同时显著提升了模型性能，相比Gated DeltaNet在下游任务准确率提升1.8个百分点，且以一半的状态大小达到Mamba-2的困惑度水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer模型虽然质量优异，但二次方计算复杂度和线性内存需求导致推理开销大；近期线性模型虽降低了计算复杂度，但以牺牲模型质量和能力（如状态跟踪）为代价，且理论线性推理在实际硬件上效率不佳。

Method: 从推理优先视角出发，结合状态空间模型（SSM）观点引入三项核心改进：(1)源自SSM离散化的更具表达力的递归；(2)支持更丰富状态跟踪的复数值状态更新规则；(3)在不增加解码延迟的前提下提升性能的多输入多输出（MIMO）架构，并配合架构优化。

Result: 在1.5B规模下，Mamba-3相比次优模型Gated DeltaNet的平均下游准确率提升0.6个百分点，MIMO变体额外提升1.2个百分点，总计提升1.8个百分点；在不同状态规模实验中，Mamba-3使用Mamba-2一半的状态大小即可达到相当的困惑度。

Conclusion: Mamba-3成功推进了性能-效率帕累托前沿，证明了通过SSM启发的架构改进可以在保持推理效率的同时显著提升模型在检索、状态跟踪和下游语言建模任务上的表现。

Abstract: Scaling inference-time compute has emerged as an important driver of LLM performance, making inference efficiency a central focus of model design alongside model quality. While the current Transformer-based models deliver strong model quality, their quadratic compute and linear memory make inference expensive. This has spurred the development of sub-quadratic models with reduced linear compute and constant memory requirements. However, many recent linear models trade off model quality and capability for algorithmic efficiency, failing on tasks such as state tracking. Moreover, their theoretically linear inference remains hardware-inefficient in practice. Guided by an inference-first perspective, we introduce three core methodological improvements inspired by the state space model (SSM) viewpoint of linear models. We combine: (1) a more expressive recurrence derived from SSM discretization, (2) a complex-valued state update rule that enables richer state tracking, and (3) a multi-input, multi-output (MIMO) formulation for better model performance without increasing decode latency. Together with architectural refinements, our Mamba-3 model achieves significant gains across retrieval, state-tracking, and downstream language modeling tasks. At the 1.5B scale, Mamba-3 improves average downstream accuracy by 0.6 percentage points compared to the next best model (Gated DeltaNet), with Mamba-3's MIMO variant further improving accuracy by another 1.2 points for a total 1.8 point gain. Across state-size experiments, Mamba-3 achieves comparable perplexity to Mamba-2 despite using half of its predecessor's state size. Our evaluations demonstrate Mamba-3's ability to advance the performance-efficiency Pareto frontier.

### [275] [Unbiased and Biased Variance-Reduced Forward-Reflected-Backward Splitting Methods for Stochastic Composite Inclusions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15576)
*Quoc Tran-Dinh,Nghia Nguyen-Trung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文为前向-反射-后向分裂(FRBS)方法开发了新的方差缩减技术，用于求解一类可能非单调的随机复合包含问题，建立了首个能同时处理无偏和有偏估计器的统一框架，并获得了最优的oracle复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对包含问题和不动点问题的随机方差缩减方法仅限于无偏估计器（如mini-batching），而开发随机有偏变体面临根本性技术挑战，这一空白亟待填补。本文旨在构建一个统一框架，同时处理无偏和有偏估计器，以扩展FRBS方法的应用范围并提升其收敛性能。

Method: 核心思想是为前向-反射方向构建随机方差缩减估计器，并利用这些估计器执行迭代更新。首先提出一类无偏方差缩减估计器，涵盖递增mini-batch SGD、loopless-SVRG和SAGA。其次引入一类新的有偏方差缩减估计器，将SARAH、Hybrid SGD和Hybrid SVRG作为特例包含其中。两种类型的估计器均在相同的理论框架下进行分析。

Result: 对于无偏估计器，建立了期望平方残差范数的O(1/k)最佳迭代收敛率，以及迭代序列到解的几乎必然收敛性。当使用loopless-SVRG或SAGA时，n-有限和与期望设置下的最优oracle复杂度分别为O(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})和O(ε^{-10/3})。对于有偏估计器，收敛率保持有效，但oracle复杂度分别为O(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})和O(ε^{-5})。无偏估计器在有限和设置下获得了更优的复杂度。

Conclusion: 本文成功填补了随机有偏方差缩减技术在包含问题和不动点问题中应用的理论空白，构建了统一处理无偏和有偏估计器的框架。理论分析表明，在有限和设置下，无偏估计器（如loopless-SVRG和SAGA）能够实现更优的oracle复杂度。数值实验（包括不平衡分类的AUC优化和强化学习中的策略评估）验证了所提方法的实际有效性。

Abstract: This paper develops new variance-reduction techniques for the forward-reflected-backward splitting (FRBS) method to solve a class of possibly nonmonotone stochastic composite inclusions. Unlike unbiased estimators such as mini-batching, developing stochastic biased variants faces a fundamental technical challenge and has not been utilized before for inclusions and fixed-point problems. We fill this gap by designing a new framework that can handle both unbiased and biased estimators. Our main idea is to construct stochastic variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction and use them to perform iterate updates. First, we propose a class of unbiased variance-reduced estimators and show that increasing mini-batch SGD, loopless-SVRG, and SAGA estimators fall within this class. For these unbiased estimators, we establish a $\mathcal{O}(1/k)$ best-iterate convergence rate for the expected squared residual norm, together with almost-sure convergence of the iterate sequence to a solution. Consequently, we prove that the best oracle complexities for the $n$-finite-sum and expectation settings are $\mathcal{O}(n^{2/3}ε^{-2})$ and $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-10/3})$, respectively, when employing loopless-SVRG or SAGA, where $ε$ is a desired accuracy. Second, we introduce a new class of biased variance-reduced estimators for the forward-reflected direction, which includes SARAH, Hybrid SGD, and Hybrid SVRG as special instances. While the convergence rates remain valid for these biased estimators, the resulting oracle complexities are $\mathcal{O}(n^{3/4}ε^{-2})$ and $\mathcal{O}(ε^{-5})$ for the $n$-finite-sum and expectation settings, respectively. Finally, we conduct two numerical experiments on AUC optimization for imbalanced classification and policy evaluation in reinforcement learning.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的二次注意力大语言模型蒸馏为次二次线性架构的方法存在性能损失问题，蒸馏后的学生模型在下游任务上往往无法匹配教师模型的性能。因此，研究目标是实现无损蒸馏，通过容忍度校正的Win-and-Tie率来衡量学生与教师模型在任务集上的表现。

Method: 提出了一种针对xLSTM学生模型的有效蒸馏流程，核心创新是在蒸馏过程中引入了一个合并阶段（merging stage），将单独线性化的专家模型组合成一个统一模型。该流程应用于Llama、Qwen和Olmo系列的基座模型和指令微调模型。

Abstract: There have been numerous attempts to distill quadratic attention-based large language models (LLMs) into sub-quadratic linearized architectures. However, despite extensive research, such distilled models often fail to match the performance of their teacher LLMs on various downstream tasks. We set out the goal of lossless distillation, which we define in terms of tolerance-corrected Win-and-Tie rates between student and teacher on sets of tasks. To this end, we introduce an effective distillation pipeline for xLSTM-based students. We propose an additional merging stage, where individually linearized experts are combined into a single model. We show the effectiveness of this pipeline by distilling base and instruction-tuned models from the Llama, Qwen, and Olmo families. ### [277] [Robust and Computationally Efficient Linear Contextual Bandits under Adversarial Corruption and Heavy-Tailed Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15596)
*Naoto Tani,Futoshi Futami*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于在线镜像下降的高效算法，在有限(1+ε)阶矩（ε∈(0,1]）假设下，同时实现了对对抗性腐败和重尾噪声的鲁棒性，将每轮计算复杂度从O(t log T)降至O(1)，且无需预知噪声矩界或腐败总量即可保证次线性遗憾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有同时处理对抗性腐败和重尾噪声的研究依赖于有限方差（二阶矩）假设，且存在计算效率低下的问题（计算成本为O(t log T)）。本文旨在解决更一般的有限(1+ε)阶矩场景下的线性上下文老虎机问题，并提升算法的计算效率。

Method: 提出了一种基于在线镜像下降（Online Mirror Descent）的计算高效算法。该算法无需预知噪声矩界或对抗性腐败总量的先验知识，通过精心设计实现对重尾噪声和对抗性腐败的双重鲁棒性。

Result: 算法将每轮计算复杂度从O(t log T)降低至O(1)。建立了加性遗憾界，包含一个依赖于噪声(1+ε)阶矩界的项和一个依赖于腐败总量的项。当ε=1时，恢复了有限方差假设下的现有保证；无腐败时，匹配重尾噪声下已知的最优速率。

Conclusion: 本文成功解决了线性上下文老虎机中对抗性腐败与重尾噪声并存的挑战，突破了有限方差假设的限制，显著提升了计算效率，且算法具有无需先验知识的实用性，为鲁棒在线学习提供了新的理论基础和高效解决方案。

Abstract: We study linear contextual bandits under adversarial corruption and heavy-tailed noise with finite $(1+ε)$-th moments for some $ε\in (0,1]$. Existing work that addresses both adversarial corruption and heavy-tailed noise relies on a finite variance (i.e., finite second-moment) assumption and suffers from computational inefficiency. We propose a computationally efficient algorithm based on online mirror descent that achieves robustness to both adversarial corruption and heavy-tailed noise. While the existing algorithm incurs $\mathcal{O}(t\log T)$ computational cost, our algorithm reduces this to $\mathcal{O}(1)$ per round. We establish an additive regret bound consisting of a term depending on the $(1+ε)$-moment bound of the noise and a term depending on the total amount of corruption. In particular, when $ε= 1$, our result recovers existing guarantees under finite-variance assumptions. When no corruption is present, it matches the best-known rates for linear contextual bandits with heavy-tailed noise. Moreover, the algorithm requires no prior knowledge of the noise moment bound or the total amount of corruption and still guarantees sublinear regret.

### [278] [SmartSearch: How Ranking Beats Structure for Conversational Memory Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15599)
*Jesper Derehag,Carlos Calva,Timmy Ghiurau*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SmartSearch提出了一种无需LLM结构化和学习型检索策略的对话记忆检索系统，通过完全确定性的流程（NER加权子串匹配、基于规则的实体发现和CrossEncoder+ColBERT排序融合）在两个基准测试上超越所有已知记忆系统，token使用量减少8.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对话记忆系统在摄入时依赖昂贵的LLM结构化处理，在查询时依赖学习型检索策略。作者旨在证明这两种方式都不必要，探索一种完全确定性、无需每数据集调优的检索方案。

Method: 采用完全确定性的三阶段流程：(1) NER加权子串匹配实现召回；(2) 基于规则的实体发现进行多跳扩展；(3) CrossEncoder+ColBERT排序融合（唯一的学习组件），在CPU上运行约650ms。引入分数自适应截断机制处理token预算限制。

Result: 在LoCoMo基准上达到93.5%，在LongMemEval-S上达到88.4%，在相同评估协议下超越所有已知记忆系统。检索召回率达98.6%，通过智能排序解决截断瓶颈。token使用量比全上下文基线减少8.5倍。

Conclusion: SmartSearch证明了无需LLM结构化和学习型检索策略即可实现优异的对话记忆检索性能。完全确定性的流程配合分数自适应截断机制，在保证高效的同时显著降低了计算成本和token消耗。

Abstract: Recent conversational memory systems invest heavily in LLM-based structuring at ingestion time and learned retrieval policies at query time. We show that neither is necessary. SmartSearch retrieves from raw, unstructured conversation history using a fully deterministic pipeline: NER-weighted substring matching for recall, rule-based entity discovery for multi-hop expansion, and a CrossEncoder+ColBERT rank fusion stage -- the only learned component -- running on CPU in ~650ms. Oracle analysis on two benchmarks identifies a compilation bottleneck: retrieval recall reaches 98.6%, but without intelligent ranking only 22.5% of gold evidence survives truncation to the token budget. With score-adaptive truncation and no per-dataset tuning, SmartSearch achieves 93.5% on LoCoMo and 88.4% on LongMemEval-S, exceeding all known memory systems under the same evaluation protocol on both benchmarks while using 8.5x fewer tokens than full-context baselines.

</details>


### [279] [HorizonMath: Measuring AI Progress Toward Mathematical Discovery with Automatic Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15617)
*Erik Y. Wang,Sumeet Motwani,James V. Roggeveen,Eliot Hodges,Dulhan Jayalath,Charles London,Kalyan Ramakrishnan,Flaviu Cipcigan,Philip Torr,Alessandro Abate*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了HorizonMath基准，包含100多个主要未解决的数学问题，用于评估大语言模型在数学研究前沿的探索能力，并发现GPT-5.4 Pro在两个问题上提出了超越已知最优结果的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型已具备复杂的数学和科学推理能力，但其在生成新颖研究成果方面的能力仍存在争议且缺乏系统探索；现有研究级基准依赖形式化证明验证或人工审查，成本高且难以规模化。

Method: 构建HorizonMath基准，包含8个计算与应用数学领域的100多个以未解决问题为主的测试集，配套开源自动化验证框架；问题设计遵循"发现困难、验证高效"的原则，确保基准不受数据污染影响。

Result: 大多数最先进模型在HorizonMath上的得分接近0%；GPT-5.4 Pro在两个问题上提出了改进已知最优结果的解决方案，具有潜在新颖贡献价值（待专家审查确认）。

Conclusion: HorizonMath为评估AI在未解决数学问题上的研究能力提供了可扩展、抗污染的基准平台，正确解答未解决问题可能构成数学文献中的新颖成果，并作为开放挑战和社区资源持续发展。

Abstract: Can AI make progress on important, unsolved mathematical problems? Large language models are now capable of sophisticated mathematical and scientific reasoning, but whether they can perform novel research is still widely debated and underexplored. We introduce HorizonMath, a benchmark of over 100 predominantly unsolved problems spanning 8 domains in computational and applied mathematics, paired with an open-source evaluation framework for automated verification. Our benchmark targets a class of problems where discovery is hard, requiring meaningful mathematical insight, but verification is computationally efficient and simple. Because these solutions are unknown, HorizonMath is immune to data contamination, and most state-of-the-art models score near 0%. Existing research-level benchmarks instead rely on formal proof verification or manual review, both of which are expensive to scale. Using this platform, we find two problems for which GPT 5.4 Pro proposes solutions that improve on the best-known published results, representing potential novel contributions (pending expert review). We release HorizonMath as an open challenge and a growing community resource, where correct solutions to problems in the unsolved problem classes could constitute novel results in the mathematical literature.

### [280] [NCCL EP: Towards a Unified Expert Parallel Communication API for NCCL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13606)
*Amos Goldman,Nimrod Boker,Maayan Sheraizin,Nimrod Admoni,Artem Polyakov,Subhadeep Bhattacharya,Fan Yu,Kai Sun,Georgios Theodorakis,Hsin-Chun Yin,Peter-Jan Gootzen,Aamir Shafi,Assaf Ravid,Salvatore Di Girolamo,Manjunath Gorentla Venkata,Gil Bloch*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了NCCL EP，一个基于NCCL Device API从头构建的MoE通信库，提供低延迟（LL）和高吞吐（HT）两种模式，在H100集群上展现了竞争性能，为专家并行提供了原生支持方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着MoE架构成为大语言模型扩展的关键技术，现有专用通信库（如DeepEP、Hybrid-EP）展示了GPU发起RDMA的性能优势，但缺乏统一的原生支持方案。需要构建一个完全基于NCCL Device API的MoE通信库，以在当前和未来NVIDIA平台上提供受支持的专家并行路径。

Method: 基于NCCL Device API从头构建NCCL EP通信库，提供统一的ncclEpDispatch和ncclEpCombine原语（支持C和Python接口）。设计两种模式：(1)低延迟（LL）模式针对小批量（1-128 tokens），使用直接all-to-all RDMA+NVLink网格连接和双缓冲通信；(2)高吞吐（HT）模式针对大批量（4096+ tokens），使用层次化通信在NVLink域内聚合token后再进行跨节点RDMA传输。两种模式均利用Device API的拓扑感知和优化的GPU发起实现。

Result: 在基于H100的集群上跨多节点配置进行评估，NCCL EP展现出具有竞争力的LL内核性能，并与vLLM集成展示了端到端结果。通过在NCCL内原生构建MoE通信，为当前和新兴NVIDIA平台上的专家并行提供了受支持路径。

Conclusion: NCCL EP成功将MoE通信原生集成到NCCL中，通过完全基于Device API的实现，在保持性能竞争力的同时为专家并行提供了官方支持的标准化方案，为未来NVIDIA平台上的MoE部署奠定了基础。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures have become essential for scaling large language models, driving the development of specialized device-initiated communication libraries such as DeepEP, Hybrid-EP, and others. These libraries demonstrate the performance benefits of GPU-initiated RDMA for MoE dispatch and combine operations.
  This paper presents NCCL EP (Expert Parallelism), a ground-up MoE communication library built entirely on NCCL's Device API. NCCL EP provides unified ncclEpDispatch and ncclEpCombine primitives with both C and Python interfaces, supporting Low-Latency (LL) mode for inference decoding and High-Throughput (HT) mode for training and inference prefill. LL targets small batch sizes (1-128 tokens) using direct all-to-all RDMA+NVLink mesh connectivity with double-buffered communication for overlapping dispatch and combine phases. HT targets large batches (4096+ tokens) using hierarchical communication that aggregates tokens within NVLink domains before inter-node RDMA transmission. Both modes leverage Device API for both intra- and inter-node communications, taking advantage of its topology awareness and optimized GPU-initiated implementation.
  We evaluate NCCL EP on an H100-based cluster across multi-node configurations, demonstrating competitive LL kernel performance and presenting end-to-end results with vLLM integration. By building MoE communication natively within NCCL, NCCL EP provides a supported path for expert parallelism on current and emerging NVIDIA platforms.

</details>

### [282] [Guaranteeing Semantic and Performance Determinism in Flexible GPU Sharing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15042)
*Zhenyuan Yang,Wenxin Zheng,Mingyu Li*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: DetShare是一个新型GPU共享系统，通过引入GPU协程抽象实现逻辑执行上下文与物理资源的解耦，在不修改代码的前提下同时保证语义确定性和性能确定性，显著提升训练吞吐量并降低推理尾延迟。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DetShare系统，引入GPU协程(GPU coroutines)这一新抽象，将逻辑执行上下文与物理GPU资源解耦。通过轻量级上下文迁移实现灵活、细粒度的资源分配。采用负载感知放置策略和TPOT-First调度策略优化推理性能。整个系统保证完全透明性（零代码修改）并确保语义确定性（未修改内核产生相同结果）和性能确定性（可预测的尾延迟）。

Result: 与时间共享相比，训练吞吐量提升高达79.2%。在混合部署场景中，P99尾延迟降低15.1%且不损失吞吐量。通过负载感知放置和TPOT-First调度策略，平均推理延迟降低69.1%，TPOT SLO违规减少21.2%。

Conclusion: DetShare成功解决了GPU共享中确定性与透明性的矛盾，为数据中心GPU资源的高效利用提供了实用解决方案，在训练和推理场景中均取得显著性能提升，证明了GPU协程抽象和细粒度资源管理的有效性。

Abstract: GPU sharing is critical for maximizing hardware utilization in modern data centers. However, existing approaches present a stark trade-off: coarse-grained temporal multiplexing incurs severe tail-latency spikes for interactive services, while fine-grained spatial partitioning often necessitates invasive kernel modifications that compromise behavioral equivalence.
  We present DetShare, a novel GPU sharing system that prioritizes determinism and transparency. DetShare ensures semantic determinism (unmodified kernels yield identical results) and performance determinism (predictable tail latency), all while maintaining complete transparency (zero code modification). DetShare introduces GPU coroutines, a new abstraction that decouples logical execution contexts from physical GPU resources. This decoupling enables flexible, fine-grained resource allocation via lightweight context migration.
  Our evaluation demonstrates that DetShare improves training throughput by up to 79.2% compared to temporal sharing. Abstract: Global cryptocurrencies are unbacked and have high transaction cost incurred by global consensus. In contrast, grassroots cryptocurrencies are backed by the goods and services of their issuers -- any person, natural or legal -- and have no transaction cost beyond operating a smartphone. Liquidity in grassroots cryptocurrencies arises from mutual credit via coin exchange among issuers. However, as grassroots coins are redeemable 1-for-1 against any other grassroots coin, the credit-forming exchange must also be 1-for-1, lest prompt redemption after exchange would leave the parties with undue profit or loss. Thus, grassroots coins are incongruent with liquidity through interest-bearing credit.
  Here we introduce grassroots bonds, which extend grassroots coins with a maturity date, reframing grassroots coins -- cash -- as mature grassroots bonds. Bond redemption generalises coin redemption, allowing the lending of liquid coins in exchange for interest-bearing future-maturity bonds. We show that digital social contracts -- voluntary agreements among persons, specified, fulfilled, and enforced digitally -- can express the full gamut of financial instruments as the voluntary swap of grassroots bonds, including credit lines, loans, sale of debt, forward contracts, options, and escrow-based instruments, and that classical liquidity ratios are applicable just as well to grassroots bonds. The implementation is illustrated by a running multiagent village market scenario, also implemented in GLP by AI.

### [284] [LMetric: Simple is Better - Multiplication May Be All You Need for LLM Request Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15202)
*Dingyan Zhang,Jinbo Han,Kaixi Zhang,Xingda Wei,Sijie Shen,Chenguang Fang,Wenyuan Yu,Jingren Zhou,Rong Chen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需超参数调优的LLM请求调度方法，通过简单的指标乘法同时实现KV缓存感知和负载均衡，在真实工作负载中显著降低了TTFT和TPOT。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM请求调度方法难以同时兼顾KV缓存利用和负载均衡两个目标。当前方法使用复杂的组合器（如线性组合）计算调度分数，需要大量针对工作负载的超参数调优或开发模型-硬件感知的模拟器，且仍可能导致次优性能。

Method: 提出一种简单的乘法策略，将两个精心选择的指标相乘作为调度分数：KV感知指标（路由到实例的新预填充token数）和负载均衡感知指标（实例的当前批大小）。该方法在比较过程中原始超参数会被抵消，因此无需调优。同时数学推导了乘法可能失效的条件，并发现这些条件在实践中极其罕见且可提前检测和缓解。

Result: 在涵盖聊天机器人、API调用和编程代理的真实世界工作负载上进行了大量实验。与vLLM-v1相比，TTFT降低92%，TPOT降低21%；与生产调度器相比，TTFT降低52%，TPOT降低20%。

Conclusion: 通过理论分析和实验验证，证明了简单的指标乘法可以有效同时实现KV缓存感知和负载均衡两个目标，无需超参数调优，显著优于现有的复杂方法。该方法为LLM请求调度提供了一种简单、高效且理论上可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: High-quality LLM request scheduling requires achieving two key objectives: whether the routed instance has KV$ to accelerate the request execution and whether the workload is balanced across instances. Achieving both objectives is challenging because pursuing one objective may compromise the other. Current approaches adopt various combinators (e.g., linear combinations) to compute a scheduling score combining indicators for the two objectives, which are complex in that they either require significant workload-specific hyperparameter tuning or model-hardware-aware simulator development, and could still lead to suboptimal performance. In this paper, we show that using a simple multiplication of two carefully chosen indicators-one for KV$-aware (new prefill tokens if routed to an instance) and one for load balancing-aware (current batch size of the instance)-as the scheduling score can simultaneously achieve both objectives well without any hyperparameter tuning. The key idea is that the multiplied score considers both objectives in a manner similar to a linear combination, with a nice property that the original hyperparameters are canceled out during comparison so we don't need tuning to find the best parameters. The two indicators are chosen based on our analysis of LLM characteristics, and our extensive experiments show that this simple approach can reduce TTFT by 92% and 52%, and TPOT by 21% and 20%, compared to vLLM-v1 and a production scheduler on real-world workloads covering chatbots, API calls, and coding agents. We also mathematically derive the conditions under which multiplication may fail, and find that such conditions are extremely rare in practice and can be detected (and mitigated) beforehand.

</details>


### [285] [The Markovianity of Time: The Category Mistake in Open Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13738)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文挑战了马尔可夫近似必然导致时间不对称性的普遍假设，证明马尔可夫性本身是时间对称的，不对称性源于边界条件而非动力学。这一发现动摇了分布式计算中FLP、CAP等不可能定理的基础假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理学和信息理论领域普遍认为马尔可夫近似本质上是时间不对称的（仅向前演化），这一假设已渗透到香农信道模型、Lamport逻辑时钟以及分布式计算的基础理论中。作者旨在揭示这一广泛接受的观点实际上是一个"范畴错误"，即混淆了约定俗成与物理定律。

Method: 基于Guff、Shastry和Rocco（2025）关于Caldeira-Leggett模型的最新研究成果，分析马尔可夫近似在开放量子系统中的应用。追踪时间不对称性假设从物理学经香农信息理论到Lamport先于关系和分布式计算不可能定理的传播路径，识别每一步中FITO假设如何从约定被误认为物理定律。

Result: 马尔可夫近似在Caldeira-Leggett模型中保持时间反演对称性，由此导出的量子布朗运动、Lindblad主方程和Pauli主方程的时间对称形式表明，热化过程可以在两个相反的时间方向上发生。不对称性并非来自动力学本身，而是源于边界条件。这证明了最基本的不可逆性推导所用的近似本身就是时间对称的。

Conclusion: 马尔可夫性所假设的方向性是一个跨领域的范畴错误——从物理学到信息理论再到分布式计算，每一步都将约定误认为物理定律。这种混淆不仅在哲学上可疑，在数学上也是不必要的，动摇了分布式计算基础理论的根基。

Abstract: The Markov approximation is arguably the most ubiquitous tool in physics, underpinning quantum master equations, stochastic processes, and -- via Shannon's channel model and Lamport's logical clocks -- the foundational assumptions of distributed computing. It is widely assumed that Markovianity inherently implies temporal asymmetry: that the Markov property is a forward-in-time-only (FITO) construct. We show that this assumption is a category mistake in the sense of Ryle (1949).
  Guff, Shastry, and Rocco (2025) have recently demonstrated that the Markov approximation applied to the Caldeira-Leggett model -- a paradigmatic open quantum system -- maintains time-reversal symmetry in the derived equations of motion. The resulting time-symmetric formulations of quantum Brownian motion, Lindblad master equations, and Pauli master equations describe thermalisation that can occur in two opposing temporal directions. Asymmetry arises not from the dynamics but from boundary conditions.
  We trace how Markovianity's assumed directionality propagated from physics through Shannon's information theory to Lamport's happens-before relation and the impossibility theorems of distributed computing (FLP, CAP, Two Generals). Each step encodes FITO as convention, then treats it as physical law -- the same category mistake repeated across domains. The Surrey result establishes that this conflation is not merely philosophically suspect but mathematically unnecessary: the most fundamental approximation used to derive irreversibility is itself time-symmetric.

</details>


### [286] [The Forward-In-Time-Only Assumption in SmartNIC Resource Management: A Critique of Wave and the Case for Bilateral Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13750)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文批评Wave系统的FITO通信模式导致性能下降，提出使用双向原子交换原语可从根本上解决延迟和一致性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者观察到Wave将工作卸载到SmartNIC时出现350%的性能下降，认为这并非可通过工程优化解决的表面问题，而是源于更深层的架构缺陷：FITO（仅向前传递时间）通信模式存在决策过期的时序漏洞。

Method: 对Wave的FITO通信模型进行系统诊断，揭示其继承了Lamport happened-before和Shannon信道模型的分类错误，然后展示Open Atomic Ethernet的双边交换原语如何在同一Intel IPU硬件上从根本上解决问题。

Result: FITO诊断成功解释了Wave性能下降的根本原因；使用双向原子交换原语可以消除延迟、原子性和超时问题，无需复杂的工程绕行方案。

Conclusion: SmartNIC是资源管理的正确位置，但关键在于使用正确的通信原语——双向原子交换而非单向消息传递。

Abstract: The datacenter industry is converging on SmartNIC-based resource management. Wave (Humphries et al., ASPLOS '25) demonstrates the practical feasibility of offloading kernel thread scheduling, memory management, and RPC stacks to the ARM cores of Intel's Mount Evans Infrastructure Processing Unit (IPU). The engineering is careful and the results are honest: without Wave's PCIe latency mitigations, offloaded workloads degrade by 350%.
  We argue that this 350% degradation is not an engineering problem to be optimized away but a diagnostic symptom of a deeper architectural issue: Wave's communication model is Forward-In-Time-Only (FITO). Every interaction between host and SmartNIC is a unidirectional message -- event forward, decision back -- creating a temporal vulnerability window in which decisions can become stale before they are enforced. Wave's entire optimization stack (write-combining page table entries, prestaging, prefetching, atomic transaction abort) exists to hide or tolerate this window.
  We apply the FITO diagnostic to Wave's architecture systematically, identify the category mistake it inherits from Lamport's happened-before and Shannon's channel model, and show how Open Atomic Ethernet's bilateral swap primitive -- implemented on the same Intel IPU hardware -- dissolves the latency, atomicity, and timeout problems without engineering around them. The SmartNIC is the right location for resource management; what is missing is the right communication primitive at that location.

### [287] [Committee Configuration Optimization for Parallel Byzantine Consensus in a Trusted Execution Environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14445)
*Yifei Xie,Btissam Er-Rahmadi,Xiao Chen,Tiejun Ma,Jane Hillston*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文针对可信并行BFT协议中委员会配置随机分配导致性能下降的问题，提出了基于混合整数规划的委员会配置优化（CCO）模型，通过考虑通信延迟和节点故障率来最小化交易延迟，实验表明在正常操作和可信硬件故障回退场景下吞吐量分别提升15%和21%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于委员会分片的并行BFT协议提升了可扩展性但削弱了安全性。现有方法通过集成可信执行环境（TEE）增强安全性，但委员会配置仍依赖随机分配，导致交易性能下降。因此需要一种优化驱动的委员会配置方法来提升可信并行BFT系统的性能。

Method: 提出基于混合整数规划的委员会配置优化（CCO）模型，综合考虑通信延迟和节点故障率两个关键因素，确定最优委员会配置方案。该模型旨在正常操作场景和可信硬件故障场景下均能最小化交易延迟。将CCO模型集成到可信并行BFT协议中，并在微软虚拟机上进行了实现和评估。

Result: 在微软虚拟机上的实验评估显示，相比随机分配方法，CCO模型在正常操作场景下交易吞吐量提升15%，在可信硬件故障回退场景下吞吐量提升21%，证明了优化驱动的委员会配置在可信并行BFT系统中的有效性。

Conclusion: 优化驱动的委员会配置方法能够有效提升可信并行BFT系统的交易性能。通过数学建模和优化方法配置委员会，相比传统的随机分配方法，能够在保证安全性的同时显著提高系统的吞吐量和效率。

Abstract: Parallel Byzantine Fault Tolerant (BFT) protocols based on committee-based sharding improve scalability but weaken safety since smaller node groups are responsible for consensus. Recent approaches integrate trusted execution environments (TEEs) into parallel BFT frameworks to enhance safety. While the scalability and safety issues are addressed by trusted parallel BFT, existing committee configuration methods often rely on randomized assignment, which can degrade performance. This paper proposes a committee configuration optimization (CCO) model based on mixed integer programming to improve transaction performance for trusted parallel BFT. The model considers communication delays and node failure rates to determine an optimal committee configuration that minimizes transaction latency under both normal operations and scenarios of trusted hardware failures. We integrate CCO into a trusted parallel BFT protocol and evaluate the performance on Microsoft virtual machines. Experimental results demonstrate 15% and 21% improved transaction throughput under normal operations and fallback process, respectively, highlighting the benefits of optimization-driven committee configuration in trusted parallel BFT systems.

</details>


### [288] [Covariance-Guided Resource Adaptive Learning for Efficient Edge Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14577)
*Ahmad N. L. Nabhaan,Zaki Sukma,Rakandhiya D. Rachmanto,Muhammad Husni Santriaji,Byungjin Cho,Arief Setyanto,In Kee Kim*

TL;DR: CORAL是一种在线优化方法，通过距离协方差统计硬件设置与性能指标间的非线性依赖关系，无需离线性能分析即可在边缘设备上发现接近最优的深度学习推理配置，实现吞吐量-功耗协同优化。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CORAL在线优化方法，利用距离协方差统计捕获硬件设置（如DVFS和并发级别）与性能指标之间的非线性依赖关系。将挑战明确表述为吞吐量-功耗协同优化问题，以同时满足功耗预算和吞吐量目标。

Result: 在两款NVIDIA Jetson设备上评估了三个从轻量级到重量级的目标检测模型。在单目标场景中，CORAL达到了穷举搜索找到的最优性能的96%-100%。在严格的 双约束场景中（基线方法失败或超出功耗预算），CORAL能够在线持续找到合适的配置，且探索开销极小。

Conclusion: CORAL成功解决了边缘设备深度学习推理配置优化问题，无需离线性能分析即可在线发现接近最优的配置，在单目标和严格双约束场景下均表现出色，为边缘设备上的深度学习推理提供了一种高效实用的配置优化方案。

Abstract: For deep learning inference on edge devices, hardware configurations achieving the same throughput can differ by 2$\times$ in power consumption, yet operators often struggle to find the efficient ones without exhaustive profiling. Existing approaches often rely on inefficient static presets or require expensive offline profiling that must be repeated for each new model or device. To address this problem, we present CORAL, an online optimization method that discovers near-optimal configurations without offline profiling. CORAL leverages distance covariance to statistically capture the non-linear dependencies between hardware settings, e.g., DVFS and concurrency levels, and performance metrics. Unlike prior work, we explicitly formulate the challenge as a throughput-power co-optimization problem to satisfy power budgets and throughput targets simultaneously. We evaluate CORAL on two NVIDIA Jetson devices across three object detection models ranging from lightweight to heavyweight. In single-target scenarios, CORAL achieves 96% $\unicode{x2013}$ 100% of the optimal performance found by exhaustive search. In strict dual-constraint scenarios where baselines fail or exceed power budgets, CORAL consistently finds proper configurations online with minimal exploration.

### [289] [Towards an Adaptive Runtime System for Cloud-Native HPC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14630)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验证明：速率感知负载均衡显著提升了云上异构CPU和GPU实例的应用性能；Charm++的核心原则有效缓解了网络竞争和处理器性能可变性导致的性能下降；扩展的资源管理框架成功支持GPU和CPU spot实例，实现了低中断开销。

Conclusion: 本研究为HPC应用在云环境中的高效、弹性和低成本运行提供了完整框架，证明了异步消息驱动范式能够有效弥合传统HPC应用与动态云基础设施之间的差距，为HPC与云计算的融合提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: The ongoing convergence of HPC and cloud computing presents a fundamental challenge: HPC applications, designed for static and homogeneous supercomputers, are ill-suited for the dynamic, heterogeneous, and volatile nature of the cloud. Traditional parallel programming models like MPI struggle to leverage key cloud advantages, such as resource elasticity and low-cost spot instances, while also failing to address challenges like performance variability and processor heterogeneity. This paper demonstrates how the asynchronous, message-driven paradigm of the Charm++ parallel runtime system can bridge this gap. We present a set of tools and strategies that enable HPC applications to run efficiently and resiliently on dynamic cloud infrastructure across both CPU and GPU resources. Our work makes two key contributions. First, we demonstrate that rate-aware load balancing in Charm++ improves performance for applications running on heterogeneous CPU and GPU instances on the cloud. We further demonstrate how core Charm++ principles mitigate performance degradation from common cloud challenges like network contention and processor performance variability, which are exacerbated by the tightly coupled, globally synchronized nature of many science and engineering applications. Second, we extend an existing resource management framework to support GPU and CPU spot instances with minimal interruption overhead. Together, these contributions provide a robust framework for adapting HPC applications to achieve efficient, resilient, and cost-effective performance on the cloud.

### [290] [Can you keep a secret? A new protocol for sender-side enforcement of causal message delivery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14690)
*Yan Tong,Nathan Liittschwager,Lindsey Kuper*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了Cykas协议，一种新的发送端因果消息传递方法，通过允许消息急切发送并约束接收者行为，解决了传统发送端方法过于保守的问题，在长运行任务场景下性能优势明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的因果消息传递协议存在两种方式：接收端方法需要消息元数据开销，而发送端方法虽然避免了元数据开销但过于保守（不必要地延迟消息发送）。需要一种既能保持发送端方法的低开销优势，又能减少保守性的新协议。

Method: 提出Cykas协议，采用发送端因果传递执行方式。与传统发送端方法不同，Cykas允许消息急切发送（eager sending），同时对接收者的行为进行约束。使用Rust语言实现该协议，并利用Stateright实现级模型检查器验证实现的安全性和活性属性。

Result: 实验结果表明，在涉及长运行任务的应用中，Cykas相比传统发送端方法具有性能优势。Cykas使长运行任务能够更早开始和结束，从而缩短整体执行时间。协议的安全性和活性已通过模型检查验证。

Conclusion: Cykas协议成功地在发送端实现了高效的因果消息传递，通过创新的急切发送和接收者约束机制，在保持低开销的同时减少了传统方法的保守性，为长运行任务的分布式应用提供了更好的性能表现。

Abstract: Protocols for causal message delivery are widely used in distributed systems. Traditionally, causal delivery can be enforced either on the message sender's side or on the receiver's side. The traditional sender-side approach avoids the message metadata overhead of the receiver-side approach, but is more conservative than necessary. We present Cykas ("Can you keep a secret?"), a new protocol for sender-side enforcement of causal delivery that sidesteps the conservativeness of the traditional sender-side approach by allowing eager sending of messages and constraining the behavior of their recipients. We implemented the Cykas protocol in Rust and checked the safety and liveness of our implementation using the Stateright implementation-level model checker. Our experiments show that for applications involving long-running jobs, Cykas has a performance advantage: Cykas lets long-running jobs start (and end) earlier, leading to shorter overall execution time compared to the traditional sender-side approach.

</details>


### [291] [Token Coherence: Adapting MESI Cache Protocols to Minimize Synchronization Overhead in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15183)
*Vladyslav Parakhin*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文将多智能体LLM系统的同步开销问题映射到多处理器缓存一致性问题，提出Artifact Coherence System (ACS)，通过MESI协议的惰性失效机制将同步开销从O(n×S×|D|)降至O((n+W)×|D|)，在仿真中实现84%-95%的token节省。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM编排中，朴素的广播同步机制导致三重乘法级开销(O(n×S×|D|))，严重制约系统扩展性。作者认为这种开销是全状态重广播的结构性残留，而非多智能体协调的固有属性。

Method: 将LLM多智能体系统的同步问题形式化映射到共享内存多处理器的缓存一致性问题，借鉴MESI协议提出Artifact Coherence System (ACS)。证明了Token Coherence Theorem：惰性失效在S>n+W(d_i)条件下将开销从O(n×S×|D|)降至O((n+W)×|D|)。使用TLA+验证协议正确性，探索约2400个状态。

Result: 仿真实验显示token节省率：V=0.05时95.0%±1.3%，V=0.10时92.3%±1.4%，V=0.25时88.3%±1.5%，V=0.50时84.2%±1.3%，均超越定理下界。即使在V=0.9高变异率下仍保持约81%节省率。

Conclusion: 多智能体LLM系统的同步开销爆炸问题可通过缓存一致性技术有效解决，ACS系统在保证单写入者安全、单调版本控制和有限陈旧性的前提下，显著降低同步成本。提供了与LangGraph、CrewAI和AutoGen集成的Python参考实现。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM orchestration incurs synchronization costs scaling as O(n x S x |D|) in agents, steps, and artifact size under naive broadcast -- a regime I term broadcast-induced triply-multiplicative overhead. I argue this pathology is a structural residue of full-state rebroadcast, not an inherent property of multi-agent coordination.
  The central claim: synchronization cost explosion in LLM multi-agent systems maps with formal precision onto the cache coherence problem in shared-memory multiprocessors, and MESI-protocol invalidation transfers to artifact synchronization under minimal structural modification.
  I construct the Artifact Coherence System (ACS) and prove the Token Coherence Theorem: lazy invalidation attenuates cost by at least S/(n + W(d_i)) when S > n + W(d_i), converting O(n x S x |D|) to O((n + W) x |D|). A TLA+-verified protocol enforces single-writer safety, monotonic versioning, and bounded staleness across ~2,400 explored states.
  Simulation across four workload configurations yields token savings of 95.0% +/- 1.3% at V=0.05, 92.3% +/- 1.4% at V=0.10, 88.3% +/- 1.5% at V=0.25, and 84.2% +/- 1.3% at V=0.50 -- each exceeding the theorem's conservative lower bounds. Savings of ~81% persist at V=0.9, contrary to the predicted collapse threshold.
  Contributions: (1) formal MESI-to-artifact state mapping; (2) Token Coherence Theorem as savings lower bound; (3) TLA+-verified protocol with three proven invariants; (4) characterization of conditional artifact access semantics resolving the always-read objection; (5) reference Python implementation integrating with LangGraph, CrewAI, and AutoGen via thin adapter layers.

</details>


### [292] [Multi-Objective Load Balancing for Heterogeneous Edge-Based Object Detection Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15400)
*Daghash K. Alqahtani,Maria A. Rodriguez,Muhammad Aamir Cheema,Adel N. Toosi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文针对异构边缘计算环境中的目标检测系统，提出了一种多目标负载均衡方法，通过两阶段决策机制在准确率、延迟和能耗之间实现有效权衡，实验显示可降低50%能耗和80%延迟，准确率损失不超过10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物联网和智能应用的快速发展导致分布式传感设备生成的数据激增，边缘计算通过将计算推近数据源（如资源受限的单板计算机）来管理这些数据。然而，硬件和软件的异构性使得有效的负载平衡极具挑战性，尤其是在请求强度和场景复杂度随时间波动的动态环境中。

Method: 提出一种面向异构边缘目标检测系统的多目标负载均衡方法，采用两阶段决策机制：第一阶段进行准确率感知过滤，识别出在可接受准确率范围内的设备-模型候选对；第二阶段在预期延迟和能耗上应用加权和评分函数，选择最终执行目标。该方法考虑了多个设备-模型对的不同准确率、延迟和能耗配置文件。

Result: 在真实世界数据集上进行了广泛实验，与广泛使用的基线策略进行对比。结果表明，所提出的多目标负载均衡方法将能耗降低了一半（50%），端到端延迟减少了80%，而相对于以准确率为中心的基线，检测准确率仅出现轻微下降，降幅不超过10%。

Conclusion: 该研究成功证明了在异构边缘计算环境中，通过多目标负载均衡可以有效权衡准确率、延迟和能耗三个关键指标。所提出的两阶段决策机制能够在保持可接受准确率的前提下，显著降低系统的能耗和延迟，为边缘计算环境下的目标检测系统提供了一种高效的资源管理解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid proliferation of the Internet of Things (IoT) and smart applications has led to a surge in data generated by distributed sensing devices. Edge computing is a mainstream approach to managing this data by pushing computation closer to the data source, typically onto resource-constrained devices such as single-board computers (SBCs). In such environments, the unavoidable heterogeneity of hardware and software makes effective load balancing particularly challenging. In this paper, we propose a multi-objective load balancing method tailored to heterogeneous, edge-based object detection systems. We study a setting in which multiple device-model pairs expose distinct accuracy, latency, and energy profiles, while both request intensity and scene complexity fluctuate over time. To handle this dynamically varying environment, our approach uses a two-stage decision mechanism: it first performs accuracy-aware filtering to identify suitable device-model candidates that provide accuracy within the acceptable range, and then applies a weighted-sum scoring function over expected latency and energy consumption to select the final execution target. We evaluate the proposed load balancer through extensive experiments on real-world datasets, comparing against widely used baseline strategies. The results indicate that the proposed multi-objective load balancing method halves energy consumption and achieves an 80% reduction in end-to-end latency, while incurring only a modest, up to 10%, decrease in detection accuracy relative to an accuracy-centric baseline.
