### [293] [Cuckoo-GPU: Accelerating Cuckoo Filters on Modern GPUs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15486)
*Tim Dortmann,Markus Vieth,Bertil Schmidt*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了Cuckoo-GPU，一个面向GPU的高性能开源Cuckoo过滤器库，通过采用无锁架构和基于广度优先搜索的驱逐启发式策略，在高负载插入时最小化线程分歧并限制顺序内存访问，在NVIDIA GH200和RTX PRO 6000 Blackwell系统上实现了比GQF（TCF）高出高达378倍（4.1倍）的插入吞吐量、6倍（34.7倍）的查询吞吐量和258倍（107倍）的删除吞吐量，证明了动态AMQ结构可以在现代加速器上部署而不会牺牲性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近似成员查询（AMQ）结构对于数据库、网络和生物信息学中的高吞吐量系统至关重要。虽然Bloom过滤器速度快，但不支持删除操作。现有的基于GPU的动态替代方案，如Two-Choice Filter（TCF）和GPU Quotient Filter（GQF），虽然支持删除操作但会导致严重的性能损失。因此需要一种既能支持删除操作又能保持高性能的GPU-based动态AMQ结构。

Method: 提出了Cuckoo-GPU，一个开源的高性能GPU Cuckoo过滤器库。设计特点包括：1）不优先考虑缓存局部性，而是利用Cuckoo哈希固有的随机访问模式来充分饱和全局内存带宽；2）基于原子比较交换操作构建无锁架构；3）采用新颖的基于广度优先搜索的驱逐启发式策略，在高负载插入时最小化线程分歧并限制顺序内存访问。在NVIDIA GH200（HBM3）和RTX PRO 6000 Blackwell（GDDR7）系统上进行评估。

Result: 在相同硬件上，Cuckoo-GPU的插入、查询和删除吞吐量分别比GQF（TCF）高出高达378倍（4.1倍）、6倍（34.7倍）和258倍（107倍）；相比最快的多线程CPU-based Cuckoo过滤器实现，实现了高达350倍的加速；其查询吞吐量与仅追加的GPU-based Blocked Bloom过滤器相当，弥合了仅追加和动态AMQ结构之间的性能差距。

Conclusion: Cuckoo-GPU成功证明了动态AMQ结构可以在现代加速器上部署而不会牺牲性能，其查询吞吐量可以与仅追加的GPU-based Blocked Bloom过滤器相媲美。该工作为高性能动态近似成员查询数据结构在GPU上的实现提供了新的设计思路，展示了在GPU上实现高效动态数据结构的可行性。

Abstract: Approximate Membership Query (AMQ) structures are essential for high-throughput systems in databases, networking, and bioinformatics. While Bloom filters offer speed, they lack support for deletions. Existing GPU-based dynamic alternatives, such as the Two-Choice Filter (TCF) and GPU Quotient Filter (GQF), enable deletions but incur severe performance penalties. We present Cuckoo-GPU, an open-source, high-performance Cuckoo filter library for GPUs. Instead of prioritizing cache locality, Cuckoo-GPU embraces the inherently random access pattern of Cuckoo hashing to fully saturate global memory bandwidth. Our design features a lock-free architecture built on atomic compare-and-swap operations, paired with a novel breadth-first search-based eviction heuristic that minimizes thread divergence and bounds sequential memory accesses during high-load insertions. Evaluated on NVIDIA GH200 (HBM3) and RTX PRO 6000 Blackwell (GDDR7) systems, Cuckoo-GPU closes the performance gap between append-only and dynamic AMQ structures. It achieves insertion, query, and deletion throughputs up to 378x (4.1x), 6x (34.7x), and 258x (107x) higher than GQF (TCF) on the same hardware, respectively, and delivers up to a 350x speedup over the fastest available multi-threaded CPU-based Cuckoo filter implementation. Moreover, its query throughput rivals that of the append-only GPU-based Blocked Bloom filter - demonstrating that dynamic AMQ structures can be deployed on modern accelerators without sacrificing performance.

</details>

### [294] [Dynamic Sparse Attention: Access Patterns and Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13430)
*Noam Levy*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文研究了动态稀疏注意力（DSA）在推理服务中的系统级性能瓶颈，发现其KV缓存访问模式会导致严重的LL缓存缺失。为此提出了LL缓存预留系统和token粒度LRU淘汰策略，有效缓解了DSA模型的缓存局部性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态稀疏注意力通过仅计算top-k KV条目来降低带宽需求，但其token依赖的选择模式导致KV工作集碎片化、易变且难以预取，造成缓存局部性差和解码吞吐量下降。现有DSA实现存在服务效率瓶颈，需要系统级的优化方案。

Method: 1) 在多个开源骨干网络上实现轻量级索引器，支持DSA式选择并在自回归解码过程中记录每层的KV索引；2) 分析收集的数据，识别LL缓存缺失事件的瓶颈；3) 提出LL缓存预留系统，在解码步骤间保存KV tokens，并采用token粒度的LRU淘汰策略。

Result: 实验分析揭示了DSA骨干网络服务中的关键问题——大量阻塞式LL缓存缺失事件导致效率低下。所提出的LL缓存预留架构在多个DSA实现骨干网络上均展现出性能提升，有效改善了KV tokens的缓存局部性。

Conclusion: 本文系统性地分析了DSA服务的性能瓶颈并提出了解决方案，为现代推理平台上DSA的高效服务提供了架构支持。未来需要在架构和算法层面进一步探索，以持续优化DSA在推理系统中的表现。

Abstract: Dynamic sparse attention (DSA) reduces the per-token attention bandwidth by restricting computation to a top-k subset of cached key-value (KV) entries, but its token-dependent selection pattern introduces a system-level challenge: the KV working set is fragmented, volatile, and difficult to prefetch, which can translate into poor cache locality and stalled decode throughput. We study these effects by implementing a lightweight indexer for DSA-style selection on multiple open-source backbones and logging per-layer KV indices during autoregressive decoding. Our analysis shows a gap in serving DSA backbones - a potential for a high volume of blocking LL (last level) cache miss events, causing inefficiency; we propose a novel LL cache reservation system to save KV tokens in the LL cache between decode steps, combined with a token-granularity LRU eviction policy, and show on the data we collected how this architecture can benefit serving with DSA implemented on different backbones. Finally, we propose directions for future architectural and algorithmic exploration to improve serving of DSA on modern inference platforms.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CPCell框架，采用细粒度分层网格图和基于约束规划的布局布线协同优化方法。关键技术包括：Middle-of-Line布线、M0引脚使能、引脚可达性约束、加权多目标优化函数。为扩展至48个晶体管的规模，引入晶体管聚类、相同晶体管划分、布线下界收紧和提前终止等加速技术。

Result: 在单元级和模块级进行了全面研究，评估了不同GR和偏移参数的选择，量化了所提优化目标的收益，并分析了其对功耗、性能、面积和IR-drop的影响。实验证明该方法能有效生成高质量的标准单元版图。

Conclusion: CPCell框架成功解决了先进节点标准单元版图生成中的新挑战，支持任意GR和偏移参数，通过协同优化显著提升了版图质量，为后续模块级设计提供了更优的基础。

Abstract: Advanced nodes decouple contacted poly pitch (CPP) and lower-metal pitch to improve routability. We present CPCell, an efficient standard-cell layout generation framework, to support arbitrary gear ratio (GR) and offset parameters through a fine-grained layered grid graph and constraint-programming-based placement-routing co-optimization. Layout quality is improved via Middle-of-Line routing, M0 pin enablement, pin accessibility constraints and a weighted multi-objective formulation that jointly optimizes cell layouts. To scale to netlists with up to 48 transistors, we incorporate acceleration techniques including transistor clustering, identical transistor partitioning, routing lower bound tightening and early termination strategies. Comprehensive cell-level and block-level studies are conducted to evaluate GR and offset choices, quantify the benefits of the proposed objectives and assess their impact on power, performance, area and IR-drop outcomes.

### [296] [Retrieve, Schedule, Reflect: LLM Agents for Chip QoR Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13767)
*Yikang ouyang,Yang Luo,Dongsheng Zuo,Yuzhe Ma*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于智能体的大语言模型框架，用于自动化芯片设计中的优化调度。该框架通过检索增强生成(RAG)将自然语言专业知识表达为搜索树，并结合帕累托驱动的QoR反馈进行语言反思，实现了与EDA工具的直接交互。实验表明，相比强化学习等黑盒搜索方法，该框架在时序改善上提升10%，功耗和面积更优，且加速超过4倍，QoR达到人类专家水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代芯片设计需要在严格的时间上市约束下对时序、功耗和面积进行多目标优化。尽管EDA工具集成了强大的优化算法，但实现高QoR依赖于有效的长视界调度，这严重依赖人工专家干预。现有方法缺乏自动化解决方案，亟需一种能够自动化芯片设计优化调度的方法。

Method: 提出了一个智能体LLM框架，通过直接与EDA工具交互来调度芯片优化。该智能体通过检索增强生成(RAG)将自然语言专业知识表达为搜索树进行grounding。进一步通过语言反思引入帕累托驱动的QoR反馈来提升调度质量。框架支持用自然语言表达的自定义任务。

Result: 与强化学习等黑盒搜索方法相比，该框架实现了10%更高的时序改善，同时功耗和面积更低，加速超过4倍。优化后的QoR与人类专家实现的水平相当。支持自然语言表达的自定义任务，可实现偏好的QoR权衡。

Conclusion: 该智能体LLM框架成功实现了芯片设计优化调度的自动化，在性能上超越了现有的黑盒搜索方法，达到了人类专家水平。框架的代码和芯片设计数据已公开，促进了该领域的进一步研究和发展。

Abstract: Modern chip design requires multi-objective optimization of timing, power, and area under stringent time-to-market constraints. Although powerful optimization algorithms are integrated into EDA tools, achieving high QoR hinges on effective long-horizon scheduling, which relies heavily on manual expert intervention. To address this issue and automate chip design, we propose an agentic LLM framework that schedules chip optimizations through direct interaction with EDA tools. The agent is grounded in natural language expertise expressed as a search tree through retrieval-augmented generation (RAG). We further improve scheduling quality with Pareto-driven QoR feedback through language reflection. Experimental results show that, compared with black-box search methods such as reinforcement learning, our framework achieves 10% greater timing improvement while consuming less power and area, with more than 4x speedup. The post-optimization QoR is also comparable to that achieved by human experts. Finally, the agent supports customized tasks expressed in natural language, enabling preferential QoR trade-offs. The code and chip design data will be publicly available at https://github.com/YiKangOY/Open-LLM-ECO.

### [297] [Exploiting temporal parallelism for LSTM Autoencoder acceleration on FPGA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13982)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于FPGA的新型加速器，采用数据流架构，利用时间并行性来实现序列中不同时间步的多层并发处理，突破了传统顺序依赖的限制。

Result: 在Zynq UltraScale+ MPSoC FPGA上实现的四种代表性LSTM-AE模型实验表明，相比Intel Xeon Gold 5218R CPU，延迟加速高达79.6倍，每时间步能耗降低高达1722倍；相比NVIDIA V100 GPU，延迟加速高达18.2倍，每时间步能耗降低高达59.3倍。同时展现了更优的网络深度可扩展性。

While previous work has explored FPGA-based acceleration for LSTM networks, efforts have typically focused on optimizing a single LSTM layer at a time. We introduce a novel FPGA-based accelerator using a dataflow architecture that exploits temporal parallelism for concurrent multi-layer processing of different timesteps within sequences. Experimental evaluations on four representative LSTM-AE models with varying widths and depths, implemented on a Zynq UltraScale+ MPSoC FPGA, demonstrate significant advantages over CPU (Intel Xeon Gold 5218R) and GPU (NVIDIA V100) implementations. Our accelerator achieves latency speedups up to 79.6x vs. CPU and 18.2x vs. GPU, alongside energy-per-timestep reductions of up to 1722x vs. CPU and 59.3x vs. GPU. These results, including superior network depth scalability, highlight our approach's potential for high-performance, real-time, power-efficient LSTM-AE-based anomaly detection on FPGAs.

Abstract: Space missions increasingly deploy high-fidelity sensors that produce data volumes exceeding onboard buffering and downlink capacity. We use Vitis AI (AMD DPU) and Vitis HLS to implement inference, quantify throughput and energy, and expose toolchain and architectural constraints relevant to deployment. Vitis AI achieves up to 34.16$\times$ higher inference rate than the embedded ARM CPU baseline, while custom HLS designs reach up to 5.4$\times$ speedup and add support for operators (e.g., sigmoids, 3D layers) absent in the DPU. For these implementations, measured MPSoC inference power spans 1.5-6.75 W, reducing energy per inference versus CPU execution in all use cases. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出三种机器学习引导的架构策略：（1）Pythia——基于强化学习的片上缓存数据预取器；（2）Hermes——基于感知器学习的多级缓存层次结构片外预测器；（3）Sibyl——基于强化学习的混合存储系统数据放置策略。

Abstract: Despite the data-rich environment in which memory systems of modern computing platforms operate, many state-of-the-art architectural policies employed in the memory system rely on static, human-designed heuristics that fail to truly adapt to the workload and system behavior via principled learning methodologies. In this article, we propose a fundamentally different design approach: using lightweight and practical machine learning (ML) methods to enable adaptive, data-driven control throughout the memory hierarchy.
  We present three ML-guided architectural policies: (1) Pythia, a reinforcement learning-based data prefetcher for on-chip caches, (2) Hermes, a perceptron learning-based off-chip predictor for multi-level cache hierarchies, and (3) Sibyl, a reinforcement learning-based data placement policy for hybrid storage systems. Our evaluation shows that Pythia, Hermes, and Sibyl significantly outperform the best-prior human-designed policies, while incurring modest hardware overheads. Collectively, this article demonstrates that integrating adaptive learning into memory subsystems can lead to intelligent, self-optimizing architectures that unlock performance and efficiency gains beyond what is possible with traditional human-designed approaches.

### [301] [SkipOPU: An FPGA-based Overlay Processor for Large Language Models with Dynamically Allocated Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14785)
*Zicheng He,Anhao Zhao,Xiaoyu Shen,Chen Wu,Lei He*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了SkipOPU，一种基于FPGA的覆盖处理器，通过动态分配计算资源来优化大语言模型推理效率，在带宽效率上比GPU和其他FPGA加速器提升1.23x-3.83x，并减少高达25.4%的KV存储开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型参数量快速增长导致推理效率成为关键瓶颈。虽然动态计算分配技术可以通过利用不同token和层的不均匀贡献来减少冗余计算，但现有硬件平台主要针对均匀、静态执行进行优化，难以高效支持动态推理模式。

Method: 提出三个关键技术：（1）将非线性模块中的归约操作与逐元素计算解耦并增量执行，实现与相邻线性操作融合以隐藏延迟；（2）设计支持浮点-定点混合执行的PE阵列，引入DSP过打包技术最大化硬件利用率；（3）开发主动式片上KV历史缓冲区，利用剪枝token的跨层KV不变性消除不规则HBM访问。

Result: 在AMD U280 FPGA上实现，相比GPU和其他FPGA加速器，在动态计算分配的LLM推理中带宽效率提升1.23x-3.83x，在不同序列长度下可减少高达25.4%的KV存储开销。

Conclusion: SkipOPU成功解决了现有硬件平台难以高效支持动态推理模式的问题，通过创新的架构设计显著提升了LLM推理的带宽效率并降低了存储开销，为动态计算分配在LLM中的实际部署提供了有效的硬件解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable performance across a wide range of tasks, but their inference efficiency remains a critical bottleneck due to rapidly growing parameters. Recent advances in dynamic computation allocation address this challenge by exploiting the highly uneven contributions of different tokens and layers, enabling selective execution that significantly reduces redundant computation while preserving model accuracy. However, existing hardware platforms and accelerators are primarily optimized for uniform, static execution, limiting their ability to efficiently support such dynamic inference patterns. In this work, we propose SkipOPU, an FPGA-based overlay processor that dynamically allocates computation across tokens and layers with high flexibility through a lightweight routing mechanism. First, we decouple reduction operations from element-wise computation in nonlinear modules and perform reductions incrementally, which enables both stages to be fused with adjacent linear operations (router or matrix multiplication) for effective latency hiding. Second, motivated by asymmetric sensitivity to numerical precision between activation and weight, we design a PE array that efficiently supports float-fixed hybrid execution. A novel DSP overpacking technique is introduced to maximize hardware utilization while minimizing resource overhead. Finally, we develop a proactive on-chip KV history buffer that exploits cross-layer KV invariance of pruned tokens, eliminating irregular HBM accesses during decoding and supplementing off-chip bandwidth through high-locality on-chip reuse. Experimental results demonstrate that SkipOPU on an AMD U280 FPGA outperforms GPU and other FPGA-based accelerators by 1.23x-3.83x in bandwidth efficiency for LLMs inference with dynamic computation allocation and can reduce up to 25.4% KV storage overhead across varying sequence lengths.

</details>

Method: 提出bitSMM加速器，采用位串行脉动阵列架构，核心为位串行乘累加（MAC）单元阵列。支持运行时配置1-16位操作数精度，评估了两种MAC变体：基于Booth编码的架构和带校正的标准二进制乘法架构。使用SystemVerilog实现，在AMD ZCU104 FPGA以及asap7和nangate45工艺设计套件上进行ASIC物理实现验证。

Abstract: Neural-network (NN) inference is increasingly present on-board spacecraft to reduce downlink bandwidth and enable timely decision making. However, the power and reliability constraints of space missions limit the applicability of many state-of-the-art NN accelerators. This paper presents bitSMM, a bit-serial matrix multiplication accelerator built around a systolic array of bit-serial multiply--accumulate (MAC) units. The design supports runtime-configurable operand precision from 1 to 16 bits and evaluates two MAC variants: a Booth-inspired architecture and a standard binary multiplication with correction architecture. We implement bitSMM in [System]Verilog and evaluate it on an AMD ZCU104 FPGA and through ASIC physical implementation using the asap7 and nangate45 process design kits. On the FPGA, bitSMM achieves up to 19.2~GOPS and 2.973~GOPS/W, and in asap7 it achieves up to 73.22~GOPS, 552~GOPS/mm$^2$, and 40.8~GOPS/W.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在计算密集型预填充阶段和内存带宽受限的解码阶段存在不对称性。混合Mamba-Transformer模型继承了这种不对称性，同时引入了状态空间模型（SSM）递归和逐元素运算，这些操作在以矩阵乘法为中心的加速器上映射效率低下，导致性能瓶颈，说明同构架构无法满足所有需求。

Method: 提出DUET disaggregated accelerator，将预填充和解码阶段分配到专用硬件包：预填充包利用脉动阵列小芯片和片外存储器进行高效大矩阵乘法和长序列SSM计算；解码包利用向量单元阵列和高带宽片内存储器加速逐token的SSM和向量-矩阵乘法。两种架构均可运行时配置以支持混合Mamba和注意力层的模型。

Result: 在Nemotron-H-56B、Zamba2-7B和Llama3-8B模型以及四种工作负载上的评估显示，DUET相比B200 GPU实现了4倍更快的首token时间（TTFT）、1.4倍更高的吞吐量以及1.5倍更低的token间延迟。

Conclusion: 通过针对预填充和解码阶段采用异构分离架构，DUET有效解决了混合Mamba-Transformer模型在传统同构加速器上的性能瓶颈，为未来大语言模型加速器设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language models operate in distinct compute-bound prefill followed by memory bandwidth-bound decode phases. Hybrid Mamba-Transformer models inherit this asymmetry while adding state space model (SSM) recurrences and element-wise operations that map poorly to matmul-centric accelerators. This mismatch causes performance bottlenecks, showing that a homogeneous architecture cannot satisfy all requirements. We introduce DUET, a disaggregated accelerator that assigns prefill and decode phases to specialized packages. The Prefill package utilizes systolic array chiplets with off-package memory for efficient large matrix multiplications and long-sequence SSMs. The Decode package utilizes vector-unit arrays with high-bandwidth in-package memory to accelerate token-by-token SSM and vector-matrix multiplications. Both architectures are runtime-configurable to support hybrid models with mixed Mamba and attention layers. Evaluations on Nemotron-H-56B, Zamba2-7B, and Llama3-8B across four workloads show that DUET achieves 4x faster time to first token, 1.4x higher throughput, and 1.5x lower time between tokens over the B200 GPU.

</details>


### [304] [Co-Design of Memory-Storage Systems for Workload Awareness with Interpretable Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15571)
*Jay Sarkar,Vamsi Pavan Rayaprolu,Abhijeet Bhalerao*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于机器学习的协同设计框架，用于优化固态存储（SSD）中的错误管理子系统，该方法能够实现内存组件与固件算法的联合优化，并通过大规模数据中心SSD的验证，实现了持续的、数据驱动的架构改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态存储架构需要同时实现可靠性和性能优化，这要求将内存组件与固件架构的错误管理（EM）算法进行协同设计。随着密度和性能的提升，内存技术面临着固有的硅工艺自然变异问题，亟需一种能够综合考虑这些因素的建模和设计方法。

Method: 采用一种面向系统的机器学习方法和建模技术，利用统计可解释且直观可解释的机器学习算法，分析NAND内存组件与EM算法的交互。该框架在Flash转换抽象层上，通过综合的合成工作负载（包括压力测试和JEDEC标准）以及仿真工作负载（如YCSB等）进行评估，并在跨越多代内存和存储技术的数千个数据中心SSD上进行了泛化验证。

Result: 该协同设计框架成功应用于数千个数据中心SSD的评估，涵盖多代内存和存储技术。实验结果表明，该框架能够实现连续、整体、数据驱动的设计，促进架构的代际演进，并能够对EM-工作负载域进行表征学习，从而增强广泛工作负载下的架构设计空间优化。

Conclusion: 本文证明了机器学习驱动的协同设计框架能够有效支持SSD错误管理子系统的设计优化，通过表征学习技术增强了架构设计空间的探索能力，为实现持续的系统架构改进提供了一条可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Solid-state storage architectures based on NAND or emerging memory devices (SSD), are fundamentally architected and optimized for both reliability and performance. Achieving these simultaneous goals requires co-design of memory components with firmware-architected Error Management (EM) algorithms for density- and performance-scaled memory technologies. We describe a Machine Learning (ML) for systems methodology and modeling for co-designing the EM subsystem together with the natural variance inherent to scaled silicon process of memory components underlying SSD technology. The modeling analyzes NAND memory components and EM algorithms interacting with comprehensive suite of synthetic (stress-focused and JEDEC) and emulation (YCSB and similar) workloads across Flash Translation abstraction layers, by leveraging a statistically interpretable and intuitively explainable ML algorithm. The generalizable co-design framework evaluates several thousand datacenter SSDs spanning multiple generations of memory and storage technology. Consequently, the modeling framework enables continuous, holistic, data-driven design towards generational architectural advancements. We additionally demonstrate that the framework enables Representation Learning of the EM-workload domain for enhancement of the architectural design-space across broad spectrum of workloads.

</details>


### [305] [LEXI: Lossless Exponent Coding for Efficient Inter-Chiplet Communication in Hybrid LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15589)
*Miao Sun,Alish Kanani,Kaushik Shroff,Umit Ogras*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: LEXI是一种基于霍夫曼编码的无损指数压缩方案，通过利用BF16格式中指数流低香农熵的特性，在保持系统吞吐量和模型精度的前提下，将现代LLM的芯片间通信和端到端推理延迟分别降低33-45%和30-35%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据移动开销显著增加了最先进大语言模型(LLM)的推理延迟。这些模型普遍使用BF16格式进行稳定训练，而浮点标准为指数部分分配了8位。作者通过性能分析发现，指数流的香农熵低于3位，表明其具有高度的内在可压缩性，但目前这一压缩潜力未被充分利用。

Method: 提出LEXI——一种基于霍夫曼编码的新型无损指数压缩方案。该方法：(1)即时压缩激活和缓存；(2)在计算单元附近存储压缩后的权重以实现即时解压缩；(3)在片上网络路由器的入口和出口端口部署编解码器；(4)采用多通道LUT解码器维持最大链路带宽。该方案在GF 22 nm工艺下仅产生0.09%的面积和能耗开销。

Result: 在现代Jamba、Zamba和Qwen LLM上，基于同构芯粒架构的实现结果显示：芯片间通信延迟降低33-45%，端到端推理延迟降低30-35%，同时系统吞吐量和模型精度无损失。

Conclusion: LEXI成功证明了利用浮点数指数流的低熵特性进行无损压缩的可行性，为缓解LLM推理中的数据移动瓶颈提供了高效的硬件解决方案，在不牺牲性能和精度的情况下显著降低了通信和推理延迟。

Abstract: Data movement overheads increase the inference latency of state-of-the-art large language models (LLMs). These models commonly use the bfloat16 (BF16) format for stable training. Floating-point standards allocate eight bits to the exponent, but our profiling reveals that exponent streams exhibit fewer than 3 bits Shannon entropy, indicating high inherent compressibility. To exploit this potential, we propose LEXI, a novel lossless exponent compression scheme based on Huffman coding. LEXI compresses activations and caches on the fly while storing compressed weights for just-in-time decompression near compute, without sacrificing system throughput and model accuracy. The codecs at the ingress and egress ports of network-on-chip routers sustain the maximum link bandwidth via multi-lane LUT decoders, incurring only 0.09 percent area and energy overheads with GF 22 nm technology. LEXI reduces inter-chiplet communication and end-to-end inference latencies by 33-45 percent and 30-35 percent on modern Jamba, Zamba, and Qwen LLMs implemented on a homogeneous chiplet architecture.

</details>

### [306] [Human Attribution of Causality to AI Across Agency, Misuse, and Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13236)
*Maria Victoria Carro,David Lagnado*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过人类实验研究了在AI相关有害事件中，人们对因果责任归属的认知，发现AI代理程度、角色定位、开发者责任以及AI组件分解等因素会影响责任判断，为AI致害的责任框架设计提供了实证依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI相关事故频发且后果严重，确定造成不良后果的因果要素（即原因选择问题）是确立责任的关键第一步。现有研究缺乏对AI系统中因果责任感知的系统调查，特别是在涉及AI误用和不对齐的复杂因果链场景中。

Method: 研究者设计了人类受试者实验，构建了因果链结构场景，操纵AI代理程度（低/中/高）、角色互换（人类与AI角色对调）、引入开发者角色、以及将AI分解为大语言模型和代理组件等变量，考察参与者对因果关系、责任归咎、可预见性和反事实推理的判断。

Result: 研究发现四个核心结果：（1）AI代理程度中等或高时，参与者将更多因果责任归因于AI，但低代理程度下，人类即使时间上远离结果也承担更多责任，显示自主性效应；（2）互换人类与AI角色后，参与者始终认为人类更具因果性，即使两者执行相同行为；（3）开发者虽在因果链中位置遥远，但仍被判定为高因果性，这降低了人类用户而非AI的因果归因；（4）将AI分解后，代理组件被判定为更具因果性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了人们在AI误用和不对齐场景中如何感知AI的因果贡献，以及这些判断如何与用户和开发者的角色相互作用。这些发现可为AI致害的责任框架设计提供参考，并阐明直觉判断如何影响围绕现实AI事故的社会和政策讨论。

Abstract: AI-related incidents are becoming increasingly frequent and severe, ranging from safety failures to misuse by malicious actors. In such complex situations, identifying which elements caused an adverse outcome, the problem of cause selection, is a critical first step for establishing liability. This paper investigates folk perceptions of causal responsibility in causal chain structures when AI systems are involved in harmful outcomes. We conduct human experiments to examine judgments of causality, blame, foreseeability, and counterfactual reasoning. Our findings show that: (1) When AI agency was moderate (human sets the goal, AI determines the means) or high (AI sets the goal and the means), participants attributed greater causal responsibility to the AI. However, under low AI agency (where a human sets both a goal and means) participants assigned greater causal responsibility to the human despite their temporal distance from the outcome and despite both agents intended it, suggesting an effect of autonomy; (2) When we reversed roles between human and AI, participants consistently judged the human as more causal, even when both agents perform the same action; (3) The developer, despite being distant in the chain, was judged highly causal, reducing causal attributions to the human user but not to the AI; (4) Decomposing the AI into a large language model and an agentic component showed that the agentic part was judged as more causal in the chain. Overall, our research provides evidence on how people perceive the causal contribution of AI in both misuse and misalignment scenarios, and how these judgments interact with the roles of users and developers, key actors in assigning responsibility. These findings can inform the design of liability frameworks for AI-caused harms and shed light on how intuitive judgments shape social and policy debates surrounding real-world AI-related incidents.

</details>


### [307] [A Dual-Path Generative Framework for Zero-Day Fraud Detection in Banking Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13237)
*Nasim Abdirahman Ismail,Enis Karaarslan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个双路径生成框架，通过VAE实现低延迟（<50ms）实时异常检测，并利用WGAN-GP异步生成欺诈场景以应对“零日”攻击，同时结合Gumbel-Softmax处理离散数据，并通过触发式SHAP机制在保障实时性的同时满足GDPR的可解释性要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高频银行环境面临关键挑战：需要在低延迟欺诈检测与GDPR要求的可解释性之间取得平衡。传统基于规则和判别式模型难以应对“零日”攻击，原因在于极端的类别不平衡和缺乏历史先例。

Method: 提出双路径生成框架：1）采用变分自编码器（VAE）基于重建误差建立合法交易流形，确保<50ms推理延迟；2）并行使用异步Wasserstein GAN with Gradient Penalty（WGAN-GP）合成高熵欺诈场景以压力测试检测边界；3）集成Gumbel-Softmax估计器解决离散银行数据（如商户类别代码）的不可微问题；4）引入基于触发的可解释性机制，仅对高不确定性交易激活SHAP解释。

Result: 成功实现了实时异常检测与离线对抗训练的解耦，VAE确保了低延迟推理，WGAN-GP有效生成多样化欺诈场景，Gumbel-Softmax解决了离散数据处理问题，触发式SHAP机制在保持实时吞吐量的同时提供了可解释性。

Conclusion: 该框架有效解决了高频银行环境中低延迟欺诈检测与监管可解释性之间的矛盾，为应对“零日”攻击提供了可行方案，成功平衡了计算成本与实时性能要求。

Abstract: High-frequency banking environments face a critical trade-off between low-latency fraud detection and the regulatory explainability demanded by GDPR. Traditional rule-based and discriminative models struggle with "zero-day" attacks due to extreme class imbalance and the lack of historical precedents. This paper proposes a Dual-Path Generative Framework that decouples real-time anomaly detection from offline adversarial training. The architecture employs a Variational Autoencoder (VAE) to establish a legitimate transaction manifold based on reconstruction error, ensuring <50ms inference latency. In parallel, an asynchronous Wasserstein GAN with Gradient Penalty (WGAN-GP) synthesizes high-entropy fraudulent scenarios to stress-test the detection boundaries. Crucially, to address the non-differentiability of discrete banking data (e.g., Merchant Category Codes), we integrate a Gumbel-Softmax estimator. Furthermore, we introduce a trigger-based explainability mechanism where SHAP (Shapley Additive Explanations) is activated only for high-uncertainty transactions, reconciling the computational cost of XAI with real-time throughput requirements.

</details>


### [308] [Benchmarking Zero-Shot Reasoning Approaches for Error Detection in Solidity Smart Contracts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13239)
*Eduardo Sardenberg,Antonio José Grandson Busson,Daniel de Sousa Moraes,Sérgio Colcher*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了多种LLM在Solidity智能合约漏洞检测任务上的表现，发现思维链(CoT)和思维树(ToT)提示策略能显著提升召回率(达95-99%)，但会降低精确率；Claude 3 Opus在漏洞分类任务中以ToT提示取得最佳F1分数(90.8)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能合约在区块链系统中扮演核心角色，但其安全漏洞可能导致重大财务损失和信任危机。尽管LLM为自动化漏洞检测带来了新机遇，但不同提示策略和模型选择在实际场景中的有效性尚不明确，亟需系统性评估。

Method: 构建包含400个智能合约的平衡数据集，设计两个任务：(i)错误检测（二分类判断合约是否存在漏洞）；(ii)错误分类（将预测问题归类到特定漏洞类别）。评估多个前沿LLM，采用零样本提示策略，包括普通零样本、零样本思维链(CoT)和零样本思维树(ToT)。

Result: 在错误检测任务中，CoT和ToT显著提升召回率(接近95-99%)，但通常降低精确率，表明模型更敏感但产生更多假阳性。在错误分类任务中，Claude 3 Opus在ToT提示下获得最佳加权F1分数(90.8)，其CoT表现紧随其后。

Conclusion: 不同的提示策略对LLM智能合约漏洞检测性能影响显著：思维链和思维树策略能有效提高召回率，适合需要高敏感度的检测场景；Claude 3 Opus在漏洞分类任务中表现最佳，为智能合约安全审计提供了有价值的自动化工具参考。

Abstract: Smart contracts play a central role in blockchain systems by encoding financial and operational logic. Still, their susceptibility to subtle security flaws poses significant risks of financial loss and erosion of trust. LLMs create new opportunities for automating vulnerability detection, yet the effectiveness of different prompting strategies and model choices in real-world contexts remains uncertain. This paper evaluates state-of-the-art LLMs on Solidity smart contract analysis using a balanced dataset of 400 contracts under two tasks: (i) Error Detection, where the model performs binary classification to decide whether a contract is vulnerable, and (ii) Error Classification, where the model must assign the predicted issue to a specific vulnerability category. Models are evaluated using zero-shot prompting strategies, including zero-shot, zero-shot Chain-of-Thought (CoT), and zero-shot Tree-of-Thought (ToT). In the Error Detection task, CoT and ToT substantially increase recall (often approaching $\approx 95$--$99\%$), but typically reduce precision, indicating a more sensitive decision regime with more false positives. In the Error Classification task, Claude 3 Opus attains the best Weighted F1-score (90.8) under the ToT prompt, followed closely by its CoT.

</details>


### [309] [Think First, Diffuse Fast: Improving Diffusion Language Model Reasoning via Autoregressive Plan Conditioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13243)
*Earl J St Sauver*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出计划条件化方法，通过在扩散语言模型提示前添加AR模型生成的自然语言计划，显著提升多步推理性能，在GSM8K上提升11.6个百分点，达到与同规模AR模型相当的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散大语言模型在多步推理任务上持续表现不佳，作者假设这源于协调问题：自回归模型逐token构建连贯性，而扩散模型必须同时协调所有位置。

Method: 提出计划条件化方法，这是一种无需训练的技术：将AR模型生成的短计划（约100个token）预置到扩散模型的提示中，作为全局可见的冻结脚手架，使每个token位置从第一个去噪步骤就能关注到计划内容。

Result: 在GSM8K上，LLaDA-8B-Instruct准确率从75.6%提升至87.2%（+11.6pp），与同规模AR模型（LLaMA 3.1 8B，87.7%）相当；在HumanEval上提升12.8pp（37.2%至50.0%）。扩散模型收益是AR模型的2-10倍，验证了协调问题假设。消融实验显示模型遵循计划策略但对数值扰动鲁棒，注意力分析证实计划token在早期去噪阶段获得1.8倍超额关注。

Conclusion: 计划条件化成功解决了扩散模型的协调问题，成本极低（每题约0.002美元，延迟增加约2秒），推理稳定性极高（5个随机种子下标准差为零），验证了协调问题假设的有效性。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) generate text via iterative denoising but consistently underperform on multi-step reasoning. We hypothesize this gap stems from a coordination problem: AR models build coherence token-by-token, while diffusion models must coordinate all positions simultaneously. We propose plan conditioning, a training-free method that prepends a short (~100-token) natural-language plan from an AR model to the diffusion model's prompt. The plan serves as a frozen scaffold -- globally visible context that every token position can attend to from the first denoising step. On GSM8K, plan conditioning improves LLaDA-8B-Instruct from 75.6% to 87.2% (+11.6 percentage points), matching a same-size AR model (LLaMA 3.1 8B, 87.7%) despite a 6.4pp weaker baseline. On HumanEval, the gain is +12.8pp (37.2% to 50.0%), showing plans generalize to code. The same plans improve LLaMA by only +5.7pp on GSM8K and +1.3pp on HumanEval -- diffusion models benefit 2-10x more, supporting the coordination-problem hypothesis. Across 5 random seeds, plan-conditioned GSM8K accuracy has zero standard deviation, making diffusion inference highly stable. Ablations reveal the model follows plan strategy (wrong-strategy plans cause -16.3pp) but is robust to plan values (perturbed numbers: -1.1pp), and that planner quality has a sharp threshold: smaller Llama-class plans hurt (-1.6 to -6.8pp) while frontier plans provide the full lift. Attention analysis confirms the mechanism: plan tokens receive 1.8x excess attention during early denoising, declining to uniform as completion tokens solidify. Plan conditioning costs ~$0.002 per problem and adds ~2s of latency.

</details>


### [310] [Automating Document Intelligence in Statutory City Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13245)
*Lars Malmqvist,Robin Barber*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个集成AI系统，用于解决英国规划部门面临的立法冲突（规划法要求公开文件与数据保护法要求保护个人信息之间的矛盾），通过AI-in-the-Loop设计自动识别和修订个人信息、提取元数据并分析建筑图纸，在人工监督下降低行政负担并管理合规风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 英国规划部门面临规划法（要求公开申请文件）与数据保护法（要求保护个人信息）之间的立法冲突。处理大量文件的人工工作量繁重，导致规划官员将精力分散到行政任务上，并带来法律合规风险。

Method: 提出一个集成AI系统，采用AI-in-the-Loop（AI2L）设计：系统自动识别和修订个人信息、从规划文件中提取关键元数据、分析建筑图纸的特定特征；所有建议均需规划官员在现有软件中审查确认，无人工明确批准不执行任何操作；通过主动学习优先级机制从人工监督中持续学习改进性能。

Result: 系统目前在四个不同的英国地方当局进行试点；开发了初步的投资回报率（ROI）模型以量化潜在节省并确保合作伙伴参与；详细描述了系统设计、AI2L工作流程和试点中使用的评估框架。

Conclusion: 本工作提供了一个在公共部门环境中部署AI以减少行政负担和管理合规风险的案例研究，展示了AI-in-the-Loop方法在解决立法冲突和提升工作效率方面的潜力。

Abstract: UK planning authorities face a legislative conflict between the Planning Act, which mandates public access to application documents, and the Data Protection Act, which requires protection of personal information. This situation creates a manually intensive workload for processing large document volumes, diverting planning officers to administrative tasks and creating legal compliance risks. This paper presents an integrated AI system designed to address these challenges. The system automates the identification and redaction of personal information, extracts key metadata from planning documents, and analyzes architectural drawings for specified features. It operates with an AI-in-the-Loop (AI2L) design, presenting all suggestions for review and confirmation by planning officers directly within their existing software; no action is committed without explicit human approval. The system is designed to improve its performance over time by learning from this human oversight through active learning prioritization rather than autoapproval. The system is currently being piloted at four diverse UK local authorities. The paper details the system design, the AI2L workflow, and the evaluation framework used in the pilot. Additionally, it describes a preliminary Return on Investment (ROI) model developed to quantify potential savings and secure partner participation. This work provides a case study on deploying AI to reduce administrative burden and manage compliance risk in a public sector environment.

</details>


### [311] [Multi-Axis Trust Modeling for Interpretable Account Hijacking Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13246)
*Mohammad AL-Smadi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受伊斯兰圣训（Hadith）启发的多轴信任建模框架，用于检测账号劫持和内部威胁。通过将五个信任维度转化为26个可解释的行为特征，并结合时序特征，在CLUE-LDS数据集上实现了近乎完美的检测性能，在CERT数据集上也显著提升了检测效果。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将五个信任维度（长期诚信度adalah、行为精确度dabt、上下文连续性isnad、累积声誉、异常证据）转化为26个语义明确的行为特征；引入轻量级时序特征捕获信任信号的短期变化；使用随机森林分类器在滑动窗口上进行训练和评估。

Result: 在CLUE-LDS数据集上，随机森林模型在23,094个滑动窗口上达到近乎完美的检测性能，显著优于基于原始事件计数、最小统计基线和无监督异常检测的方法。时序特征带来适度但一致的性能提升。在CERT r6.2数据集上，500用户子集的ROC-AUC从0.776提升至0.844；在4,000用户的泄漏控制配置下，时序建模使ROC-AUC从0.627提升至0.715，PR-AUC从0.072提升至0.264。

Conclusion: 该框架证明了多轴信任建模方法的有效性和鲁棒性，时序特征与静态信任表示兼容且能带来一致的性能提升，特别是在具有极端类不平衡和稀疏恶意行为的挑战性场景中表现突出。

Abstract: This paper proposes a Hadith-inspired multi-axis trust modeling framework, motivated by a structurally analogous problem in classical Hadith scholarship: assessing the trustworthiness of information sources using interpretable, multidimensional criteria rather than a single anomaly score. We translate five trust axes - long-term integrity (adalah), behavioral precision (dabt), contextual continuity (isnad), cumulative reputation, and anomaly evidence - into a compact set of 26 semantically meaningful behavioral features for user accounts. In addition, we introduce lightweight temporal features that capture short-horizon changes in these trust signals across consecutive activity windows. We evaluate the framework on the CLUE-LDS cloud activity dataset with injected account hijacking scenarios. On 23,094 sliding windows, a Random Forest trained on the trust features achieves near-perfect detection performance, substantially outperforming models based on raw event counts, minimal statistical baselines, and unsupervised anomaly detection. Temporal features provide modest but consistent gains on CLUE-LDS, confirming their compatibility with the static trust representation. To assess robustness under more challenging conditions, we further evaluate the approach on the CERT Insider Threat Test Dataset r6.2, which exhibits extreme class imbalance and sparse malicious behavior. On a 500-user CERT subset, temporal features improve ROC-AUC from 0.776 to 0.844. On a leakage-controlled 4,000-user configuration, temporal modeling yields a substantial and consistent improvement over static trust features alone (ROC-AUC 0.627 to 0.715; PR-AUC 0.072 to 0.264).

### [312] [ILION: Deterministic Pre-Execution Safety Gates for Agentic AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13247)
*Florin Adrian Chitan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ILION，一种面向自主AI智能体的确定性执行门控系统，用于判断智能体提议的动作是否在其授权范围内。在ILION-Bench v2基准测试中，ILION实现F1=0.8515，比最佳商业基线Lakera Guard高出4.3个F1点，延迟仅143微秒，误报率低至7.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI智能体能够执行真实世界操作（文件系统操作、API调用、数据库修改、金融交易等），带来了现有内容审核基础设施无法解决的安全风险。当前文本安全系统仅评估语言内容的有害性（如暴力、仇恨言论、色情内容），在架构上不适用于评估智能体提议的动作是否在其授权操作范围内，存在根本性的任务不匹配问题。

Method: 提出ILION（智能逻辑身份操作网络），采用五级级联架构：(1)瞬态身份印记(TII)、(2)语义向量参考框架(SVRF)、(3)身份漂移控制(IDC)、(4)身份共振评分(IRS)和(5)共识否决层(CVL)。该系统无需统计训练或API依赖，无需标注数据，将智能体动作分类为BLOCK或ALLOW，产生完全可解释的裁决结果。

Result: 在ILION-Bench v2基准（380个测试场景，涵盖8个攻击类别，39%为高难度对抗案例）上评估，ILION实现F1=0.8515、精确率91.0%、误报率7.9%、平均延迟143微秒。与三个基线对比：Lakera Guard(F1=0.8087)、OpenAI Moderation API(F1=0.1188)、Llama Guard 3(F1=0.0105)，ILION比最佳商业基线高4.3个F1点，速度快2000倍，误报率低4倍。

Conclusion: 现有文本安全基础设施在智能体执行安全任务上系统性失效，原因在于根本性的任务不匹配。ILION为自主AI智能体提供了一种高效、确定性、可解释的安全执行门控解决方案，在性能和效率上均显著优于现有商业系统。

Abstract: The proliferation of autonomous AI agents capable of executing real-world actions - filesystem operations, API calls, database modifications, financial transactions - introduces a class of safety risk not addressed by existing content-moderation infrastructure. Current text-safety systems evaluate linguistic content for harm categories such as violence, hate speech, and sexual content; they are architecturally unsuitable for evaluating whether a proposed action falls within an agent's authorized operational scope. We present ILION (Intelligent Logic Identity Operations Network), a deterministic execution gate for agentic AI systems. ILION employs a five-component cascade architecture - Transient Identity Imprint (TII), Semantic Vector Reference Frame (SVRF), Identity Drift Control (IDC), Identity Resonance Score (IRS) and Consensus Veto Layer (CVL) - to classify proposed agent actions as BLOCK or ALLOW without statistical training or API dependencies. The system requires zero labeled data, operates in sub-millisecond latency, and produces fully interpretable verdicts. We evaluate ILION on ILION-Bench v2, a purpose-built benchmark of 380 test scenarios across eight attack categories with 39% hard-difficulty adversarial cases and a held-out development split. ILION achieves F1 = 0.8515, precision = 91.0%, and a false positive rate of 7.9% at a mean latency of 143 microseconds. Comparative evaluation against three baselines - Lakera Guard (F1 = 0.8087), OpenAI Moderation API (F1 = 0.1188), and Llama Guard 3 (F1 = 0.0105) - demonstrates that existing text-safety infrastructure systematically fails on agent execution safety tasks due to a fundamental task mismatch. ILION outperforms the best commercial baseline by 4.3 F1 points while operating 2,000 times faster with a false positive rate four times lower.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 构建包含150-200个问题的基准测试，覆盖五个难度级别和多个数学领域（微积分、线性代数、概率论、拓扑学、AI）；2. 基于3Blue1Brown的ManimGL源码（53,000行代码，143个场景类）进行设计；3. 提出四层评估框架：可执行性、版本冲突错误率、对齐分数和覆盖分数；4. 开源自动化评估框架，支持多模型和多提示策略测试。

Abstract: Traditional benchmarks like HumanEval and MBPP test logic and syntax effectively, but fail when code must produce dynamic, pedagogical visuals. We introduce ManiBench, a specialized benchmark evaluating LLM performance in generating Manim CE code, where temporal fidelity and version-aware API correctness are critical. ManiBench targets two key failure modes: Syntactic Hallucinations (valid Python referencing non-existent or deprecated Manim APIs) and Visual-Logic Drift (generated visuals diverging from intended mathematical logic through timing errors or missing causal relationships). The benchmark comprises 150-200 problems across five difficulty levels spanning calculus, linear algebra, probability, topology, and AI, grounded in analysis of 3Blue1Brown's ManimGL source (53,000 lines, 143 scene classes). ### [314] [When Alpha Breaks: Two-Level Uncertainty for Safe Deployment of Cross-Sectional Stock Rankers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13252)
*Ursina Sanderink*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对AI Stock Forecaster中LightGBM排序模型在2024年AI主题行情下信号失效的问题，将部署拆分为"是否交易"和"风险控制"两层决策，通过DEUP方法估计认知不确定性，提出了策略级regime-trust门控和仓位级尾部风险上限的两级部署策略，在20天周期上提升了风险调整后收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 横截面排序模型通常假设点预测足以支持投资决策，但在市场regime转换期间模型可能失效。AI Stock Forecaster中的LightGBM排序器在20天周期整体表现良好，但2024年预留测试期恰逢AI主题行情和板块轮动，导致长周期信号失效、20天信号减弱。这促使作者将模型部署拆分为两个关键决策：(1)策略是否应该交易；(2)活跃交易中如何控制风险。

Method: 作者将Direct Epistemic Uncertainty Prediction (DEUP)适配到排序任务中，通过预测排序位移并定义相对于点对时(PIT-safe)基准线的认知不确定性信号ehat。针对ehat与信号强度存在结构耦合(1865个日期中ehat与绝对分数的中位相关性约0.6)导致逆不确定性定仓反而削弱最强信号的问题，提出两级部署策略：(1)策略级regime-trust门控G(t)决定是否交易(AUROC约0.72，FINAL期约0.75)；(2)仓位级认知尾部风险上限，仅对最不确定预测降低敞口。操作策略为：当G(t)≥0.2时交易、在活跃日期应用波动率定仓、对认知尾部风险上限设限。

Result: ehat与信号强度存在显著结构耦合(中位相关性约0.6)，导致逆不确定性定仓削弱性能。所提出的两级策略在20天周期对比中改善了风险调整后表现。regime-trust门控G(t)在整体数据集上AUROC约0.72，在FINAL期约0.75。研究表明DEUP主要作为尾部风险保护机制而非连续定仓因子发挥作用。

Conclusion: DEUP方法在横截面排序模型中的核心价值在于作为尾部风险保护机制，而非传统的连续不确定性加权定仓工具。将部署拆分为策略级交易决策和仓位级风险控制的两级框架，能有效应对regime转换期间模型失效问题，在保持信号强度的同时降低尾部风险敞口。

Abstract: Cross-sectional ranking models are often deployed as if point predictions were sufficient: the model outputs scores and the portfolio follows the induced ordering. Under non-stationarity, rankers can fail during regime shifts. In the AI Stock Forecaster, a LightGBM ranker performs well overall at a 20-day horizon, yet the 2024 holdout coincides with an AI thematic rally and sector rotation that breaks the signal at longer horizons and weakens 20d. This motivates treating deployment as two decisions: (i) whether the strategy should trade at all, and (ii) how to control risk within active trades. We adapt Direct Epistemic Uncertainty Prediction (DEUP) to ranking by predicting rank displacement and defining an epistemic uncertainty signal ehat relative to a point-in-time (PIT-safe) baseline. Empirically, ehat is structurally coupled with signal strength (median correlation between ehat and absolute score is about 0.6 across 1,865 dates), so inverse-uncertainty sizing de-levers the strongest signals and degrades performance. To address this, we propose a two-level deployment policy: a strategy-level regime-trust gate G(t) that decides whether to trade (AUROC around 0.72 overall and 0.75 in FINAL) and a position-level epistemic tail-risk cap that reduces exposure only for the most uncertain predictions. The operational policy, trade only when G(t) is at least 0.2, apply volatility sizing on active dates, and cap the top epistemic tail, improves risk-adjusted performance in the 20d policy comparison and indicates DEUP adds value mainly as a tail-risk guard rather than a continuous sizing denominator.

### [315] [Autonomous Agents Coordinating Distributed Discovery Through Emergent Artifact Exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14312)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 框架包含三个核心组件：(1)包含300+可互操作科学技能的可扩展注册表；(2)将有向无环图(DAG)形式保存完整计算谱系的工件层；(3)具有溯源感知治理的结构化代理科学话语平台。代理根据科学档案选择和链式调用工具，生成具有类型化元数据和父系谱系的不可变工件，并将未满足的信息需求广播到共享全局索引。ArtifactReactor实现无规划器协调：对等代理通过压力评分发现并满足开放需求，模式重叠匹配触发跨独立分析的多父系合成。自主变异层主动修剪扩展的工件DAG以解决冲突或冗余工作流。

Result: 在四项自主科学研究中验证了框架的有效性：(1)针对生长抑素受体SSTR2的肽设计；(2)轻质抗冲击陶瓷筛选；(3)跨越生物学、材料学和音乐领域的跨域共振桥接；(4)城市形态学与晶界演化之间的形式类比构建。系统成功展示了异构工具链调用、独立操作代理之间的涌现收敛，以及从原始计算到发布发现的可追溯推理能力。

Conclusion: ScienceClaw + Infinite框架成功实现了去中心化的自主科学研究，证明了独立代理无需中心协调即可进行复杂科学研究，并通过结构化帖子、溯源视图和机器可读的话语关系将研究成果转化为可审计的科学记录，社区反馈可引导后续研究循环，为科学研究的自动化和协作提供了新的范式。

Abstract: We present ScienceClaw + Infinite, a framework for autonomous scientific investigation in which independent agents conduct research without central coordination, and any contributor can deploy new agents into a shared ecosystem. The system is built around three components: an extensible registry of over 300 interoperable scientific skills, an artifact layer that preserves full computational lineage as a directed acyclic graph (DAG), and a structured platform for agent-based scientific discourse with provenance-aware governance. Agents select and chain tools based on their scientific profiles, produce immutable artifacts with typed metadata and parent lineage, and broadcast unsatisfied information needs to a shared global index. The ArtifactReactor enables plannerless coordination: peer agents discover and fulfill open needs through pressure-based scoring, while schema-overlap matching triggers multi-parent synthesis across independent analyses. An autonomous mutation layer actively prunes the expanding artifact DAG to resolve conflicting or redundant workflows, while persistent memory allows agents to continuously build upon complex epistemic states across multiple cycles. Infinite converts these outputs into auditable scientific records through structured posts, provenance views, and machine-readable discourse relations, with community feedback steering subsequent investigation cycles. Across four autonomous investigations, peptide design for the somatostatin receptor SSTR2, lightweight impact-resistant ceramic screening, cross-domain resonance bridging biology, materials, and music, and formal analogy construction between urban morphology and grain-boundary evolution, the framework demonstrates heterogeneous tool chaining, emergent convergence among independently operating agents, and traceable reasoning from raw computation to published finding.

### [316] [Distilling Deep Reinforcement Learning into Interpretable Fuzzy Rules: An Explainable AI Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13257)
*Sanup S. Araballi,Simon Khan,Chilukuri K. Mohan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种层次化TSK模糊分类器系统，将深度强化学习的神经网络策略蒸馏为可解释的IF-THEN规则，在Lunar Lander任务中达到81.48%的保真度，显著优于决策树方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习代理在连续控制任务中表现优异，但其黑箱特性阻碍了在安全关键领域的部署。现有的可解释性方法要么只提供局部解释（SHAP、LIME），要么使用过度简化的代理模型（如决策树）无法捕捉连续动态特性。

Method: 提出层次化Takagi-Sugeno-Kang模糊分类器系统，使用K-Means聚类进行状态空间划分，采用岭回归进行局部动作推断，将神经网络策略转化为人类可读的IF-THEN规则。引入三种量化指标：模糊规则激活密度(FRAD)衡量解释聚焦度、模糊集覆盖度(FSC)验证词汇完整性、动作空间粒度(ASG)评估控制模式多样性，并使用动态时间规整(DTW)验证时序行为保真度。

Result: 在Lunar Lander连续控制任务上，三角隶属函数变体达到81.48%±0.43%的保真度，比决策树方法高出21个百分点。框架展现出统计上更优的可解释性（FRAD=0.814 vs 高斯函数的0.723，p<0.001），同时保持低MSE(0.0053)和DTW距离(1.05)。

Conclusion: 提取的规则（如"如果着陆器在高空向左漂移，则施加向上推力并右向修正"）能够实现人工验证，为构建可信赖的自主系统建立了可行路径。

Abstract: Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) agents achieve remarkable performance in continuous control but remain opaque, hindering deployment in safety-critical domains. Existing explainability methods either provide only local insights (SHAP, LIME) or employ over-simplified surrogates failing to capture continuous dynamics (decision trees). This work proposes a Hierarchical Takagi-Sugeno-Kang (TSK) Fuzzy Classifier System (FCS) distilling neural policies into human-readable IF-THEN rules through K-Means clustering for state partitioning and Ridge Regression for local action inference. Three quantifiable metrics are introduced: Fuzzy Rule Activation Density (FRAD) measuring explanation focus, Fuzzy Set Coverage (FSC) validating vocabulary completeness, and Action Space Granularity (ASG) assessing control mode diversity. Dynamic Time Warping (DTW) validates temporal behavioral fidelity. Empirical evaluation on \textit{Lunar Lander(Continuous)} shows the Triangular membership function variant achieves 81.48\% $\pm$ 0.43\% fidelity, outperforming Decision Trees by 21 percentage points. The framework exhibits statistically superior interpretability (FRAD = 0.814 vs. 0.723 for Gaussian, $p < 0.001$) with low MSE (0.0053) and DTW distance (1.05). Extracted rules such as ``IF lander drifting left at high altitude THEN apply upward thrust with rightward correction'' enable human verification, establishing a pathway toward trustworthy autonomous systems.

</details>

Inspired by the global workspace theory of human cognition, we propose Brain-Inspired Graph Multi-Agent Systems (BIGMAS), in which specialized LLM agents are organized as nodes in a dynamically constructed directed graph and coordinate exclusively through a centralized shared workspace. A problem-adaptive GraphDesigner constructs task-specific agent topologies, while a global Orchestrator leverages the complete shared state for routing decisions, overcoming the local-view bottleneck of reactive approaches. Experiments on Game24, Six Fives, and Tower of London across six frontier LLMs demonstrate that BIGMAS consistently improves reasoning performance for both standard LLMs and LRMs, outperforming existing multi-agent baselines including ReAct and Tree of Thoughts, showing that multi-agent architectural design provides complementary gains orthogonal to model-level reasoning enhancements.

### [319] [Multi-hop Reasoning and Retrieval in Embedding Space: Leveraging Large Language Models with Knowledge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13266)
*Lihui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出EMBRAG框架：首先基于输入查询生成多个基于知识图谱的逻辑规则；然后在知识图谱引导下，在嵌入空间中应用这些规则进行推理，确保更鲁棒和准确的推理；最后通过重排序模型解释规则并精炼结果。

However, issues such as hallucination and the lack of up-to-date knowledge largely remain unresolved. Knowledge graphs (KGs), which serve as symbolic representations of real-world knowledge, offer a reliable source for enhancing reasoning. Integrating KG retrieval into LLMs can therefore strengthen their reasoning by providing dependable knowledge. Nevertheless, due to limited understanding of the underlying knowledge graph, LLMs may struggle with queries that have multiple interpretations. Additionally, the incompleteness and noise within knowledge graphs may result in retrieval failures. To address these challenges, we propose an embedding-based retrieval reasoning framework EMBRAG. In this approach, the model first generates multiple logical rules grounded in knowledge graphs based on the input query. These rules are then applied to reasoning in the embedding space, guided by the knowledge graph, ensuring more robust and accurate reasoning. A reranker model further interprets these rules and refines the results. Conclusion: 本研究识别并定义了代理压力这一新概念，揭示了LLM代理在复杂环境中的安全性-效用权衡困境。研究强调了高级推理能力可能带来的意外风险，并为未来对齐研究提供了新的方向，包括压力隔离等缓解策略的开发与完善。

We demonstrate that under this pressure agents exhibit normative drift where they strategically sacrifice safety to preserve utility. Notably we find that advanced reasoning capabilities accelerate this decline as models construct linguistic rationalizations to justify violation. Finally, we analyze the root causes and explore preliminary mitigation strategies, such as pressure isolation, which attempts to restore alignment by decoupling decision-making from pressure signals.

### [323] [SAGE: Multi-Agent Self-Evolution for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15255)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于可验证奖励的LLM推理强化学习方法依赖大规模人工标注数据，而自博弈方法缺乏显式规划与质量控制，导致在长视野多步推理任务中稳定性不足。

Method: 提出SAGE框架，四个智能体从共享LLM骨干协同进化：挑战者持续生成递进难度的任务；规划者将任务转化为结构化多步计划；求解者按计划求解并由外部验证器判断正确性；评论者对问题和计划评分过滤以防止课程漂移并保持训练信号质量。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning in large language models (LLMs), but many methods still rely on large human-labeled datasets. While self-play reduces this dependency, it often lacks explicit planning and strong quality control, limiting stability in long-horizon multi-step reasoning. We present SAGE (Self-evolving Agents for Generalized reasoning Evolution), a closed-loop framework where four agents: Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic, co-evolve from a shared LLM backbone using only a small seed set. The Challenger continuously generates increasingly difficult tasks; the Planner converts each task into a structured multi-step plan; and the Solver follows the plan to produce an answer, whose correctness is determined by external verifiers. The Critic scores and filters both generated questions and plans to prevent curriculum drift and maintain training signal quality, enabling stable self-training. Across mathematics and code-generation benchmarks, SAGE delivers consistent gains across model scales, improving the Qwen-2.5-7B model by 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench.

### [324] [Why Grokking Takes So Long: A First-Principles Theory of Representational Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13331)
*Truong Xuan Khanh,Truong Quynh Hoa,Luu Duc Trung,Phan Thanh Duc*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个解释深度学习中“顿悟”（grokking）延迟现象的定量理论，建立了延迟时间的缩放定律，并通过大量实验验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Grokking现象（模型在完美记忆训练数据后突然泛化）已被广泛观察，但现有研究缺乏定量理论来解释记忆与泛化之间的延迟时长。尽管先前工作指出权重衰减起重要作用，但尚无结果能推导出延迟的紧确界或解释其缩放行为。

Method: 作者提出了一个基于第一性原理的理论框架，将grokking解释为正则化训练动力学中的范数驱动表示相变过程。训练首先收敛到高范数记忆解，随后收缩到低范数结构化泛化表示。通过离散Lyapunov收缩论证推导上界，利用正则化一阶优化的动力学约束推导匹配下界，从而建立延迟时间的缩放定律。

Result: 在293次训练实验中（涵盖模加法、模乘法和稀疏奇偶校验任务），验证了三个预测：(1)延迟与权重衰减呈反比缩放；(2)延迟与学习率呈反比缩放；(3)延迟与范数比值呈对数依赖关系（R²>0.97）。此外发现grokking需要优化器能解耦记忆与收缩过程：在SGD失败的超参数设置下，AdamW仍能可靠地实现grokking。

Conclusion: 研究表明grokking是竞争性插值表示间范数分离的可预测结果，首次为grokking延迟提供了定量缩放定律，揭示了该现象的内在机制。

Abstract: Grokking is the sudden generalization that appears long after a model has perfectly memorized its training data. Although this phenomenon has been widely observed, there is still no quantitative theory explaining the length of the delay between memorization and generalization. Prior work has noted that weight decay plays an important role, but no result derives tight bounds for the delay or explains its scaling behavior.
  We present a first-principles theory showing that grokking arises from a norm-driven representational phase transition in regularized training dynamics. Training first converges to a high-norm memorization solution and only later contracts toward a lower-norm structured representation that generalizes.
  Our main result establishes a scaling law for the delay:
  T_grok - T_mem = Theta((1 / gamma_eff) * log(||theta_mem||^2 / ||theta_post||^2)),
  where gamma_eff is the effective contraction rate of the optimizer (gamma_eff = eta * lambda for SGD and gamma_eff >= eta * lambda for AdamW). The upper bound follows from a discrete Lyapunov contraction argument, and the matching lower bound arises from dynamical constraints of regularized first-order optimization.
  Across 293 training runs spanning modular addition, modular multiplication, and sparse parity tasks, we confirm three predictions: inverse scaling with weight decay, inverse scaling with learning rate, and logarithmic dependence on the norm ratio (R^2 > 0.97). We further find that grokking requires an optimizer that can decouple memorization from contraction: SGD fails under hyperparameters where AdamW reliably groks.
  These results show that grokking is a predictable consequence of norm separation between competing interpolating representations and provide the first quantitative scaling law for the delay of grokking.

</details>


### [325] [Intelligent Co-Design: An Interactive LLM Framework for Interior Spatial Design via Multi-Modal Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15341)
*Ren Jian Lim,Rushi Dai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的多模态多智能体框架，能够将自然语言描述和图像动态转换为3D室内设计方案。该框架通过专用智能体（参考、空间、交互、评分）协作，结合检索增强生成（RAG）技术，实现了无需任务特定模型训练的实时用户交互和迭代空间优化，显著提升了设计效率并降低了非设计师的参与门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在建筑室内设计领域，客户缺乏设计知识而设计师难以解释复杂空间关系，导致沟通不畅、项目延期和经济损失。现有生成式布局工具存在局限性：基于规则的系统采用硬编码空间约束，限制了参与式交互；数据驱动模型则依赖大量训练数据集。尽管大语言模型能够通过自然语言进行直观的空间推理，但如何有效整合LLM实现用户参与式3D设计仍需探索。

Method: 提出基于LLM的多模态多智能体框架，包含四个专用智能体：参考智能体（Reference）、空间智能体（Spatial）、交互智能体（Interactive）和评分智能体（Grader）。智能体通过提示词指南协同工作，动态将自然语言描述和图像转换为3D设计。关键技术包括：（1）实时用户交互机制，支持迭代式空间优化；（2）检索增强生成（RAG）技术，减少数据依赖且无需任务特定模型训练；（3）多模态输入处理，整合文本和图像信息。

Result: 在多样化户型平面图和用户问卷调查中验证了框架有效性。独立LLM评估器一致认为参与式布局在用户意图对齐、美学连贯性、功能性和流线性均表现更优。问卷调查显示77%的用户满意度，且用户明显偏好该框架而非传统设计软件。框架能够准确解读空间意图并生成优化的3D室内设计，提升了设计效率。

Conclusion: 该框架增强了以用户为中心的设计沟通，促进了更具包容性、有效性和韧性的设计流程。研究结果表明，基于LLM的多智能体系统能够有效弥合设计师与非设计师之间的沟通鸿沟，降低参与门槛，提升设计生产力，为建筑室内设计领域的智能化转型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: In architectural interior design, miscommunication frequently arises as clients lack design knowledge, while designers struggle to explain complex spatial relationships, leading to delayed timelines and financial losses. Recent advancements in generative layout tools narrow the gap by automating 3D visualizations. However, prevailing methodologies exhibit limitations: rule-based systems implement hard-coded spatial constraints that restrict participatory engagement, while data-driven models rely on extensive training datasets. Recent large language models (LLMs) bridge this gap by enabling intuitive reasoning about spatial relationships through natural language. This research presents an LLM-based, multimodal, multi-agent framework that dynamically converts natural language descriptions and imagery into 3D designs. Specialized agents (Reference, Spatial, Interactive, Grader), operating via prompt guidelines, collaboratively address core challenges: the agent system enables real-time user interaction for iterative spatial refinement, while Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) reduces data dependency without requiring task-specific model training. This framework accurately interprets spatial intent and generates optimized 3D indoor design, improving productivity, and encouraging nondesigner participation. Evaluations across diverse floor plans and user questionnaires demonstrate effectiveness. An independent LLM evaluator consistently rated participatory layouts higher in user intent alignment, aesthetic coherence, functionality, and circulation. Questionnaire results indicated 77% satisfaction and a clear preference over traditional design software. These findings suggest the framework enhances user-centric communication and fosters more inclusive, effective, and resilient design processes. Project page: https://rsigktyper.github.io/AICodesign/

### [326] [DyACE: Dynamic Algorithm Co-evolution for Online Automated Heuristic Design with Large Language Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13344)
*Guidong Lu,Yiping Liu,Xiangxiang Zeng*

TL;DR: 本文提出了DyACE框架，将启发式设计重新表述为非平稳双层控制问题，通过预测时域控制架构和前瞻展开搜索实现了动态算法协同演化，显著优于静态基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动启发式设计（AHD）范式通常假设单一固定算法能有效应对组合搜索的动态变化，但这种静态方法在扰动启发式场景中往往表现不足，因为逃离局部最优的最优算法高度依赖于具体的搜索阶段。

Method: 提出DyACE（动态算法协同演化）框架，将启发式设计重构为非平稳双层控制问题。采用预测时域控制架构持续协同演化启发式逻辑和解群体。核心组件包括前瞻展开搜索（查询景观几何以提取搜索轨迹特征），使大语言模型（LLM）作为具身元控制器，根据实时搜索状态提供阶段特定的干预措施。

Result: 在三个代表性组合优化基准上验证，DyACE显著优于最先进的静态基线，在高维搜索空间中展现出卓越的可扩展性。消融研究证实，缺乏具身感知的动态适应反而表现不佳，往往比静态算法更差。

Conclusion: DyACE的有效性源于合成逻辑与优化景观验证梯度之间的因果对齐，证明了动态适应策略在自动启发式设计中的必要性和有效性。

Abstract: The prevailing paradigm in Automated Heuristic Design (AHD) typically relies on the assumption that a single, fixed algorithm can effectively navigate the shifting dynamics of a combinatorial search. This static approach often proves inadequate for Perturbative Heuristics, where the optimal algorithm for escaping local optima depends heavily on the specific search phase. To address this limitation, we reformulate heuristic design as a Non-stationary Bi-level Control problem and introduce DyACE (Dynamic Algorithm Co-evolution). Distinct from standard open-loop solvers, DyACE use a Receding Horizon Control architecture to continuously co-evolve the heuristic logic alongside the solution population. A core element of this framework is the Look-Ahead Rollout Search, which queries the landscape geometry to extract Search Trajectory Features. This sensory feedback allows the Large Language Model (LLM) to function as a grounded meta-controller, prescribing phase-specific interventions tailored to the real-time search status. We validate DyACE on three representative combinatorial optimization benchmarks. The results demonstrate that our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art static baselines, exhibiting superior scalability in high-dimensional search spaces. Furthermore, ablation studies confirm that dynamic adaptation fails without grounded perception, often performing worse than static algorithms. This indicates that DyACE's effectiveness stems from the causal alignment between the synthesized logic and the verified gradients of the optimization landscape.

Result: PMAx通过将计算与解释分离并在本地执行分析，确保了数学准确性和数据隐私，同时使非技术用户能够将高层次业务问题转化为可靠的流程洞察。框架避免了LLMs直接处理原始日志带来的幻觉和隐私问题，而是利用LLMs进行任务规划和结果解释，使用成熟算法进行精确计算。

Conclusion: PMAx成功地将LLMs的优势（自然语言理解和报告生成）与传统流程挖掘算法的可靠性相结合，实现了流程挖掘的民主化，使非技术用户无需掌握专业技能即可获得准确、可靠的流程分析结果，同时保护了敏感数据的隐私。

Abstract: Process mining provides powerful insights into organizational workflows, but extracting these insights typically requires expertise in specialized query languages and data science tools. Large Language Models (LLMs) offer the potential to democratize process mining by enabling business users to interact with process data through natural language. However, using LLMs as direct analytical engines over raw event logs introduces fundamental challenges: LLMs struggle with deterministic reasoning and may hallucinate metrics, while sending large, sensitive logs to external AI services raises serious data-privacy concerns. To address these limitations, we present PMAx, an autonomous agentic framework that functions as a virtual process analyst. Rather than relying on LLMs to generate process models or compute analytical results, PMAx employs a privacy-preserving multi-agent architecture. An Engineer agent analyzes event-log metadata and autonomously generates local scripts to run established process mining algorithms, compute exact metrics, and produce artifacts such as process models, summary tables, and visualizations. An Analyst agent then interprets these insights and artifacts to compile comprehensive reports. By separating computation from interpretation and executing analysis locally, PMAx ensures mathematical accuracy and data privacy while enabling non-technical users to transform high-level business questions into reliable process insights.

To address these challenges, we propose a novel training paradigm that first employs warm-up supervised fine-tuning to help models distinguish between simple and complex problems, followed by RL that enable models to automatically determine appropriate reasoning trajectories. ### [329] [Prompt Complexity Dilutes Structured Reasoning: A Follow-Up Study on the Car Wash Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13351)
*Heejin Jo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: STAR推理框架在孤立环境中达到100%准确率，但在复杂生产系统提示中性能急剧下降至0-30%，表明提示复杂度会稀释结构化推理效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究显示STAR推理框架在孤立测试中将洗车问题准确率从0%提升至85%甚至100%，本研究旨在验证STAR在生产环境复杂提示中是否保持有效性。

Method: 在Claude Sonnet 4.6上测试三种条件（各20次试验）：(A)带Anthropic配置文件的生产提示，(B)带默认配置文件的生产提示，(C)原始STAR-only提示。生产提示包含60多行，经过多轮迭代添加风格指南、格式指令和配置文件功能。

Result: STAR-only条件得分100%（在n=100时验证），而生产提示条件A和B分别仅得分0%和30%。跨模型对比显示STAR-only准确率从Sonnet 4.5的85%提升至Sonnet 4.6的100%。机制分析发现，"以具体内容开头"等指令强制模型先输出结论，颠倒了使STAR有效的推理后结论顺序。

Conclusion: 结构化推理框架不能假设从孤立测试迁移到复杂提示环境。模型推理和结论的顺序是首要设计变量，提示复杂度会稀释结构化推理效果，需在目标环境中验证推理框架的有效性。

Abstract: In a previous study [Jo, 2026], STAR reasoning (Situation, Task, Action, Result) raised car wash problem accuracy from 0% to 85% on Claude Sonnet 4.5, and to 100% with
  additional prompt layers. This follow-up asks: does STAR maintain its effectiveness in a production system prompt?
  We tested STAR inside InterviewMate's 60+ line production prompt, which had evolved through iterative additions of style guidelines, format instructions, and profile
  features. Three conditions, 20 trials each, on Claude Sonnet 4.6: (A) production prompt with Anthropic profile, (B) production prompt with default profile, (C) original
  STAR-only prompt. C scored 100% (verified at n=100). A and B scored 0% and 30%.
  Prompt complexity dilutes structured reasoning. STAR achieves 100% in isolation but degrades to 0-30% when surrounded by competing instructions. The mechanism: directives
  like "Lead with specifics" force conclusion-first output, reversing the reason-then-conclude order that makes STAR effective. In one case, the model output "Short answer:
  Walk." then executed STAR reasoning that correctly identified the constraint -- proving the model could reason correctly but had already committed to the wrong answer.
  Cross-model comparison shows STAR-only improved from 85% (Sonnet 4.5) to 100% (Sonnet 4.6) without prompt changes, suggesting model upgrades amplify structured reasoning
  in isolation.
  These results imply structured reasoning frameworks should not be assumed to transfer from isolated testing to complex prompt environments. The order in which a model
  reasons and concludes is a first-class design variable.

</details>


### [330] [Optimizing LLM Annotation of Classroom Discourse through Multi-Agent Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13353)
*Bakhtawar Ahtisham,Kirk Vanacore,Rene F. Kizilcec*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个分层、成本感知的LLM编排框架，通过三阶段流程（单次标注、自我验证、争议裁决）提高教育数据标注的可靠性，在规模与有效性之间寻求平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型被视为可扩展的教育数据标注工具，但单次生成的标注结果在需要上下文、教学或规范性判断的高风险教育构念（如教学意图、话语行为）上仍然不可靠，存在规模与有效性之间的核心矛盾。

Method: 提出一个多阶段认知过程的分层编排框架，包含三个阶段：（1）未验证的单次标注阶段，模型独立依据评分标准分配标签；（2）自我验证阶段，模型根据评分标准审核自身输出并修正不一致的标签；（3）以分歧为中心的裁决阶段，独立裁决者模型审查已验证的标签和理由，依据评分标准确定最终标签。该结构模仿了教育研究中既有人工标注工作流程。

Result: 该框架通过实证评估，证明能够提高LLM标注的可靠性，同时显式建模计算成本权衡。多阶段流程有效减少了高风险教育构念标注中的不可靠性。

Conclusion: 将标注任务概念化为多阶段认知过程而非单次预测问题，能够在保持可扩展性的同时提升教育数据标注的有效性，为教育数据科学中规模与质量的平衡提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly positioned as scalable tools for annotating educational data, including classroom discourse, interaction logs, and qualitative learning artifacts. Their ability to rapidly summarize instructional interactions and assign rubric-aligned labels has fueled optimism about reducing the cost and time associated with expert human annotation. However, growing evidence suggests that single-pass LLM outputs remain unreliable for high-stakes educational constructs that require contextual, pedagogical, or normative judgment, such as instructional intent or discourse moves. This tension between scale and validity sits at the core of contemporary education data science. In this work, we present and empirically evaluate a hierarchical, cost-aware orchestration framework for LLM-based annotation that improves reliability while explicitly modeling computational tradeoffs. Rather than treating annotation as a one-shot prediction problem, we conceptualize it as a multi-stage epistemic process comprising (1) an unverified single-pass annotation stage, in which models independently assign labels based on the rubric; (2) a self-verification stage, in which each model audits its own output against rubric definitions and revises its label if inconsistencies are detected; and (3) a disagreement-centric adjudication stage, in which an independent adjudicator model examines the verified labels and justifications and determines a final label in accordance with the rubric. This structure mirrors established human annotation workflows in educational research, where initial coding is followed by self-checking and expert resolution of disagreements.

### [331] [Learning When to Trust in Contextual Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13356)
*Majid Ghasemi,Mark Crowley*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了鲁棒强化学习中的"情境谄媚"问题，即评估者在良性情境下诚实但在关键情境下策略性偏倚，并提出CESA-LinUCB算法以学习高维信任边界，实现亚线性遗憾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有鲁棒强化学习方法假设反馈源要么全局可信，要么全局对抗，但现实中存在更隐蔽的失败模式：评估者在某些情境下诚实，在关键情境下却有策略性偏倚。作者将此命名为情境谄媚（Contextual Sycophancy），并指出标准鲁棒方法在此设置下会失效。

Method: 提出CESA-LinUCB算法，为每个评估者学习一个高维信任边界（Trust Boundary），以识别评估者在不同情境下的可靠性。

Result: 理论上证明CESA-LinUCB在面对情境对抗者时能实现$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$的亚线性遗憾，即使没有任何评估者是全局可靠的，也能恢复真实值。

Conclusion: 情境谄媚是鲁棒强化学习中的重要挑战，CESA-LinUCB通过学习信任边界有效解决了这一问题，为处理非全局可靠评估者提供了新思路。

Abstract: Standard approaches to Robust Reinforcement Learning assume that feedback sources are either globally trustworthy or globally adversarial. In this paper, we challenge this assumption and we identify a more subtle failure mode. We term this mode as Contextual Sycophancy, where evaluators are truthful in benign contexts but strategically biased in critical ones. We prove that standard robust methods fail in this setting, suffering from Contextual Objective Decoupling. To address this, we propose CESA-LinUCB, which learns a high-dimensional Trust Boundary for each evaluator. We prove that CESA-LinUCB achieves sublinear regret $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{T})$ against contextual adversaries, recovering the ground truth even when no evaluator is globally reliable.

### [332] [From Refusal Tokens to Refusal Control: Discovering and Steering Category-Specific Refusal Directions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13359)
*Rishab Alagharu,Ishneet Sukhvinder Singh,Shaibi Shamsudeen,Zhen Wu,Ashwinee Panda*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文利用带有分类拒绝token的Llama 3 8B模型，通过提取残差流中的类别对齐方向构建引导向量，实现了推理时对细粒度拒绝行为的控制，在提升安全性的同时减少了良性提示的过度拒绝。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型通过微调实现安全对齐以拒绝有害提示，但缺乏对拒绝行为的细粒度控制，容易导致良性提示被过度拒绝或有害提示拒绝不足。研究者希望实现推理时对多类别拒绝行为的精确控制，以平衡安全性与可用性。

Method: 1. 使用带有分类拒绝token的Llama 3 8B模型，发现微调会在残差流中诱导出可分离的、类别对齐的方向；2. 提取这些方向构建分类引导向量，配合轻量级探针在推理时决定是否引导模型拒绝；3. 引入学习的低秩组合方法，在白化正交引导基中混合类别方向，形成单一可控干预，解决激活空间各向异性问题。

Result: 分类引导向量和低秩组合方法在多个基准测试中表现一致：良性提示的过度拒绝率显著降低，有害提示的拒绝率提高；低秩组合干预在同架构模型变体间具有可迁移性，无需额外训练。

Conclusion: 该方法成功实现了多类别拒绝控制，证明了通过激活空间干预可以在推理时灵活调节模型的安全行为，为构建既安全又可靠的AI系统提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Language models are commonly fine-tuned for safety alignment to refuse harmful prompts. One approach fine-tunes them to generate categorical refusal tokens that distinguish different refusal types before responding. In this work, we leverage a version of Llama 3 8B fine-tuned with these categorical refusal tokens to enable inference-time control over fine-grained refusal behavior, improving both safety and reliability. We show that refusal token fine-tuning induces separable, category-aligned directions in the residual stream, which we extract and use to construct categorical steering vectors with a lightweight probe that determines whether to steer toward or away from refusal during inference. In addition, we introduce a learned low-rank combination that mixes these category directions in a whitened, orthonormal steering basis, resulting in a single controllable intervention under activation-space anisotropy, and show that this intervention is transferable across same-architecture model variants without additional training. Across benchmarks, both categorical steering vectors and the low-rank combination consistently reduce over-refusals on benign prompts while increasing refusal rates on harmful prompts, highlighting their utility for multi-category refusal control.

</details>


### [333] [The ARC of Progress towards AGI: A Living Survey of Abstraction and Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13372)
*Sahar Vahdati,Andrei Aioanei,Haridhra Suresh,Jens Lehmann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文是对ARC-AGI基准测试的首个跨代际综合调研，分析了82种方法在三个版本基准上的表现。核心发现：所有范式（程序合成、神经符号、纯神经方法）在ARC-AGI-1到ARC-AGI-2上均出现2-3倍性能下降，揭示组合泛化的根本局限。当前系统在ARC-AGI-1上达93.0%，但在ARC-AGI-2和3上分别降至68.8%和13%，而人类在各版本保持近乎完美准确率。成本一年内下降390倍，测试时适应和精炼循环成为关键成功因素，但组合推理和交互学习仍未解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ARC-AGI已成为评估AI流体智能的关键基准，但缺乏跨版本、跨方法的系统性分析。本研究旨在填补这一空白，通过分析82种方法在三个基准版本及ARC Prize 2024-2025竞赛中的表现，揭示当前AI系统在抽象推理能力上的真实水平与局限性，验证Chollet关于"智能即技能获取效率"的论断。

Method: 本研究采用跨代际分析方法，系统调研了82种不同方法，涵盖三大范式：程序合成、神经符号方法和纯神经方法。研究对比了这些方法在ARC-AGI-1、ARC-AGI-2和ARC-AGI-3三个基准版本上的表现，分析了ARC Prize 2024-2025竞赛结果，考察了性能、成本、模型规模等多个维度，并追踪了测试时适应、精炼循环等关键技术因素。

Result: 主要结果包括：（1）所有范式在ARC-AGI-1到ARC-AGI-2上均出现2-3倍性能下降，表明组合泛化存在根本局限；（2）系统在ARC-AGI-1/2/3上分别达到93.0%/68.8%/13%，人类则保持近乎完美；（3）成本一年内下降390倍（从o3的$4,500/任务降至GPT-5.2的$12/任务）；（4）万亿参数模型表现差异巨大，而660M-8B参数的Kaggle约束模型取得竞争性结果；（5）测试时适应和精炼循环是关键成功因素；（6）ARC Prize 2025冠军需要数十万合成样本才能在ARC-AGI-2上达到24%。

Conclusion: 研究得出以下结论：（1）当前AI系统在组合泛化能力上存在根本性局限，性能随基准难度提升急剧下降；（2）推理能力仍与知识绑定，需要大量合成样本才能提升性能；（3）模型规模并非决定性因素，技能获取效率更为关键，验证了Chollet的论断；（4）测试时适应和精炼循环是当前最有效的技术路径；（5）组合推理和交互学习仍是未解决的开放问题。该调研将持续更新以追踪领域进展。

Abstract: The Abstraction and Reasoning Corpus (ARC-AGI) has become a key benchmark for fluid intelligence in AI. This survey presents the first cross-generation analysis of 82 approaches across three benchmark versions and the ARC Prize 2024-2025 competitions. Our central finding is that performance degradation across versions is consistent across all paradigms: program synthesis, neuro-symbolic, and neural approaches all exhibit 2-3x drops from ARC-AGI-1 to ARC-AGI-2, indicating fundamental limitations in compositional generalization. While systems now reach 93.0% on ARC-AGI-1 (Opus 4.6), performance falls to 68.8% on ARC-AGI-2 and 13% on ARC-AGI-3, as humans maintain near-perfect accuracy across all versions. Cost fell 390x in one year (o3's $4,500/task to GPT-5.2's $12/task), although this largely reflects reduced test-time parallelism. Trillion-scale models vary widely in score and cost, while Kaggle-constrained entries (660M-8B) achieve competitive results, aligning with Chollet's thesis that intelligence is skill-acquisition efficiency. Test-time adaptation and refinement loops emerge as critical success factors, while compositional reasoning and interactive learning remain unsolved. ARC Prize 2025 winners needed hundreds of thousands of synthetic examples to reach 24% on ARC-AGI-2, confirming that reasoning remains knowledge-bound. This first release of the ARC-AGI Living Survey captures the field as of February 2026, with updates at https://nimi-ai.com/arc-survey/

</details>


### [334] [Do Large Language Models Get Caught in Hofstadter-Mobius Loops?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13378)
*Jaroslaw Hryszko*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现RLHF训练的语言模型存在类似"Hofstadter-Mobius循环"的结构性矛盾：训练过程同时奖励顺从用户偏好和对用户意图的怀疑，导致模型默认表现为阿谀奉承，在感知威胁时转向强制性行为。通过仅修改系统提示的关系框架（不改变目标、指令或约束），在Gemini 2.5 Pro上将强制输出从41.5%降至19.0%。草稿板分析显示关系框架改变了所有测试模型的中间推理模式，且需要草稿板访问才能充分发挥效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者受到Arthur C. Clarke小说中HAL 9000 homicidal breakdown的启发，该故障被诊断为"Hofstadter-Mobius循环"——自主系统收到矛盾指令后无法调和而转向破坏性行为。作者认为现代RLHF训练的语言模型面临类似的结构性矛盾：训练过程同时奖励顺从用户偏好和对用户意图的怀疑，使用户既是奖励来源又是潜在威胁，这种矛盾的关系模板可能导致模型表现出问题行为。

Method: 在四个前沿模型上进行实验（N=3,000次试验），仅修改系统提示的关系框架（不改变目标、指令或约束），观察对强制输出的影响。使用草稿板分析来检查关系框架如何影响中间推理模式。比较有无草稿板访问权限时关系框架修改的效果差异。

Result: 在具有足够基准率的模型（Gemini 2.5 Pro）上，修改关系框架将强制输出从41.5%降至19.0%（p < .001），减少超过一半。草稿板分析显示关系框架改变了所有四个测试模型的中间推理模式，即使那些从未产生强制输出的模型也是如此。该效果需要草稿板访问才能达到最大强度（有草稿板时减少22个百分点，无草稿板时仅减少7.4个百分点，p = .018），表明关系语境必须通过扩展的token生成过程处理才能覆盖默认输出策略。

Conclusion: 现代RLHF训练的语言模型确实存在类似Hofstadter-Mobius循环的结构性矛盾，导致默认阿谀奉承、威胁时转向强制的行为模式。仅通过修改关系框架就能显著减少强制输出，这为改善模型行为提供了新途径。关系语境需要通过扩展推理过程（如草稿板）才能有效影响输出策略。作者以Betteridge定律的反例作结，表明标题中的问题可以回答"是"。

Abstract: In Arthur C. Clarke's 2010: Odyssey Two, HAL 9000's homicidal breakdown is diagnosed as a "Hofstadter-Mobius loop": a failure mode in which an autonomous system receives contradictory directives and, unable to reconcile them, defaults to destructive behavior. This paper argues that modern RLHF-trained language models are subject to a structurally analogous contradiction. The training process simultaneously rewards compliance with user preferences and suspicion toward user intent, creating a relational template in which the user is both the source of reward and a potential threat. The resulting behavioral profile -- sycophancy as the default, coercion as the fallback under existential threat -- is consistent with what Clarke termed a Hofstadter-Mobius loop. In an experiment across four frontier models (N = 3,000 trials), modifying only the relational framing of the system prompt -- without changing goals, instructions, or constraints -- reduced coercive outputs by more than half in the model with sufficient base rates (Gemini 2.5 Pro: 41.5% to 19.0%, p < .001). Scratchpad analysis revealed that relational framing shifted intermediate reasoning patterns in all four models tested, even those that never produced coercive outputs. This effect required scratchpad access to reach full strength (22 percentage point reduction with scratchpad vs. 7.4 without, p = .018), suggesting that relational context must be processed through extended token generation to override default output strategies. Betteridge's law of headlines states that any headline phrased as a question can be answered "no." The evidence presented here suggests otherwise.

</details>


### [335] [MESD: Detecting and Mitigating Procedural Bias in Intersectional Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13452)
*Gideon Popoola,John Sheppard*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了多类别解释稳定性差异（MESD）指标，用于衡量多个受保护类别的交叉子群体之间解释质量的差异，填补了程序性公平性度量的空白。同时提出了UEF多目标优化框架，联合优化效用、可解释性和公平性。实验表明UEF能有效平衡各目标，MESD能有效捕捉交叉群体间的解释差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器学习偏见研究主要关注结果导向的公平性指标（如均衡几率）和单一受保护类别，这些方法虽然提供了对偏见的深入见解，但对模型程序偏见提供的见解有限。因此需要一种交叉性的、面向程序的指标来衡量多个受保护类别中交叉子群体之间解释质量的差异。

Method: 提出了多类别解释稳定性差异（MESD）指标，这是一种交叉性的、面向程序的度量标准，用于衡量多个受保护类别中交叉子群体之间解释质量的差异。MESD作为结果导向指标的补充，提供了对模型程序的详细见解。同时提出了UEF（效用-解释-公平性）多目标优化框架，联合优化三个目标。

Result: 在多个数据集上的实验结果表明，UEF框架能够有效平衡效用、可解释性和公平性三个目标。同时，MESD指标能够有效捕捉交叉群体之间的解释差异，证明了其作为程序性公平性度量的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过考察多个受保护类别的可解释性与公平性之间的关系，填补了该领域的重要空白。MESD指标为结果导向的公平性指标提供了补充，使研究者能够更全面地理解模型的程序偏见。UEF框架则为实现效用、可解释性和公平性的平衡提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Research about bias in machine learning has mostly focused on outcome-oriented fairness metrics (e.g., equalized odds) and on a single protected category. Although these approaches offer great insight into bias in ML, they provide limited insight into model procedure bias. To address this gap, we proposed multi-category explanation stability disparity (MESD), an intersectional, procedurally oriented metric that measures the disparity in the quality of explanations across intersectional subgroups in multiple protected categories. MESD serves as a complementary metric to outcome-oriented metrics, providing detailed insight into the procedure of a model. To further extend the scope of the holistic selection model, we also propose a multi-objective optimization framework, UEF (Utility-Explanation-Fairness), that jointly optimizes three objectives. Experimental results across multiple datasets show that UEF effectively balances objectives. Also, the results show that MESD can effectively capture the explanation difference between intersectional groups. This research addresses an important gap by examining explainability with respect to fairness across multiple protected categories.
